<div id="page-1279206">
<h3><a name="page-1279206">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 039)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>39</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees June 11th 1855. Special Meeting'>Trustees <date when='1855-06-11'>June 11<sup>th</sup> 1855</date>. Special Meeting</span></p>
<p>A Special Meeting of the Trustees was held in<span class='line-break'> </span>accordance with previous notice, at the Office of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary, on <date when='1855-06-11'>the eleventh day of June A. D. 1855</date>. "to <span class='line-break'> </span>receive and act upon the resignation of <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a> as <span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent". _</p>
<p>Present Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Jacob-->Bigelow</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54775' title='Kuhn, George H.'>Kuhn</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>,<span class='line-break'> </span>Little and</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>.</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read &amp; approved.<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The Pres<sup>t</sup></a> stated that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> had received <s>the</s><span class='line-break'> </span>a <s>following</s> a communication from <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a>, which was <span class='line-break'> </span>then read, of which the following is a copy.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Mr Howe&apos;s Letter of resignation as Supt'><a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a>'s Letter of resignation as Sup<sup>t</sup></span></p>
<p>"Mount Auburn <date when='1855-06-05'>June 5<sup>th</sup> 1855</date>. ~<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. J. Coolidge Esq.</a> Secretary of the Proprietors of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery of Mount Auburn</p>
<p>Dear Sir,<span class='line-break'> </span>I have received an attested copy <span class='line-break'> </span>of a Report submitted to the Trustees yesterday &amp; adopted <span class='line-break'> </span>by them. _ Please bring this communication before the <span class='line-break'> </span>President, and Trustees as soon as possible, in order to <span class='line-break'> </span>a speedy action upon it.</p>
<p>In noticing the change comtemplated by this report,<span class='line-break'> </span>I feel compelled to say that I do not understand the portion <span class='line-break'> </span>of it which states the object of the measure to be "the <u>pro-</u><span class='line-break'> </span><u>motion</u>  of <u>harmony</u> am<u>ong</u> <u>the agents of the Corporation</u>".<span class='line-break'> </span>So far as appears from the document, it will apparently <span class='line-break'> </span>affect the relations of no other persons than the new <span class='line-break'> </span>Assistant Superintendent and myself.  I am happy to say, <span class='line-break'> </span>that there never has been, to my knowledge, any want of "harmony"<span class='line-break'> </span>between us, on the contrary I have, according to my pledge,</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279207">
<h3><a name="page-1279207">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 040)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>40</p>
<p>given to the Trustees in September last, "<u>cooperated</u> <u>cor<span class='line-break'></span>dially</u>" with <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Mr Mann</a> in every respect, and I have no <span class='line-break'> </span>complaint to make of any want of the same spirit on his <span class='line-break'> </span>part: were it otherwise, however, this measure would <span class='line-break'> </span>not be calculated to restore harmony, but rather the <span class='line-break'> </span>contrary.  The Trustees will pardon me, if I show this more <span class='line-break'> </span>particularly, not as a criticising of their action in reference <span class='line-break'> </span>to myself, but to suggest to them, the embarrassment of such <span class='line-break'> </span>relations, for the benefit of others who may succeed me. -</p>
<p>By the standing rules of the Cemetery, passed in 1841, it was <span class='line-break'> </span>made one of the duties of the Superintendent "to see <u>that</u> <u>all</u> <span class='line-break'> </span><u>persons in the employ of the Proprietors faithfully perform</u><span class='line-break'> </span><u>their duties</u>",  and he was also specially made responsible for <span class='line-break'> </span>various matters and things in connection with the labor <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; laborers.</p>
<p>By the report adopted in <date when='1855-03'>march 1855</date>, &amp; communicated <span class='line-break'> </span>to me in relation to the Office of an Assistant Superintendent,<span class='line-break'> </span>and defining his duties, it was stated as his duty <u>under</u><span class='line-break'> </span>the <u>Superintendent</u>, to have the immediate charge of the <span class='line-break'> </span>workmen, &amp; see that they perform the work assigned <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp;c. _ so much is harmonious: but it is obvious , that<span class='line-break'> </span>to hold one person responsible for the faithful perform<span class='line-break'></span>ance of work, while the sole power to engage &amp; discharge <span class='line-break'> </span>laborers is placed in the hands of his subordinate officer, <span class='line-break'> </span>would at once open the way for misunderstanding &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>differences.  This seems so clearly to me, to be the natural, <span class='line-break'> </span>if not the necessary result, that I cannot but apprehend<span class='line-break'> </span>that the Trustees feel that some want of "harmony"<span class='line-break'> </span>exists elsewhere than between me and my Assistant, and <span class='line-break'> </span>if this be so, it may serve to explain some other</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279208">
<h3><a name="page-1279208">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 041)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>41</p>
<p>things in the report in question, which are not clear <span class='line-break'> </span>to me at present. -</p>
<p>If, on the other hand, the Trustees meant to put the<span class='line-break'> </span>two offices on an equal footing, and to revoke the rule <span class='line-break'> </span>laid down in March last, in their general plan de<span class='line-break'></span>fining the duties of present &amp; future officers "by which <span class='line-break'> </span>it was made the duty of the Assistant to act under<span class='line-break'> </span>the <u>Superintendent"</u>, it would  be a measure which would <span class='line-break'> </span>not change my view of my present duty.</p>
<p>Two independent executive officers at the Cemetery <span class='line-break'> </span>without one directing mind above them, would not <span class='line-break'> </span>only not "<u>promote harmony</u>" , but would seriously interfere<span class='line-break'> </span>with the interest of the Proprietors.</p>
<p>The Trustees all know that I have, for several<span class='line-break'> </span>years, been desirous to withdraw from the Office of Sup<span class='line-break'></span>erintendent, &amp; that I have tendered my resignation to <span class='line-break'> </span>them.  Most of the Trustees know that the only reason <span class='line-break'> </span>why I did not peremptorily withdraw at once after the last <span class='line-break'> </span>Annual meeting, was in order that some person might <span class='line-break'> </span>be so far initiated into the duties of the office before I <span class='line-break'> </span>left, that individual proprietors might not be inconve<span class='line-break'></span>nienced, &amp; that the interests of the Corporation might not <span class='line-break'> </span>suffer by my action.</p>
<p>The reason no longer exists.  <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Mr Mann</a> has become <span class='line-break'> </span>somewhat acquainted in the Cemetery, &amp; has, no doubt, <span class='line-break'> </span>the confidence of the Trustees.  In order therefore, that the <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees, with greater freedom, may go on with their experiment,<span class='line-break'> </span>and make such arrangements as they deem requsite for <span class='line-break'> </span>the <u>promotion</u> of <u>harmony</u> among <u>the agents</u> of the <span class='line-break'> </span><u>Corporation</u> &amp; of <u>economy</u> <u>in its expenditure</u>." _<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279209">
<h3><a name="page-1279209">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 042)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>42</p>
<p>I now announce through you to the Trustees my<span class='line-break'> </span>unchangeable determination to withdraw at once from<span class='line-break'> </span>the post of Superintendent of the Cemetery of Mount<span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn, which I have now filled for several years,<span class='line-break'> </span>and I beg the Trustees to allow this resignation to<span class='line-break'> </span>take effect at the earliest date which is consistent<span class='line-break'> </span>with the due arrangement of the details incident<span class='line-break'> </span>to the change.</p>
<p>The severe and painful sickness of my wife, will<span class='line-break'> </span>prevent my immediately vacating the house which I now<span class='line-break'> </span>occupy, but I will do so as soon as possible. I<span class='line-break'> </span>should be glad to have this letter entered at length<span class='line-break'> </span>upon the Trustees records."</p>
<p>With respect yours etc.<span class='line-break'> </span>(Signed) <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Rufus Howe</a> Superintendent</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Mr Howe&apos;s resignation acceptedโ'><a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe's</a> resignation acceptedโ</span></p>
<p>After some remarks by different gentlemen, resolution<span class='line-break'> </span>of which the following is a copy, were offered by <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Mr Gould</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>and adopted.โ</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Resolutions in regard to Mr Howe'>Resolutions in regard to <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a></span></p>
<p>"Whereas <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Rufus Howe</a> has tendered<span class='line-break'> </span>to this Board the resignation of his Office of Superintendent<span class='line-break'> </span>of Mount Auburn, which he has so long &amp; so acceptably<span class='line-break'> </span>filled: we should not do justice to <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a> or to our own<span class='line-break'> </span>feelings, did we permit this occasion to pass without some<span class='line-break'> </span>expression of our sense of his eminent personal worth, &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>of the faithful services he has rendered to this Corporation</p>
<p>Be it therefore<span class='line-break'> </span>Resolved, that this Board have received,<span class='line-break'> </span>and do accept with regret, the resignation by <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a><span class='line-break'> </span>of the Office which, for so many years, he has held in this<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279210">
<h3><a name="page-1279210">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 043)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>43</p>
<p>Corporation,โ an office the arduous &amp; delicate duties of<span class='line-break'> </span>which he has discharged with singular fidelity, &amp; the<span class='line-break'> </span>most considerate kindness &amp; urbanity.</p>
<p>Resolved that <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe's</a> salary be continued<span class='line-break'> </span>up to the <date when='1855-09-01'>first of September next</date>, together with the use<span class='line-break'> </span>of the house which he occupies, should he find it de<span class='line-break'></span>sirable to retain it: &amp; that he be requested to retain<span class='line-break'> </span>his office till a successor can be appinted to take his place."</p>
<p>Voted that these resolutions be entered upon the<span class='line-break'> </span>records with the letter of <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a>, &amp; that a copy be sent<span class='line-break'> </span>to <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a>.โ</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee to nominate officers at Mt. Auburn &amp; prepare regulations for same_'>Com<sup>ee</sup> to nominate officers at Mt. Auburn &amp; prepare regulations for same_</span></p>
<p>On motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54775' title='Kuhn, George H.'>Mr Kuhn</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>on Grounds be requested to prepare a code of regulations for<span class='line-break'> </span>the government of the Officers at Mount Auburn, &amp; to nom<span class='line-break'></span>inate suitable persons to fill any existing vacancies.โ</p>
<p>After some further conversation opon various mat--<span class='line-break'> </span>ters. the meeting was dissolved.</p>
<p>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> Secretary</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees. Special Meeting June 18 &apos;55'>Trustees. Special Meeting <date when='1855-06-18'>June 18 '55</date></span></p>
<p>A Special Meeting of the Trustees, called "to hear<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; act upon the Report of the Committee in relation to Super--<span class='line-break'> </span>intendent &amp;c., &amp; to transact any other business may<span class='line-break'> </span>come before the meeting"โ was held at the office of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Secretary on <date when='1855-06-18'>the eighteenth day of June A.D. 1855.</date>โ</p>
<p>There were presentโ Messers <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Jacob-->Bigelow</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/58383' title='Crockett, George W.'>Crockett</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>, Read and</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>.โ</p>

<div id="page-1279211">
<h3><a name="page-1279211">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 044)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>44</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Comee to nominate Officers for the Cemetery'>Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> to nominate Officers for the Cemetery</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr Bigelow</a>, Charman of the Committee appointed<span class='line-break'> </span>at the last meeting, submitted a Report, of which<span class='line-break'> </span>the following is a copy.โ</p>
<p>"The Committee to whom was referred the<span class='line-break'> </span>subject of nominating resident officers at Mount<span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn, &amp; of preparing a code of regulations for the gov--<span class='line-break'> </span>ernment of the same:โ</p>
<p>Report, in part, โ That they recommend <span class='line-break'> </span>the appointment of <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Mr Jonathan Mann</a> as <u>Superintendent</u><span class='line-break'> </span><u>pro</u> <u>tem.</u> until further action of the Trustees: he to<span class='line-break'> </span>receive compensation for his services at the rate of<span class='line-break'> </span>Eight hundred dollars per annum, beginning on the<span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1855-07-01'>first day of July next</date>. And he is to perform all the<span class='line-break'> </span>duties hitherto required of the Superintendent, with<span class='line-break'> </span>power to call on other resident officers for assistance<span class='line-break'> </span>when necessary.โ</p>
<p>They further recommend ^<sup>that</sup> <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr B.F. Wyeth</a><span class='line-break'> </span>be retained, until further action of the Board,<span class='line-break'> </span>in the Office of Gate Keeper &amp; Superintendent's Clerk,<span class='line-break'> </span>with the same salary as at present.โ</p>
<p>(Signed) <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Jacob Bigelow</a>.โ for the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1855-06-18'>June 18<sup>th</sup> 1855</date>."โ</p>
<p>Voted - that the foregoing report be adopted.โ</p>

<div id="page-1279212">
<h3><a name="page-1279212">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 045)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>45</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Fence about tree'>Fence about tree</span></p>
<p>Voted, also that the same Committee be authorized <span class='line-break'> </span>to cause the erection of a suitable fence around the large <span class='line-break'> </span>oak tree in front of the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a>.โ</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Windows for Chapel'>Windows for <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a></span></p>
<p>Voted, that the Committee upon rebuilding the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> be <span class='line-break'> </span>authorized to procure new windows for the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span>cast iron sashes for the clerestory</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Foundation for Statues'>Foundation for Statues</span></p>
<p>Votedโ that the Committee upon Statues for the <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a>, be authorized to cause a foundation to be laid <span class='line-break'> </span>for the pedestals to said Statues.โ</p>
<p>The meeting was then dissolved<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>, Secretary</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees July 2 1855.'>Trustees <date when='1855-07-02'>July 2 1855</date>.</span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees was <span class='line-break'> </span>held at the Office of the Secretary on <date when='1855-07-02'>Monday, the second <span class='line-break'> </span>day of July A.D. 1855.</date></p>
<p>Presentโ Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Jacob-->Bigelow</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/58383' title='Crockett, George W.'>Crockett</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54775' title='Kuhn, George H.'>Kuhn</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, <span class='line-break'> </span>Little and</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>.โ</p>
<p>The Record of the last monthly meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; the latter portion of that of the last special meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>was read &amp; approved.</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->The Treasurer</a> having stated that <span class='line-break'> </span>large payments on the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> &amp;c. would soon have to be met, <span class='line-break'> </span>it was</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Finance Comee power to sell Stocks.'>Finance Com<sup>ee</sup> power to sell Stocks.</span></p>
<p>Voted. that we recommend to the Finance Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee to sell such stocks of this Corporation as they shall <span class='line-break'> </span>think most expedient.</p>
<p>Adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. J. Coolidge</a> Secretary</p>

<p>to the present condition of the <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>receiving tombs</a>โ:<span class='line-break'> </span>and as to the compensation for interments:โ</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee upon Receiving tomb Bonds'>Com<sup>ee</sup> upon <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving tomb</a> Bonds</span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Fees for Interments'>Fees for Interments</span></p>
<p>Voted that <span class='line-break'> </span>hereafter two dollars &amp; fifty cents ($2.50) shall be charged<span class='line-break'> </span>for digging a grave &amp; making an interment, and fifty (.50)<span class='line-break'> </span>cents additional for recording the same; and that, for each <span class='line-break'> </span>interment in a tomb, a proportional part of said sum<span class='line-break'> </span>be charged, according to the amount of service rendered <span class='line-break'> </span>in each case.</p>
<p>Another communication was submitted from <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'><!--Mann-->the Sup<sup>t</sup></a>, in relation to obstructions placed in the <span class='line-break'> </span>Avenues &amp; paths by persons making erections &amp; doing other work.โ</p>

<p>48</p>
<p>also in relation to rapid driving in the grounds &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>injury caused thereby: in relation to which it was</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Consent of Comee on Lots be obtained for erection of Tombs, Monuments &amp;c.'>Consent of Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots be obtained for erection of Tombs, Monumen<sup>ts</sup> &amp;c.</span></p>
<p>Voted. that no person shall hereafter erect any<span class='line-break'> </span>tomb, monument, fence or other <sup>important</sup> structure in Mount <span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn, without the consent of the Committee upon<span class='line-break'> </span>lots being first obtained; and in case of grave-<span class='line-break'></span>stones &amp; small structures the consent of the Superinten<span class='line-break'></span>dent shall be first obtained.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Gatekeeper to enforce rule as to fast driving'>Gatekeeper to enforce rule as to fast driving</span></p>
<p>Voted, that the<span class='line-break'> </span>gate-keeper be instructed to call the attention of all <span class='line-break'> </span>persons whom he may see violating the rule in re-<span class='line-break'></span>lation to rapid driving in the grounds, to said <span class='line-break'> </span>regulation.โ</p>

Brown</a>, son <span class='line-break'> </span>of the deceased, be designated to represent said <span class='line-break'> </span>lot, &amp; vote at the meetings of the Corporation, re-<span class='line-break'></span>ceiving a ticket of admission in that capacity, until <span class='line-break'> </span>the further action of this board.</p>
<p>It was alsoโ</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Quarter lots to be laid out'>Quarter lots to be laid out</span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Novr 5. 1855'>Trustees <date when='1855-11-05'>Nov<sup>r</sup> 5. 1855</date></span></p>
<p>The Regular monthly meeting of the Trustees was <span class='line-break'> </span>held at the usual place <date when='1855-11-05'>on Monday the fifth <span class='line-break'> </span>day of November AD. 1855</date>. ~</p>
<p>There were present Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Jacob-->Bigelow</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/58383' title='Crockett, George W.'>Crockett</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54775' title='Kuhn, George H.'>Kuhn</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little &amp;</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Accounts of late Supr Comee make partial report.'>Accounts of late Sup<sup>r</sup> Com<sup>ee</sup> make partial report.</span></p>
<p>The report of the Committee appointed to make a <span class='line-break'> </span>settlement with <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a>, after some explanation <span class='line-break'> </span>by the Chairman, <a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Mr Little</a>, was read by <a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'>Mr Bond</a>;<span class='line-break'> </span>showing a considerable amount, charged upon the books<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Superintendent, remaining uncollected.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Same Recommitted-'>Same Recommitted-</span></p>
<p>Voted to recommend the whole matter of unsettled<span class='line-break'> </span>accounts of the late Superintendent to the same Committee,<span class='line-break'> </span>with authority to collect all sums due the Corporation <span class='line-break'> </span>in such manner as they may think most expedient.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Receiving Tomb_ Comee for clearing out same report_'>Receiving Tomb_ Com<sup>ee</sup> for clearing out same report_</span></p>
<p>The same Committee, who were authorized to cause <span class='line-break'> </span>the removal of old deposits from the <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tombs</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>reported, that this work had been nearly accomplished<span class='line-break'> </span>by the Superintendent, excepting one or two cases where <span class='line-break'> </span>the identity of the deposit was lost.</p>
<p>The same Committee who were also requested to <span class='line-break'> </span>look into the present system of <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tomb</a> Bonds, <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; report, reported that the Committee upon Grounds &amp;c. --<span class='line-break'> </span>who were charged with the duty of inquiring whether a <span class='line-break'> </span>sum of money should not be placed upon deposit instead<span class='line-break'> </span>of giving bonds in such case, at the last meeting, - had<span class='line-break'> </span>a plan to propose in relation thereto.</p>
<p>The Committee upon Grounds &amp;c. accordingly made<span class='line-break'> </span>the following recommendations: ~</p>

<div id="page-1279219">
<h3><a name="page-1279219">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 052)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>52</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Receiving Tombs -'><a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tombs</a> -</span><span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Future regulation of - [?]y money deposit _'>Future regulation of - [?]y money deposit _</span></p>
<p>"That no deposit shall hereafter be made in <span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tombs</a> except upon payment of the <span class='line-break'> </span>sum of fifteen dollars: - that if, within six months <span class='line-break'> </span>after interment, the deposited body shall be removed<span class='line-break'> </span>to any part of Mount Auburn, ten dollars of the <span class='line-break'> </span>above sum shall be refunded:  otherwise the <span class='line-break'> </span>whole fifteen dollars shall be forever retained by the<span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation; and the Superintendent shall remove<span class='line-break'> </span>the body to such place as may be directed by the<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee on Grounds: or if the friends of the <span class='line-break'> </span>deceased desire it, they may remove the body from <span class='line-break'> </span>the Cemetery, forfeiting the whole sum of fifteen <span class='line-break'> </span>dollars. ~</p>
<p>The same committee to whom was referred</p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>the subject</th> <th>of introducing more light into the  <a href='/pages/subjects/57664' title='Entrance Gateway'>Keeper's Lodge</a>;-<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>of removing the <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Sup<sup>ts</sup> house</a> &amp; adjacent buildings:_</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>of constructing a new Avenue from a point near</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>the <a href='/pages/subjects/62651' title='Stable'>stable</a> to <a href='/pages/subjects/61222' title='Lime Avenue'>Lime Avenue</a> :-</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>of filling up a part or the whole of <a href='/pages/subjects/57864' title='Halcyon Lake'>Garden pond</a>:_</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Light for Lodge _'>Light for <a href='/pages/subjects/57664' title='Entrance Gateway'>Lodge</a> _</span></p>
<p>Reported.. _ that the attempt to introduce more light into <span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/57664' title='Entrance Gateway'>Lodge</a> will be made: --</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Old buildings _'>Old buildings _</span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='New Avenue _'>New Avenue _</span></p>

<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mr Tisdale</a> presented a form for a Circular in <span class='line-break'> </span>relation to the care of lots in the Cemetery, &amp; proposed<span class='line-break'> </span>that a copy should be sent to every Proprietor, which <span class='line-break'> </span>was read, with additions suggested by the Secretary <span class='line-break'> </span>designed to obtain information of Proprietors which might <span class='line-break'> </span>facilitate the progress of a new Catalogue.</p>
<p>Voted. that the Circular proposed by <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mr Tisdale</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>be adopted by the Trustees, &amp; that the matter suggested <span class='line-break'> </span>by the Secretary be stated briefly in a note appended to the <span class='line-break'> </span>same: - And that the Secretary be authorized to have <span class='line-break'> </span>the same printed, &amp; a copy sent to every Proprietor.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Adjournt_'>Adjourn<sup>t</sup>_</span></p>
<p>Voted that when we adjourn, it be to meet <span class='line-break'> </span>at this place on Saturday the second day of <span class='line-break'> </span>February, at 12 O'clock M. to hear the report of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Treasurer &amp; Sup<sup>t</sup> &amp; transact any other business <span class='line-break'> </span>that may come before the meeting. _</p>
<p>Adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. J. Coolidge</a> Sec<sup>y</sup></p>
<p>---------------------------------------------</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Feby 2d. 1856.'>Trustees <date when='1856-02-02'>Feb<sup>y</sup> 2<sup>d</sup>. 1856.</date></span></p>
<p>The adjourned meeting of the Trustees was <span class='line-break'> </span>held at the usual place on <date when='1856-02-02T12:00:00'>Saturday, the second <span class='line-break'> </span>day of February A. D. 1856, at 12 M.</date> . _</p>
<p>Present, the whole board. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='annual Rept of Treasr'>annual Rep<sup>t</sup> of Treas<sup>r</sup></span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->The Treasurer</a> presented his annual report, duly <span class='line-break'> </span>audited, &amp; the same was read. _</p>
<p>Voted to refer the same to the Annual Meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Proprietors on Monday next. _</p>

<p>changed so as to correspond with the numbers of the <span class='line-break'> </span>lots as actually occupied by them: _ <a href='/pages/subjects/62834' title='Holton, S. S.'>S.S. <p>Voted that the Treasurer be ordered to pay the<span class='line-break'> </span>same. _</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Proprietors 1856 Annual Meeting _'>Proprietors 1856 Annual Meeting _</span></p>
<p>Mount Auburn Cemetery</p>
<p>The Annual Meeting of the Proprietors of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery of Mount Auburn will be held at the <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62836' title='Meionaon, Tremont Temple'>Meionaon, Tremont Temple</a>, on <date when='1856-02-04T16:00:00'>Monday the 4<sup>th</sup> day<span class='line-break'> </span>day of February, at 4 o'clock P.M.</date> to hear the reports <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Trustees, Treasurer &amp; Superintendent: to choose <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees for the ensuing year &amp; to act on any other <span class='line-break'> </span>business which may legally come before the meeting.</p>
<p>By order of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> Secretary <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a> <date when='1856-01-26'>Jan<sup>y</sup> 26<sup>th</sup> 1856</date>.</p>

<div id="page-1279227">
<h3><a name="page-1279227">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 060)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>60</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Feby 4. 1856.'><date when='1856-02-04'>Feb<sup>y</sup> 4. 1856</date>.</span></p>
<p>Pursuant to the foregoing notice which was <span class='line-break'> </span>published more than seven days successively in <span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/58551' title='Boston Daily Advertiser'>Boston Daily Advertiser</a> &amp; in the <a href='/pages/subjects/62837' title='Boston Evening Transcript'>Boston <span class='line-break'> </span>Evening Transcript</a>, prior to the time of aid meeting, <span class='line-break'> </span>the Proprietors met at the time and place therein <span class='line-break'> </span>named.</p>
<p>A quorum being present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr. Bigelow</a> the <span class='line-break'> </span>President took the chair. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Records read _'>Records read _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> read the records of the last <span class='line-break'> </span>Annual Meeting.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Treasr&apos;s Annual Report _ Supt&apos;s. _'>Treas<sup>r</sup>'s Annual Report _ Supt's. _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->The Treasurer</a> read his annual report;<span class='line-break'> </span>also that of the Superintendent, which from the fact <span class='line-break'> </span>of his recent appointment, was less complete that it <span class='line-break'> </span>would otherwise have been. _</p>
<p>And said reports were accepted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Annual Report _'>Trustees Annual Report _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> in behalf of the Trustees presented <span class='line-break'> </span>their Annual report, &amp; the same was read &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span>accepted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Reports to be printed _'>Reports to be printed _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the reports of the Treasurer &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees be printed for general distribution among <span class='line-break'> </span>the Proprietors, &amp; that the Secretary give public notice <span class='line-break'> </span>of the place where every proprietor can call for a <span class='line-break'> </span>copy of the same. _</p>
<p>Voted to proceed to choose nine trustees for the <span class='line-break'> </span>ensuing year.</p>
<p>Upon motion this vote was subsequently re<span class='line-break'></span>considered.._ And it was then</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Twelve Trustees to be chosen. _'>Twelve Trustees to be chosen. _</span></p>
<p>Voted that this meeting proceed to choose twelve <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees for the ensuing year. _</p>

<div id="page-1279229">
<h3><a name="page-1279229">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 062)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>62</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Thanks to retiring Trustees _'>Thanks to retiring Trustees _</span></p>
<p>Voted,, that the thanks of this Corporation <span class='line-break'> </span>be presented to Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54775' title='Kuhn, George H.'>George H. Kuhn</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/58383' title='Crockett, George W.'>Geo W. <span class='line-break'> </span>Crockett</a> for their long &amp; faithful services as <span class='line-break'> </span>members of the Board of Trustees. _</p>
<p>Some discussion having arisen upon that part <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Trustees' report which stated that a large <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; respectable number of proprietors had addressed</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Conservatory for plants and flowers _'>Conservatory for plants and flowers _</span></p>
<p>a petition to the Trustees, that a conservatory for <span class='line-break'> </span>the preservation of plants &amp; flowers during the winter <span class='line-break'> </span>season might be erected at Mount Auburn: _</p>
<p>it was Voted that the Trustees are hereby <span class='line-break'> </span>instructed not to proceed in the erection of a conservatory <span class='line-break'> </span>at Mount Auburn, until they shall have first <span class='line-break'> </span>called a meeting of the Proprietors to consider the same, <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; shall have obtained the assent of the Proprietors thereto.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Resolutions respecting care of grounds &amp; workmen _'>Resolutions respecting care of grounds &amp; workmen _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/62847' title='Bird, J. H.'>Mr J. H. Bird</a> introduced some resolutions <span class='line-break'> </span>relating to the care of the grounds at Mt Auburn,<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; to the conduct of the workmen therein, after the <span class='line-break'> </span>reading of which</p>
<p>Voted to refer the same to the Board<span class='line-break'> </span>of Trustees just elected.</p>
<p>After which the meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>Adjourned without day <span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary _</p>
</div>

<div class="page-content">
<p>64</p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>Am<sup>t</sup> brought forward</th> <th>35.570.21<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>To <a href='/pages/subjects/62332' title='Parker, Henry Melville'>Henry M. W<sup>m</sup> Bond</a> Treas<sup>r</sup> 2 1/2 percent on $21.095.15</td> <td>527.38</td> </tr> <tr><td>" [To] Treas<sup>r</sup> of <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Mass. <p>The subscriber has examined the Cash account of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Treasurer of Mount Auburn Cemetery, for the year 1855. It is <span class='line-break'> </span>correctly cast. Satisfactory vouchers have been exhibited for<span class='line-break'> </span>all payments charged; as have also certificates for the various <span class='line-break'> </span>Stocks &amp; for the Scrip mentioned on this paper, On the<date when='1855-12-31'> 31<sup>st</sup> of <span class='line-break'> </span>December</date>, the Treasurer had in hand five hundred eighty three<span class='line-break'> </span>dollars 43/100 belonging to the Fund for Repairs. At same date,<span class='line-break'> </span>the balance of the general acount due him, was two hundred<span class='line-break'> </span>fifty two dollars 51/100. _</p>

<div id="page-1279234">
<h3><a name="page-1279234">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 067)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>67</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees ~ March 3d 1856.'>Trustees ~ <date when='1856-03-03'>March 3<sup>d</sup> 1856</date>.</span></p>
<p>The first regular monthly meeting of the Trustees <span class='line-break'> </span>was held agreeably to notice in the usual manner <span class='line-break'> </span>at the office of the Secretary on <date when='1856-03-03T12:00:00'>Monday the third day <span class='line-break'> </span>of March AD. 1856. at 12 o'clock M.</date> _</p>
<p>There were present Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Jacob-->Bigelow</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>, Read &amp;</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. ~</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr. Bigelow</a> took the chair. ~<span class='line-break'> </span>The record of the annual meeting was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Dr Lawrence declines to accept as Trustee.'><a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Dr Lawrence</a> declines to accept as Trustee.</span></p>
<p>A communication was read from <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Dr W<sup>m</sup> R. Lawrence</a><span class='line-break'> </span>declining to accept the office of Trustee to which he was <span class='line-break'> </span>elected. _</p>
<p>Voted that the same be referred to the next meeting of <span class='line-break'> </span>this board. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='President chosen -'>President chosen -</span></p>
<p>the Trustees then proceeded to ballot for a President for <span class='line-break'> </span>the ensuing year.  <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr. Jacob Bigelow</a>  had 8 votes,<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; was declared duly elected. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Treasurer chosen _'>Treasurer chosen _</span></p>
<p>The Trustees then proceeded to ballot for Treasurer.<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'>Geo. W<sup>m</sup>. Bond</a> had 8 votes &amp; was declared duly elected.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Secretary chosen _'>Secretary chosen _</span></p>
<p>They next proceeded to ballot for a Secretary.<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> had 8 votes &amp; was declared duly elected.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee on Lots chosen_'>Committee on Lots chosen_</span></p>
<p>They next proceeded to ballot for a Comittee upon Lots <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a> were declared <span class='line-break'> </span>duly elected. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279235">
<h3><a name="page-1279235">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 068)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>68</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee of Finance chosen _'>Committee of Finance chosen _</span></p>
<p>They next proceeded to ballot for a Committee of <span class='line-break'> </span>Finance: &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Messrs Little</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> were declared<span class='line-break'> </span>duly elected.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee upon Grounds enlarged &amp; chosen _'>Committee upon Grounds enlarged &amp; chosen _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the number of the Committee upon <span class='line-break'> </span>Grounds be increased to five for the present year.</p>
<p>The Trustees then proceeded to ballot for a Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>upon Grounds: ~ And Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Jacob-->Bigelow</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a> were declared duly <span class='line-break'> </span>elected. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee on Trees _'>Committee on Trees _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the Committee upon Grounds shall per<span class='line-break'></span>form the duties of the Committee upon Trees for the <span class='line-break'> </span>present year. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee upon Stone Farm.'>Committee upon <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a>.</span></p>
<p>Voted that the Committee upon Grounds shall also be <span class='line-break'> </span>the Committee upon the <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a> for the ensuing year.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee upon Chapel _'>Committee upon <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the Committee upon the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> be the same <span class='line-break'> </span>as last year _  Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Jacob-->Bigelow</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little &amp;</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Auditors chosen _'>Auditors chosen _</span></p>
<p>Voted that Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> be chosen Auditors of <span class='line-break'> </span>Accounts for the ensuing year. ~</p>
<p>Voted that until otherwise ordered five members of this</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Quorum _'>Quorum _</span></p>
<p>Board present at any meeting constitute a quorum for <span class='line-break'> </span>the transaction of business. --</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Duties and compensation of Officers'>Duties and compensation of Officers</span></p>
<p>Voted that the duties &amp; compensation of the various offices <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Corporation be referred to the Committee upon Grounds, <span class='line-break'> </span>to be reported upon at the next meeting of this Board,</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279236">
<h3><a name="page-1279236">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 069)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>69</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='referred to Comee on Grounds _'>referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds _</span></p>
<p>unless said Committee shall deem it necessary to <span class='line-break'> </span>call a special meeting sooner, in relation thereto.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Supt House referred to Comee on Grounds.'><a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Sup<sup>t</sup> House</a> referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds.</span></p>
<p>Voted to refer the hiring of a <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>house for the Sup<sup>t</sup></a> to the <span class='line-break'> </span>same Committee with full powers. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lots 1809, 1810_ T. Dowse&apos;s proposal _'><a href='/pages/subjects/67214' title='Lot 1809'>Lots 1809</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/64044' title='Lot 1810'><!--lot-->1810</a>_ <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>T. Dowse's</a> proposal _</span></p>
<p>A proposition from <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Thomas Dowse</a>, Proprietor of <a href='/pages/subjects/67214' title='Lot 1809'>lots 1809</a><span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/64044' title='Lot 1810'><!--lot-->1810</a>, to convey said lots to the corporation in trust, with <span class='line-break'> </span>the condition that no interment should be made therein, <span class='line-break'> </span>after that of his own body, was submitted verbally through the <span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary.</p>
<p>Voted that the same be referred to the committee upon lots <span class='line-break'> </span>^&amp; <sup>the Secretary</sup> with full power. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lot 349 _ Perpetl Repair of _'><a href='/pages/subjects/63592' title='Lot 349'>Lot 349</a> _ Perpet<sup>l</sup> Repair of _</span></p>
<p>An application was also verbally presented, through the Secretary, <span class='line-break'> </span>from <a href='/pages/subjects/58330' title='Barnard, Charles'>Charles Barnard</a>, Proprietor of <a href='/pages/subjects/63592' title='lot 349'>lot 349</a>, desiring to <span class='line-break'> </span>make a contract for the perpetual repair of said lot. _</p>
<p>Voted that the same be referred to the Committee upon Lots <span class='line-break'> </span>^<sup>&amp; the Secretary,</sup> with full power. --</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='H. W. Dutton &amp; others Petitn'><a href='/pages/subjects/62831' title='Dutton, H. W.'>H. W. Dutton</a> &amp; others Petit<sup>n</sup></span></p>
<p><small>The pettion of <a href='/pages/subjects/62831' title='Dutton, H. W.'>H. W. <p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Time of meeting changed _'>Time of meeting changed _</span></p>
<p>Voted that until otherwise ordered, the hour of meeting of <span class='line-break'> </span>this Board be 10 o'clock. _</p>
<p>The meeting was then dissolved.  Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. J. Coolidge</a> Secretary</p>

<h3><a name="page-1279237">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 070)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>70</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees April 7th &apos;56'>Trustees <date when='1856-04-07'>April 7<sup>th</sup> '56</date></span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees was <span class='line-break'> </span>held at the usual place, on <date when='1856-04-07T10:00:00'>Monday April 7<sup>th</sup> 1856,<span class='line-break'> </span>at 10 o'clock A.M. </date>~</p>
<p>There were present <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>,<span class='line-break'> </span>Read &amp;</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read &amp; approved. --</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Dr Lawrence accepts as Trustee'><a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Dr Lawrence</a> accepts as Trustee</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Dr Lawrence</a> appeared, withdrew his letter com<span class='line-break'></span>municated to the Board last month declining to accept <span class='line-break'> </span>a place upon the Board, &amp; signified his acceptance as <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustee. _</p>
<p>The Committee upon Grounds to whom was <span class='line-break'> </span>referred last month the question of the duties &amp; compensation <span class='line-break'> </span>of the various officers of the Corporation submitted a <span class='line-break'> </span>report which was considered item by item, as follows: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Superintendent&apos;s Salary &amp; back pay_'>Superintendent's Salary &amp; back pay_</span></p>
<p>1^<sup>st</sup> That is is expedient that the salary of the Superintendent <span class='line-break'> </span>be fixed at One thousand dollars per annum, commencing <span class='line-break'> </span>on the first of March last, with the use of a house, <span class='line-break'> </span>and no perquisites. _</p>
<p>2<sup>d</sup>  That the back salary since the retirement of <a href='/pages/subjects/58929' title='Howe, Rufus'>Mr Howe</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>be made up to <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Mr Mann</a> at the same proportional <span class='line-break'> </span>rate, to begin <date when='1855-06-30'>June 30<sup>th</sup> 1855</date>. ~</p>
<p>Voted that the foregoing report be accepted &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>adopted. _</p>
<p>The next item in the report was passed over for the time<span class='line-break'> </span>being - which was as follows: -</p>
<p>"The Committee not being fully agreed on the subject of a <span class='line-break'> </span>Gatekeeper &amp; Clerk voted to refer that subject to the <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees." _  Accepted</p>
</div>
</div>

<p>71</p>
<p>they further reported recommending</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Salary &amp; Duties of Secretary'>Salary &amp; Duties of Secretary</span></p>
<p>"That the salary of the Secretary hereafter be <span class='line-break'> </span>($300) three hundred dollars per annum, _ commencing <span class='line-break'> </span>on the first of January last _ in addition to his fees for <span class='line-break'> </span>conveyances, which are to remain as heretofore. _ He shall <span class='line-break'> </span>notify and attend all meetings, and shall record the doings<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Trustees &amp; of the Corporation.  He shall prepare and <span class='line-break'> </span>superintend the advertisements and other publications of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees _ shall prepare all legal instruments directed <span class='line-break'> </span>by the Trustees, and give legal opinions on all subjects <span class='line-break'> </span>required by them." ~</p>
<p>Voted that the foregoing report be accepted &amp; adopted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Supt Clerk _'>Sup<sup>t</sup> Clerk _</span></p>
<p>The subject of continuing the office of Sup<sup>t</sup> Clerk in connection <span class='line-break'> </span>with the office of Gate Keeper next came up for consideration, &amp; there <span class='line-break'> </span>being quite a difference of opinion expressed, it was finally</p>

<p>It was then Voted to postpone the matter of Superintendent's ^<sup>clerk</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; Gate Keeper till after the report of the Committee just chosen.</p>

<p>Upon the memorial of <a href='/pages/subjects/62812' title='Blaney, George A.'>Geo A. Blaney</a> (see p.54. Nov<sup>r</sup> '55)<span class='line-break'> </span>in reference to the care of <a href='/pages/subjects/62811' title='Lot 504'>lot No. 504</a>: โ</p>
<p>The Committee learn that said <a href='/pages/subjects/62812' title='Blaney, George A.'>Blaney</a>, after making <span class='line-break'> </span>his communication to the Trustees, &amp; before any action was had <span class='line-break'> </span>thereon by the committee, settled his administration account<span class='line-break'> </span>with the Probate Court, without attempting to carry out the <span class='line-break'> </span>provision in Mrs Blaney's will for the perpetual care of <span class='line-break'> </span>said lot: โ that the proprietorship of said lot is, upon <span class='line-break'> </span>our records, in the heirs of <a href='/pages/subjects/59722' title='French, Samuel'>Samuel French</a>; and that <span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees have not, in their opinion, power to compel <span class='line-break'> </span>specific performance of the provision aforesaid: โ</p>
<p>They therefore recommend the matter be discharged from further <span class='line-break'> </span>consideration โ</p>

<div id="page-1279240">
<h3><a name="page-1279240">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 073)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>73</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Geo. Bates&apos; memorial leave to withdraw'><a href='/pages/subjects/62826' title='Bates, George'>Geo. Bates'</a> memorial leave to withdraw</span></p>
<p>Upon the request of <a href='/pages/subjects/62826' title='Bates, George'>George Bates</a>, Proprietor of<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62827' title='Lot 708'>lots 708</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/62825' title='Lot 2263'><!--lot-->2263</a>, presented at the meeting in January,<span class='line-break'> </span>(see p. 58) that the number 2263 might be erased, &amp; that<span class='line-break'> </span>the lot might become part of <a href='/pages/subjects/62827' title='lot 708'>lot 708</a>. _</p>
<p>The Committee have ascertained that the<span class='line-break'> </span>lots are entirely separate &amp; they deem it inexpedient<span class='line-break'> </span>that they should be united in one number. _</p>
<p>Voted that the same be accepted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lots 420, 421, 422 - Petition for change of numbers upon record refused.'><a href='/pages/subjects/62828' title='Lot 420'>Lots 420</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62829' title='Lot 421'><!--lot-->421</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62830' title='Lot 422'><!--lot-->422</a> - Petition for change of numbers upon record refused.</span></p>
<p>Upon the petition of <a href='/pages/subjects/62831' title='Dutton, H. W.'>H. W. Dutton</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62832' title='Winship, Freeman'>Freeman Winship</a><span class='line-break'> </span>for the heirs of <a href='/pages/subjects/62833' title='Winship, Jonathan'>Jonathan Winship</a>, &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/62834' title='Holton, S. S.'>S.S. Holton</a>, proprietors<span class='line-break'> </span>of <a href='/pages/subjects/62828' title='Lot 420'>lots 420</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62829' title='Lot 421'><!--lot-->421</a>, &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/62830' title='Lot 422'><!--lot-->422</a> respectively, presented at the meeting<span class='line-break'> </span>in February, ^<sup>(see p. 58)</sup> referred to this Board of Trustees, to by them at<span class='line-break'> </span>the March Meeting, referred to the aforesaid Committee &amp; the<span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary: _ asking that the numbers upon their deeds, &amp; the<span class='line-break'> </span>record of the same may be changed, so as to correspond with<span class='line-break'> </span>the numbers of the lots as actually occupied by them,<span class='line-break'> </span>according to a statement submitted by them: _</p>
<p>The Committee have been unable to determine from<span class='line-break'> </span>so distant a period, how the error originally arose: but<span class='line-break'> </span>independently of that consideration they deem it improper to author<span class='line-break'></span>ize the alteration of the record as it would involve a depar<span class='line-break'></span>ture from the system which has been uniformly observed <span class='line-break'></span>a correspondence between the number of the deed &amp; the page<span class='line-break'> </span>of the record; and they see no necessity in this instance,<span class='line-break'> </span>since the parties by making transfers from one to the other,<span class='line-break'> </span>can obtain what they desire. _</p>
<p>They therefore report that the petitioners have leave<span class='line-break'> </span>to withdraw. _</p>
<p>Voted that the report be accepted. _</p>
</div>
</div>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees April 14. 1856.'>Trustees <date when='1856-04-14'>April 14. 1856</date>.</span></p>
<p>An adjourned meeting of the Trustees was held at the <span class='line-break'> </span>usual place on<date when='1856-04-14T10:00:00'> Monday April 14<sup>th</sup></date> (in accordance with<span class='line-break'> </span>the vote passed at the last meeting) at 10 o'clock A.M.</p>
<p>There were present <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> &amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>  &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. ~</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read &amp; approved. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Comee on mode of keeping books, accts, &amp;c at Gate  _'>Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> on mode of keeping books, accts, &amp;c at Gate  _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>, in behalf of Committee appointed at the last meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>to confer with the Superintendent &amp; report upon the best plan <span class='line-break'> </span>of keeping the books and accounts at Mount Auburn, <span class='line-break'> </span>submitted a report at length in writing, which was <span class='line-break'> </span>read, &amp; after some remarks, it was</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Office of Supt Clerk continued _'>Office of Sup<sup>t</sup> Clerk continued _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the following <span class='line-break'> </span>portion of it which relates to retaining the office of Superintendent's <span class='line-break'> </span>Clerk be adopted. _</p>
<p>"so far as the Committee could judge,</p>
</div>

<div id="page-1279244">
<h3><a name="page-1279244">Trustees Records, Volume 2, 1854 (page 077)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>77</p>
<p>"<a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr Wyeth</a> appears to be suited to the office <span class='line-break'> </span>"which he holds, and they unanimously recommend <span class='line-break'> </span>"that the present mode of having a Gate Keeper and <span class='line-break'> </span>"Clerk combined in one individual, appointed by the <span class='line-break'> </span>"Trustees, be continued.  Indeed, in their judgment, <span class='line-break'> </span>"it would be impossible for the business pertaining to the <span class='line-break'> </span>"office to be performed, unless a person competent to ful<span class='line-break'></span>"fil all the duties should be employed." _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report in part recommitted _'>Report in part recommitted _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the report be recomitted <span class='line-break'> </span>so far as related to the other matters contained therein <span class='line-break'> </span>for the purpose of enabling the Committee to prepare <span class='line-break'> </span>such votes as will definitely express what is substan<span class='line-break'></span>tially recommended. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Supt.s House.'><a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Supt.<sup>s</sup> House</a>.</span></p>
<p>The Committee upon Grounds, to which was referred the <span class='line-break'> </span>subject of building a <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Superintendent's house</a>, reported<span class='line-break'> </span>that they had examined some plans &amp; estimates, &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>were of opinion that a suitable house might be erected <span class='line-break'> </span>for the sum of not more than $3500. above the cellar.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee Chosen to superintend building of same.'>Committee Chosen to superintend building of same.</span></p>
<p>Whereupon it was</p>
<p>Voted to choose and empower a Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>of three to erect a <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>house for Superintendent</a>, upon such <span class='line-break'> </span>part of land of the Corporation between Brattle and Mount <span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn Streets as they may think most suitable, the house <span class='line-break'> </span>itself to cost not more than ($3500) thirty-five hundred <span class='line-break'> </span>dollars. _ Accordingly</p>

<p>The Committee chosen at the last meeting to <span class='line-break'> </span>consider &amp; report whether the contracts for statuary <span class='line-break'> </span>in the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> can be rescinded, submitted a written <span class='line-break'> </span>report signed by Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. <p>After a lengthy discussion it was</p>

<p>Voted that the Committee upon Grounds, being the</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Stone farm _ repairs on house. authorized _ &amp; lease of land _'><a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone farm</a> _ repairs on house. authorized _ &amp; lease of land _</span></p>
<p>Committee upon the <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a>, be authorized to expend <span class='line-break'> </span>a sum not exceeding $200 for repairs &amp; alterations <span class='line-break'> </span>upon the Stone house, so that the same may accommo<span class='line-break'></span>date two families; and to lease the land of the farm <span class='line-break'> </span>exclusive of the buildings, upon such terms as they think <span class='line-break'> </span>proper. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Adjourt _'>Adjour<sup>t</sup> _</span></p>
<p>Voted to adjourn to meet next <date when='1856-04-21T16:00:00'>Monday (April <span class='line-break'> </span>21<sup>st</sup>) at 4 o'clock P.M.</date> _<span class='line-break'> </span>Adjourned <span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. <p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees _ April 21. 1856'>Trustees _<date when='1856-04-21'> April 21. 1856</date></span></p>
<p>An adjourned meeting of the Trustees was held <span class='line-break'> </span>at the usual place on <date when='1856-04-21T16:00:00'>Monday April 21<sup>st</sup>, 1856. at <span class='line-break'> </span>4 o'clock P.M.</date> _</p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. <p>The record of the last meeting was read &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>approved.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Tower door to be open on Sunday'><a href='/pages/subjects/54814' title='Washington Tower'>Tower</a> door to be open on Sunday</span></p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'><!--Mann-->the Superintendent</a> be instructed to <span class='line-break'> </span>keep the door of the <a href='/pages/subjects/54814' title='Washington Tower'>Tower</a> open upon Sunday, as upon other <span class='line-break'> </span>days. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on best mode of keeping books &amp;c at Gate, reported sundry regulations as follows -'>Com<sup>ee</sup> on best mode of keeping books &amp;c at Gate, reported sundry regulations as follows -</span></p>
<p>The Committee appointed to consider the best mode <span class='line-break'> </span>of keeping the books &amp; accounts at Mt Auburn &amp; other duties <span class='line-break'> </span>performed by the Gate Keeper &amp; Clerk, having made a report at <span class='line-break'> </span>the last meeting, &amp; that report having been recommitted to them<span class='line-break'> </span>with instructions to report certain specific votes on the <span class='line-break'> </span>matters recommended in said report, submitted the <span class='line-break'> </span>following votes, by <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>: _ which were severally <span class='line-break'> </span>adopted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Interment permits _'>Interment permits _</span></p>
<p>1<sup>st</sup> That no interments be permitted at Mount Auburn <span class='line-break'> </span>without such permits as may be required by law shall <span class='line-break'> </span>be presented at the gate. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Fees for same to be printed on back _'>Fees for same to be printed on back _</span></p>
<p>2<sup>d</sup> That the particulars and amounts of the fees of <span class='line-break'> </span>burial shall be printed on the backs of the permits, and <span class='line-break'> </span>at the foot shall be added the words "payable at the time <span class='line-break'> </span>of interment." _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Safe for Books &amp; papers at Gate _'>Safe for Books &amp; papers at Gate _</span></p>
<p>3<sup>d</sup> That an iron save be purchased for the safe<span class='line-break'></span>keeping of the Records &amp; other books &amp; documents at the <span class='line-break'> </span>office at Mount Auburn, at an expense not exceeding <span class='line-break'> </span>one hundred &amp; fifty dollars. _<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on Rules &amp;c of Interment -'>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Rules &amp;c of Interment -</span></p>
<p>4<sup>th</sup> That a Committee of two Trustees to be denom<span class='line-break'></span>inated "the <u>Committee on Rules &amp; Regulations of<span class='line-break'> </span>interments", &amp;c</u>, be chosen annually, whose duty it <span class='line-break'> </span>shall be to examine, from time to time, to see that the <span class='line-break'> </span>matters named in the above votes &amp; those of a kindred <span class='line-break'> </span>nature, and all rules and regulations pertaining to the <span class='line-break'> </span>same, shall be faithfully executed. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='mode of keeping records &amp;c - at Gate referred to above Comee'>mode of keeping records &amp;c - at Gate referred to above Com<sup>ee</sup></span></p>
<p>5<sup>th</sup>  That the "Committee on Rules and Regulations of <span class='line-break'> </span>interments &amp;c" be charged with the subject of the mode <span class='line-break'> </span>of keeping the Records, books &amp;c at Mount Auburn, &amp; that <span class='line-break'> </span>they make such changes in the same, as they, in concert <span class='line-break'> </span>with the Treasurer, may deem expedient.</p>
<p><b><a href='/pages/subjects/57664' title='Entrance Gateway'><!--entrance-->Office at Gate</a> - do [referred to above Com<sup>ee</sup>] -</b></p>
<p>6<sup>th</sup> That the same Committee be requested to consider <span class='line-break'> </span>the subject of the <a href='/pages/subjects/57664' title='Entrance Gateway'><!--entrance-->Office at the Gate</a>, and what alterations <span class='line-break'> </span>or additions, if any, it would be expedient to make, &amp; to <span class='line-break'> </span>report at some future meeting of the Board. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Choice of Comee postponed _'>Choice of Com<sup>ee</sup> postponed _</span></p>
<p>By unanimous consent the choice of the Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>provided for in the 4<sup>th</sup> vote was deferred to the next meeting.</p>

<p>by unanimous consent, be adopted. _</p>

(1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R.
