<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Both reports ordered to be recorded -'>Both reports ordered to be recorded -</span></p>
<p>Voted that both the majority &amp; minority reports on the <span class='line-break'> </span>Statuary be recorded as well as filed, _</p>
<p>The majority report is as follows. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Copy of majority Report upon Statuary'>Copy of majority Report upon Statuary</span></p>
<p>"The Committee appointed 'to examine, consider, &amp; report <span class='line-break'> </span>whether any or all of the contracts for making statuary for <span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> can be rescinded', have met &amp; considered the <span class='line-break'> </span>subject referred to them, _ and a majority of the Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>report _ that, although a legal contract can be <u>rescinded</u><span class='line-break'> </span>by the consent of <u>both</u> the parties to it, one of the parties cannot<span class='line-break'> </span>do so:  He may <u>repudiate</u> or <u>break</u> the contract, subjecting <span class='line-break'> </span>himself, of course, to reclamation by the other party, but <span class='line-break'> </span>he cannot rescind it.  As the artists, with whom the contracts <span class='line-break'> </span>for Statuary have been made, are in Italy, it has not</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279249">
<h3><a name="page-1279249">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 082)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>82</p>
<p>been possible to consult them touching  the rescission of <span class='line-break'> </span>their engagements with the Corporation.  But as this might <span class='line-break'> </span>be done in a few weeks, the undersigned deem it proper <span class='line-break'> </span>to express the opinion that they do not consider it expe<span class='line-break'></span>dient to take any further steps in this matter._</p>
<p>Whether, if the  purchase of statuary for the Cemetery<span class='line-break'> </span>were not an open question, it were expedient to make <span class='line-break'> </span>such purchase, is a very different one from that of re<span class='line-break'></span>scinding contracts made many months since, upon <span class='line-break'> </span>which considerable sums of money have been paid, <span class='line-break'> </span>for work already done.  It is to be recollected that <span class='line-break'> </span>these contracts were entered into by virtue of a vote of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees passed in September &amp; October 1854 _ which <span class='line-break'> </span>was adopted by seven members out of nine &amp; sanctioned<span class='line-break'> </span>by their <u>written</u> approval - an unprecended formality of this <span class='line-break'> </span>board; since then two elections of Trustees have taken <span class='line-break'> </span>place, at which all those members who voted for the pur<span class='line-break'></span>chase of Statuary, who did not voluntarily withdraw for <span class='line-break'> </span>their own convenience - were rechosen by the Proprietors.</p>
<p>The majority of the Committee are of opinion that it <span class='line-break'> </span>is expedient to go on with the contracts made for the <span class='line-break'> </span>acquisition of the three <a href='/pages/subjects/60946' title='James Winthrop Statue'>statues of John Winthrop</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54268' title='James Otis Statue'>James <span class='line-break'> </span>Otis</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/52561' title='John Adams Statue'>John Adams</a>: - And they are also of opinion, <span class='line-break'> </span>that, in future, all appropriations for the embellish<span class='line-break'></span>ment and improvement of the cemetery be restricted <span class='line-break'> </span>(Signed) <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Charles P. Curtis</a> <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>William R. Lawrence</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279250">
<h3><a name="page-1279250">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 083)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>83</p>
<p>The following is a copy of the minority report, _<span class='line-break'> </span>aforesaid. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Copy of Minority Report upon Statuary'>Copy of Minority Report upon Statuary</span></p>
<p>"The undersigned, a minority of the Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>appointed to take into consideration the subject of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Statues, &amp; whether it be expedient to proceed with <span class='line-break'> </span>the project of placing them in the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'>Chapel at Mount <span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn</a>, and to report any other matters pertaining <span class='line-break'> </span>to the same, has attended to the duty &amp; submits <span class='line-break'> </span>the following report.</p>
<p>The undersigned is aware that a diversity of <span class='line-break'> </span>opinion has existed upon the expediency, as well as the <span class='line-break'> </span>right of the Trustees to expend the money of the Corpora<span class='line-break'></span>tion for purposes extraneous to, if not directly adverse<span class='line-break'> </span>to the privileges conferred upon it by the Charter.</p>
<p>By the Act of incorporation, the Trustees were<span class='line-break'> </span>allowed to expend the money received from the sale <span class='line-break'> </span>of lots 'for the preservation, improvement, embellishment<span class='line-break'> </span>and enlargement of the Cemetery and Garden, and the <span class='line-break'> </span>incidental expenses thereof, &amp; for no other purpose what<span class='line-break'></span>soever."</p>
<p>The question then naturally arises what is the <span class='line-break'> </span>obvious &amp; real meaning of these terms, and what construc<span class='line-break'></span>tion was designed to be placed upon them?</p>
<p>In order that a correct conclusion may be arrived at, <span class='line-break'> </span>it is necessary to revert for a moment, to the circumstances <span class='line-break'> </span>under which the act of incorporation was obtained, and <span class='line-break'> </span>what was designed by those who originated the project.<span class='line-break'> </span>It appears to the undersigned, that the design was this <span class='line-break'></span>the subject of interments within the limits of the City having <span class='line-break'> </span>become one of great importance in our community, and <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279251">
<h3><a name="page-1279251">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 084)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>84</p>
<p>an evil which would be likely to increase as the <span class='line-break'> </span>population became more dense, it was very desirable <span class='line-break'> </span>that the system should be changed, so far as it was practicable<span class='line-break'> </span>to do so, &amp; some place of interment be secured in the vicinity <span class='line-break'> </span>of the <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>City<!--of Boston--></a> which should obviate the evil complained of. _</p>
<p>For these purposes the grounds now known as <span class='line-break'> </span>"Mount Auburn" were obtained &amp; consecrated.</p>
<p>An act of incorporation was granted by the Legis<span class='line-break'></span>lature, giving certain privilesges to, &amp; placing certain <span class='line-break'> </span>restrictions upon the Corporation, one of which was that <span class='line-break'> </span>the moneys received from the sales of lots should be ex<span class='line-break'></span>pended for no other purpose than those stated in this <span class='line-break'> </span>report.</p>
<p>It is obvious from the terms of the Charter that the <span class='line-break'> </span>right to erect an expensive <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->chapel</a>, and furnish it with <span class='line-break'> </span>splendid statuary, or other works of art, if it exists at <span class='line-break'> </span>all, must be derived fro the authority to embellish the <span class='line-break'> </span>grounds. _</p>
<p>An opinion has been given by one of the present <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee, (<a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>) that the Trustees do possess the legal <span class='line-break'> </span>right, at least so far as to expend fifteen thousand dol<span class='line-break'></span>ars for Statuary: which opinion is on the records of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation; and, as it has been accepted &amp; acted upon <span class='line-break'> </span>by the Trustees, it is not necessary here to discuss the <span class='line-break'> </span>question, nor to say how large a field the word "embellishment"<span class='line-break'> </span>appears to the undersigned to cover. _</p>
<p>If then it be assumed for the purposes of this discus<span class='line-break'></span>sion, that the Trustees have the legal right, the next <span class='line-break'> </span>question is as to the expediency of spending money for such <span class='line-break'> </span>embellishments. _<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279252">
<h3><a name="page-1279252">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 085)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>85</p>
<p>We have erected a substantial <a href='/pages/subjects/54812' title='Perimeter Fence'><!--Perimeter-->iron fence</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/57664' title='Entrance Gateway'>stone <span class='line-break'> </span>gate-way</a> _ a beautiful <a href='/pages/subjects/54814' title='Washington Tower'>Tower</a> _ and a <a href='/pages/subjects/61326' title='Well House Gazebo'>Well House</a>. _<span class='line-break'> </span>These are all useful &amp; desirable, &amp; add much to the beauty <span class='line-break'> </span>of the  place. _</p>
<p>We have erected a <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> at a cost of between forty &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>fifty thousand dollars, merely for embellisment, the very few <span class='line-break'> </span>funeral services held there during this year, if there be any, <span class='line-break'> </span>hardly being worthy of mention, and the building being designed <span class='line-break'> </span>for no other purpose. _  It has also been determiend to expend <span class='line-break'> </span>fifteen thousand dollars more for statues of certain men <span class='line-break'> </span>who deservidly stand high in the history of the country . _ <span class='line-break'> </span>What other embellishments the present board of Trustees, or <span class='line-break'> </span>their successors in office may deem it proper to make, by <span class='line-break'> </span>adding other works of art, the undersigned cannot foretell.</p>
<p>All the embellishments named above have been completed, <span class='line-break'> </span>or so nearly so, as to render it too late to make any change,<span class='line-break'> </span>with the exception of the Statuary _ this matter is still open,<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; a change can be made, &amp; a considerable portion of the contemplated<span class='line-break'> </span>expenditure be saved to the Corporation. _</p>
<p>The undersigned has looked into this subject, and <span class='line-break'> </span>finds it to stand substantially thus: Contracts have been <span class='line-break'> </span>entered into with <a href='/pages/subjects/52560' title='Rogers, Randolph'>Randolph Rogers</a> for a <a href='/pages/subjects/52561' title='John Adams Statue'>statue of John Adams</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>at a cost of $5,000, on which $1000 have been paid _ with <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53577' title='Greenough, Richard S.'>Richard S. Greenough</a> for a <a href='/pages/subjects/60946' title='James Winthrop Statue'>statue of Gov. Winthrop</a> at a <span class='line-break'> </span>cost of $5000 on which $1000 have been paid _ and the prelim<span class='line-break'></span>inaries to a contract with <a href='/pages/subjects/53236' title='Crawford, Thomas'>Thomas Crawford</a> for a <a href='/pages/subjects/54268' title='James Otis Statue'>statue <span class='line-break'> </span>of James Otis</a> at a cost of $5000 on which nothing has<span class='line-break'> </span>been paid. _</p>
<p>We are told that this statuary was one of the original <span class='line-break'> </span>designs of the founders of Mount Auburn.  This may or may </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279253">
<h3><a name="page-1279253">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 086)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>86</p>
<p>not have been the case. _ But if it were so, the under<span class='line-break'></span>signed can see in that fact no good reason why the <span class='line-break'> </span>design should be carried out, if it be inexpedient to<span class='line-break'> </span>do so. _ That such however was the original design,<span class='line-break'> </span>would hardly be gathered from the language of <a href='/pages/subjects/53237' title='Story, Joseph'>Judge <span class='line-break'> </span>Story</a>, as quoted in the legal opinion before referred to,<span class='line-break'> </span>or if it were the design that it was known to him. _</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr. Curtis</a> says in that opinion "It is worth ^<sup>noting</sup> nothing <span class='line-break'> </span>here, that <a href='/pages/subjects/53237' title='Story, Joseph'>Judge Story</a> in 1843, in a written report <span class='line-break'> </span>upon the subject of contemplated improvements at the <span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery, alludes particularly to the use of the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->proposed chapel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>for the purpose of a shelter for busts &amp; statues, but is guarded <span class='line-break'> </span>in his language, &amp; refers only to such "marble busts and <span class='line-break'> </span>statues &amp; other sepulchral monuments which may from <span class='line-break'> </span>time to time be placed there by liberal benefactors &amp; friends<span class='line-break'> </span>in memory of the dead' _ and <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> adds _<span class='line-break'> </span>'<u>It is probable</u> <u>that it had not then occurred to his</u> <span class='line-break'> </span><u>mind that</u> <u>the Trustees would</u> <u>ever take this thing upon</u> <span class='line-break'> </span><u> themselves.</u>.  It is therefore very plain, that <a href='/pages/subjects/53237' title='Story, Joseph'>Judge Story</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>the first President of the Corporation, was ignorant of the <span class='line-break'> </span>fact that these statues formed a part of the original <span class='line-break'> </span>design.</p>
<p>The undersigned is of opinion, that if the amount <span class='line-break'> </span>to be paid for these statues should be placed at interest <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; the income derived from it be spent upon the grounds, _<span class='line-break'> </span>in keeping them in more perfect order than has hitherto<span class='line-break'> </span>been the case, that it would be far more for the repu<span class='line-break'></span>tation of the place, and the pleasure &amp; comfort of the visitors<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; proprietors, than would be the exhibition of the statuary <span class='line-break'> </span>however beautiful. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279254">
<h3><a name="page-1279254">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 087)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>87</p>
<p>One among the many reasons why this statuary should <span class='line-break'> </span>not be procured, is the state of the finances of the Corporation. _<span class='line-break'> </span>By the last annual report fo the Treasurer, it appears <span class='line-break'> </span>that the property belonging to the Corporation amounted to <span class='line-break'> </span>the sum of $29,900. Estimating the stocks in which it <span class='line-break'> </span>was invested at par _ while nearly all of them are greatly <span class='line-break'> </span>depreciated. _ It also appears by the Treasurer's report,<span class='line-break'> </span>that the expenditures exceeded the income, (which included<span class='line-break'> </span>the sales of lots during the year) $252.51. We shall<span class='line-break'> </span>therefore find, when all the lots are sold, if we proceed<span class='line-break'> </span>in this manner, that we have the embellishments on hand,<span class='line-break'> </span>but no fund &amp; no means to meet the current expenses <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Corporation. _</p>
<p>Another reason why the statuary should not be placed <span class='line-break'> </span>in the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> is, that in the opinion of many persons<span class='line-break'> </span>who profess, or are supposed to be judges in such matters, the <span class='line-break'> </span>light will not be good, and the beauties of the statues will not<span class='line-break'> </span>be seen to advantage, nor justice be done to the artists who <span class='line-break'> </span>shall construct them. _</p>
<p>But it is not necessary here to detail all the objections <span class='line-break'> </span>to the plan. _</p>
<p>The undersigned believes that an arrangement can be <span class='line-break'> </span>entered into with the artists who have been engaged to make<span class='line-break'> </span>the statues, to relinquish the contracts by making them a liberal<span class='line-break'> </span>compensation for the work already done: but if that cannot <span class='line-break'> </span>be accomplished, that some disposition can be made of the <span class='line-break'> </span>statues when completed, by which a large part of the expen<span class='line-break'></span>diture may be returned to the Corporation; and if only<span class='line-break'> </span>one half of the amount should be saved, that sum at <span class='line-break'> </span>compound interest, in twelve years would give the original</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279255">
<h3><a name="page-1279255">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 088)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>88</p>
<p>sum expended - whereas if the statues should be placed in <span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a>, it is very evident that, during the twelve years <span class='line-break'> </span>they would not increase in value.</p>
<p>In conclusion, the undersigned would recommend <span class='line-break'> </span>the passage of the following votes _ to wit: _</p>
<p>That it is inexpedient to place the statues of <a href='/pages/subjects/60946' title='James Winthrop Statue'>Gov<sup>r</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>Winthrop</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54268' title='James Otis Statue'>James Otis</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/52561' title='John Adams Statue'>John Adams</a> in the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>or Grounds of Mount Auburn. _</p>
<p>That a Committee be appointed with full powers <span class='line-break'> </span>to carry the suggestions contained in this report regarding<span class='line-break'> </span>the Statues into effect, in such manner as they may <span class='line-break'> </span>deem expedient.</p>
<p>All of which is respectfully submitted<span class='line-break'> </span>(signed) <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Cha<sup>s</sup> G. Nazro</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Foundation for statues to be placed in Chapel _'>Foundation for statues to be placed in <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the building Committee of the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> be <span class='line-break'> </span>instructed to place a foundation en each corner of the same <span class='line-break'> </span>beneath the floor thereof, to receive the four marble statues <span class='line-break'> </span>intended for the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> whenever they shall have been <span class='line-break'> </span>completed &amp; delivered to the Corporation. _</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> presented the following memorial respecting<span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/56255' title='Joseph Story Statue'>Story Statue Fund</a>, signed by a majority in value of <span class='line-break'> </span>the subscribers thereto: which was read, &amp; it was</p>
<p>Voted that the same be recorded &amp; filed. _</p>
<p>Copy _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Memorial of a part of the subscribers to Story Statue_'>Memorial of a part of the subscribers to <a href='/pages/subjects/56255' title='Joseph Story Statue'>Story Statue</a>_</span></p>
<p>"the undersigned, subscribers now surviving, to the fund <span class='line-break'> </span>for the purchase of a <a href='/pages/subjects/56255' title='Joseph Story Statue'>Statue of the late Mr Justice Story</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>respectfully represent to the Trustees of the Cemetery of <span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn, that the sums subscribed by them</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279256">
<h3><a name="page-1279256">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 089)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>89</p>
<p>were given on the condition that the <a href='/pages/subjects/56255' title='Joseph Story Statue'><!--Story-->Statue</a> should <span class='line-break'> </span>be placed in the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> of the Cemetery: and inasmuch as <span class='line-break'> </span>the said <a href='/pages/subjects/56255' title='Joseph Story Statue'><!--Story-->statue</a> is completed, the undersigned request <span class='line-break'> </span>that it may be removed to its place of destination, as <span class='line-break'> </span>early as convenient.  Ten years have elapsed since the sub<span class='line-break'></span>scriptions were paid into the hands of the Treasurer of <span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn, &amp; about one third of the contributors have<span class='line-break'> </span>departed this life without witnessing the accomplishment <span class='line-break'> </span>of the object for which their contributions were made <span class='line-break'> </span>by them and accepted by the Trustees of the Cemetery.<span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1856-04'>April. 1856</date>. _</p>

(1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a> be <span class='line-break'> </span>Special Committee to carry the last vote into effect. - -</p>

<br />
<div id="page-1279257">
<h3><a name="page-1279257">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 090)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>90</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees May 5. 1856'>Trustees <date when='1856-05-05'>May 5. 1856</date></span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees <span class='line-break'> </span>was held at the usual place on <date when='1856-05-05T10:00:00'>Monday the <span class='line-break'> </span>fifth day of May AD 1856. at 10 o'clock A. M.</date> _</p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, &amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>, Read &amp;</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read and approved. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Foundations for Statues _'>Foundations for Statues _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the duty of having suitable foundations <span class='line-break'> </span>placed in the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> for statues, assigned, at the last <span class='line-break'> </span>meeting, to the building Committee of the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a>, be trans<span class='line-break'></span>ferred from that Committee to the Special Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>then appointed to superintend the removal of the <a href='/pages/subjects/56255' title='Joseph Story Statue'>Story<span class='line-break'> </span>Statue</a> to the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a>, viz.  <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the Pres<sup>t</sup></a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Messrs Little</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a>.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on Rules of Interment chosen _ '>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Rules of Interment chosen _ </span></p>
<p>Voted. _ upon nomination by <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, _ that <span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> be chosen as the <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee upon Rules of Interment &amp;c. the choice<span class='line-break'> </span>of which was postponed from the last meeting. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Publication of said Rules authorized _'>Publication of said Rules authorized _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the aforesaid Committee be authorized to <span class='line-break'> </span>publish the requirements of the law respecting interments, <span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; the recent action of this board in such manner as they <span class='line-break'> </span>think expedient. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lots, layout out of _'>Lots, layout out of _</span></p>
<p>A communication was received from the Superintendent in relation <span class='line-break'> </span>to the mode of laying out lots &amp;c, which was referred to the Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>upon Lots. _  The meeting was then dissolved _ <span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. J. Coolidge</a>,, Secretary _<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<h3><a name="page-1279258">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 091)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>91</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees. May 16. 1856.'>Trustees. <date when='1856-05-16'>May 16. 1856.</date></span></p>
<p>A special meeting of the Trustees was held <span class='line-break'> </span>at the usual place on <date when='1856-05-16T10:00:00'>Friday May 16<sup>th</sup>. 1856,<span class='line-break'> </span>at 10 o'clock A. M.</date> _</p>
<p>There were present <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> &amp; Messrs <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>.</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> stated that the meeting was called <span class='line-break'> </span>at the request of the Treasurer on account of the <span class='line-break'> </span>suggeston of some doubt as to his authority to accept &amp; pay <span class='line-break'> </span>certain drafts. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Concerning authority of Treasurer to pay drafts, &amp;c'>Concerning authority of Treasurer to pay drafts, &amp;c</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->The Treas<sup>r</sup></a> read from the bye-laws such portions as <span class='line-break'> </span>related to his duty in connection with the Committee of<span class='line-break'> </span>Finance, &amp; proposed the adoption of an additional<span class='line-break'> </span>bye-law authorizing the Treas<sup>r</sup> to pay all bills contracted <span class='line-break'> </span>by any Committee duly authorized, presented for payment<span class='line-break'> </span>with the approval of the Committee or a majority thereof.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' &amp; concerning Code of Bye-Laws _'> &amp; concerning Code of Bye-Laws _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a> moved the appointment of a Com<sup>ee</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>to prepare a code of bye-laws &amp; that the votes proposed<span class='line-break'> </span>by the Treas<sup>r</sup> be also referred to said Committee.</p>
<p>After some discussion, the motion was withdrawn _ <span class='line-break'> </span>the mover being informed that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> was author<span class='line-break'></span>ized by a vote of the Trustees in <date when='1856-09'>Sept<sup>r</sup> last</date> to compile all <span class='line-break'> </span>standing rules &amp; orders of the Corporation &amp; Trustees, &amp; would <span class='line-break'> </span>soon report; and the Trustees being satisfied that no bye<span class='line-break'></span>law was needed to meet the case on account of which <span class='line-break'> </span>the meeting was called. _</p>
</div>
</div>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees June 2d 1856.'>Trustees<date when='1856-06-02'> June 2<sup>d</sup> 1856</date>.</span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees was <span class='line-break'> </span>held at the usual place on <date when='1856-06-02T10:00:00'>Monday the second <span class='line-break'> </span>day of June, at 10 o'clock. A. M. </date> _</p>
<p>There were present _ <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, &amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, <span class='line-break'> </span>Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. -</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Quorum present but no vote passed.'>Quorum present but no vote passed.</span></p>
<p>The Committee appointed at the last meeting to <span class='line-break'> </span>confer with the Directors of the <a href='/pages/subjects/63961' title='Cambridge Railroad'>Cambridge Horse Rail<span class='line-break'></span>road Company</a> in reference to the location of their tracks <span class='line-break'> </span>at <a href='/pages/subjects/57664' title='Entrance Gateway'>Mt. Auburn Gate</a>, stated that they had had a conference,<span class='line-break'> </span>but were not yet able to report.</p>
<p>After further informal conversation upon various <span class='line-break'> </span>matters connected with the business of the Corporation, the meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>was dissolved.   Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. J. Coolidge</a> Secretary.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees June 24, 1856. Special Meeting _'>Trustees <date when='1856-06-24'>June 24, 1856</date>. Special Meeting _</span></p>
<p>A special meeting of the Trustees called by the<span class='line-break'> </span>President, was convened at the usual place, on<span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1856-06-24T10:00:00'>Tuesday June 24<sup>th</sup> at 10 o'clock AM.</date> _</p>
<p>These were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> &amp; Messrs<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>, Read &amp;</a><span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. ~</p>
<p>The Secretary being absent from the City<span class='line-break'> </span>it was Voted, the <a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'>Geo. W. Bond</a> be chosen Secretary<span class='line-break'> </span>pro tempore. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Drafts account of Statuary '> Drafts account of Statuary </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> stated the object of the meeting to<span class='line-break'> </span>be to consider whether ^<sup>the payment of</sup> a certain draft made by <a href='/pages/subjects/52560' title='Rogers, Randolph'>Mr Rogers</a><span class='line-break'> </span>for the sum of $1500., and a draft or drafts proposed by<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53236' title='Crawford, Thomas'>Mr Crawford</a> for the sum of $2500, shall be provided for<span class='line-break'> </span>the terms of contract not having been strictly complied<span class='line-break'> </span>with. _</p>
<p>Letters from Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/52560' title='Rogers, Randolph'>Rogers</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/53236' title='Crawford, Thomas'>Crawford</a> were read<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; ordered to be placed on file. _</p>
<p>It was then Voted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Payment same ordered _'>Payment same ordered _</span></p>
<p>Whereas a draft drawn by <a href='/pages/subjects/52560' title='Rogers, Randolph'>R.<span class='line-break'> </span>Rogers</a> for the sum of $1500 has been presented and notice<span class='line-break'> </span>has been received from <a href='/pages/subjects/53236' title='Crawford, Thomas'>Thos. Crawford</a> of a draft or drafts for<span class='line-break'> </span>the sum of $2500. about to be drawn by him _</p>
<p>That <a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->the Treasurer</a> be authorized &amp; directed to pay<span class='line-break'> </span>the same upon the approval of the Committee upon Statuary.</p>
<p>The meeting was then dissolved</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'>Geo. W<sup>m.</sup> Bond</a> Secy pro tem.   <span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Mr Cheever</a>, chairman of the building committee<span class='line-break'> </span>of the <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>house for Superintendent</a>, having, at the special meeting<span class='line-break'> </span>on the 24<sup>th</sup> of June asked an increase of $500 to the appro- <span class='line-break'> </span>priation therefor, so that the sum limited may be $4,000<span class='line-break'> </span>instead of $3500 as before ordered, (see p. 77) and the <span class='line-break'> </span>same having thereupon been informally assented to, _ it was now</p>
<p>Voted that the appropriation for erecting the <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Super- <span class='line-break'> </span>intendent's house</a>, exclusive of the foundation, be increased <span class='line-break'> </span>from $3500 to $4000. ~</p>

<p>Voted that the petition be granted. _</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Secretary upon standing rules &amp; orders of Corpn &amp;  Trustees compiled by him _ '> Report of Secretary upon standing rules &amp; orders of Corp<sup>n</sup> &amp;  Trustees compiled by him _ </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->The Secretary</a> having been authorized, by a vote <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Trustees passed <date when='1855-09-04'>Sept<sup>r</sup> 4, 1855</date>, (p. 46) to make, <span class='line-break'> </span>for the purpose of convenient reference, a compilation of <span class='line-break'> </span>all standing rules &amp; orders passed by the Trustees &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>the Corporation.</p>
<p>Reported,, that he had first made a copy <span class='line-break'> </span>from the records, in the order of dates, of all ^<sup>such</sup> standing rules &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>orders as are believed to be still in force: and had next <span class='line-break'> </span>arranged the same under such titles or captions as seemed <span class='line-break'> </span>suitable to him, so as to present, at a glance, all rules &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>orders on any particular subject connected with the <span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation; and he submitted the same in both forms<span class='line-break'> </span>to the Trustees. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Rept acceptd '> Rep<sup>t</sup> accept<sup>d</sup> </span></p>
<p>Voted that the report be accepted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Referred to Comee of three _ '> Referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> of three _ </span></p>
<p>Voted that the same be referred to a Committee of three, <span class='line-break'> </span>consisting of <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> &amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Lot 2165 _ Defective construction of &amp;c - '> <a href='/pages/subjects/63974' title='Lot 2165'>Lot 2165</a> _ Defective construction of &amp;c - </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Mr Bangs</a> of the Committee upon lots stated that the <span class='line-break'> </span>stone work &amp;c connected with the lot of <a href='/pages/subjects/63975' title='Fisk, William'>Mr W<sup>m</sup> Fisk</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/63974' title='Lot 2165'>(No 2165)</a><span class='line-break'> </span>which was recently done by the Corporation, was in a condition <span class='line-break'> </span>to need thorough repairing. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Referred _ '> Referred _ </span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Petitn for small gate at N.W. corner of Mt. Auburn. '> Petit<sup>n</sup> for small gate at N.W. corner of Mt. Auburn. </span></p>
<p>A petition was presented signed by <a href='/pages/subjects/63983' title='Hickborn, Philip'>Philip Hick- <span class='line-break'> </span>born</a> &amp; twenty five others, that they might have leave to put <span class='line-break'> </span>in a small gate, at the end of the stockade fence, near <span class='line-break'> </span>the old elm, at the northwest corner of Mount Auburn,<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; that the key might be placed in the hands of the station <span class='line-break'> </span>agent of the <a href='/pages/subjects/57590' title='Fitchburg Railroad'>Fitchburg Railroad</a>, the privilege to be withdrawn <span class='line-break'> </span>whenever any rule of the Corporation shall be violated. - -</p>

<p>And it was unanimously <span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that it is inexpedient to <span class='line-break'> </span>grant the requst of the petitioners. -</p>

<p>These were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, &amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>, &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Chapel '> <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> </span></p>
<p>Voted that, in consequence of the delay which has oc- <span class='line-break'> </span>curred on the part of the contractors for the rebuilding<span class='line-break'> </span>of the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a>, the Trustees will employ some other party <span class='line-break'> </span>to complete the work at the expense of the present con- <span class='line-break'> </span>tractors, unless they shall immediately proceed with &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>finish it without delay. -</p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> send a copy of the foregoing <span class='line-break'> </span>vote to <a href='/pages/subjects/57485' title='Whitcher, Sheldon &amp; Co.'>Messrs Whicher &amp; Sheldon</a>, Contractors. -</p>

<div id="page-1279264">
<h3><a name="page-1279264">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 097)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>97</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Grounds _'> Grounds _</span></p>
<p>Voted,,  that the Superintendent be instructed under the <span class='line-break'> </span>direction of the Committee upon Grounds, to fill up the <span class='line-break'> </span>hollow on the Westerly side of the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> with gravel <span class='line-break'> </span>from the Easterly side of <a href='/pages/subjects/57664' title='Entrance Gateway'><!--entrance-->the gate</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Interment in Public Lots _ '> Interment in <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public Lots</a> _ </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a> called the attention of the Board to the mode <span class='line-break'> </span>of interment in the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>public lots</a> without any system by means <span class='line-break'> </span>of which the place of interment of any person could be identified.</p>
<p>Upon which it was<span class='line-break'> </span>Voted,, that <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a> be a Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>to report at a future meeting a plan to designate the <span class='line-break'> </span>places of interment upon the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>public lots</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Building at Gate inexpedient this year_ '> Building at Gate inexpedient this year_ </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>, in behalf of the Committee on Rules &amp; Regulations of <span class='line-break'> </span>interment &amp;c, to which, at the meeting in April, (p. 80) was committed <span class='line-break'> </span>the subject of considering what alterations or additions might be <span class='line-break'> </span>made to the buildings at the Gate, to be reported upon at a <span class='line-break'> </span>future meeting,, _ submitted a written report recommending <span class='line-break'> </span>the erection of a building for the accommodation of visitors so <span class='line-break'> </span>soon as the financial state of the Corporation shall allow it;<span class='line-break'> </span>but advising the postponement of the same to another year,<span class='line-break'> </span>on account of the large payments required to be made for the <span class='line-break'> </span><small><a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Superintendent's house</a>, Statuary &amp; other purposes, and that the <span class='line-break'> </span>subject for the present be laid upon the table _</small></p>
<p>Voted that the report be accepted &amp; placed on file. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Lots _ '> Lots _ </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, Chairman of the Committee upon lots, to which <span class='line-break'> </span>a communication from the Superintendent was referred at the May <span class='line-break'> </span>meeting (p. 90) asking information _ 1<sup>st</sup> What distance shall be <span class='line-break'> </span>left between lots in laying them out. _ 2<sup>d</sup> - Whether the refusal of <span class='line-break'> </span>a lot should be given to any one, &amp; for what time; _</p>

<p>98</p>
<p>and 3<sup>d</sup> that the Board would consider the expediency of of [sic]<span class='line-break'> </span>selling lots for tombs in certain locations &amp;c: _</p>
<p>Stated that the first &amp; second items of inquiry were within <span class='line-break'> </span>the province of the Committee upon Lots, &amp; he would <span class='line-break'> </span>submit no recommendation thereupon. _ In relation to <span class='line-break'> </span>the third item, he proposed the following vote, which <span class='line-break'> </span>was passed. __</p>

<h3><a name="page-1279266">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 099)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>99</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Septr 1. 1856.'>Trustees <date when='1856-09-01'>Sept<sup>r</sup> 1. 1856</date>.</span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees <span class='line-break'> </span>was held at the usual place on <date when='1856-09-01T10:00:00'>Monday the <span class='line-break'> </span>first day of September AD 1856, at 10 o'clock AM</date>.</p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> &amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>.</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Committee upon Public Lots _ recommends '> Report of Committee upon <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public Lots</a> _ recommends </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>, the Committee appointed at the last <span class='line-break'> </span>meeting, to report a plan by means of which the inter- <span class='line-break'> </span>ments in the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>public lots</a> may be property identified<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; recorded, submitted a written report which con- <span class='line-break'> </span>cluded with the following recommendations. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Recording past interments - '> Recording past interments - </span></p>
<p>"First _ That the whole matter be referred to a Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>with full powers _ 1<sup>st</sup> To have the lots put in order _<span class='line-break'> </span>the graves opened where necessary _ and a full and <span class='line-break'> </span>complete record made of all the interments which <span class='line-break'> </span>have been made therein. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' New fence _'> New fence _</span></p>
<p>2<sup>d</sup> to have the old fence <span class='line-break'> </span>on the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>S<sup>t</sup> James Lot</a>, which merely consists of small <span class='line-break'> </span>iron posts with a chain, removed, and stone posts <span class='line-break'> </span>substituted _ .</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' numbering of graves in order _ '> numbering of graves in order _ </span></p>
<p>3<sup>d</sup> to have stones with the numbers <span class='line-break'> </span>placed on each of the graves in the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>St James' Lot</a><span class='line-break'> </span>and those in the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>St. John's Lot</a> which have been <span class='line-break'> </span>sold without that condition. _"</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Charge for stone with number_ '> Charge for stone with number_ </span></p>
<p>"Secondly,,  That in future sales of graves in the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>public Lots</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>in addition to the price heretofore charged, that fifty</p>
</div>
</div>

<p>100</p>
<p>cents shall be added for a stone number, &amp; that <span class='line-break'> </span>none be sold without that condition. ~ ."</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='and book for recording such interments _'>and book for recording such interments _</span></p>
<p>"Thirdly,, That a separate book shall be kept for recording <span class='line-break'> </span>interments in the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>public lots</a>, said interments <span class='line-break'> </span>to be also fully described in the general Records." _</p>

<p>[ <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Mr Cheever</a> here left the meeting to attend another <span class='line-break'> </span>meeting at 11 o'clock.]</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' T. Dowse&apos;s application to purchase  strip of land _ '> <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>T. Dowse's</a> application to purchase  strip of land _ </span></p>
<p>A communication was presented to the meeting, of <span class='line-break'> </span>which the following is a copy. _</p>
<p>"<a href='/pages/subjects/53203' title='Cambridge, MA'>Cambridge</a> <date when='1856-09-01'>Sept. 1. 1856</date><span class='line-break'> </span>To the Board of Trustees of Mount Auburn Cemetery,<span class='line-break'> </span>Gentlemen,</p>
<p>I should like to purchase in behalf <span class='line-break'> </span>of <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Mr Thomas Dowse</a> the land between the lots of <span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/80045' title='Wetherell, John G.'>Wetherell</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/63999' title='Faulkner, Mr.'>Faulkner</a> - and leading from <a href='/pages/subjects/59585' title='Pine Avenue'>Pine <span class='line-break'> </span>Avenue</a> to lot of said Dowse.</p>
<p>Conditions of sale to be that said land shall <span class='line-break'> </span>be kept open as a Path forever.-<span class='line-break'> </span>Very Respectfully<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/64000' title='Watriss, O. W.'>O. W. Watriss</a>". _</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> suggested that the proposition in behalf of <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Mr Dowse</a> should be referred to the Standing Committee</p>

<p>101</p>
<p>on Lots, but this was rejected. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' T. Dowse&apos;s application granted _ Sale authorized. _'> <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>T. Dowse's</a> application granted _ Sale authorized. _</span></p>
<p>It was then Voted,, that this Corporation will<span class='line-break'> </span>sell said land to <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Mr Dowse</a> upon the condition that<span class='line-break'> </span>the same shall be kept open as a path forever, _<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> voting against the same. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Mr Curtis&apos; resignation as member of Comee on Lots โ '> <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>' resignation as member of Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots โ </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> here tendered his resignation as<span class='line-break'> </span>member of the Committee upon Lots.<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; it was Voted to accept the same. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Rules re-specting Admission _ '> Rules re-specting Admission _ </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a> stated that there seemed to be some<span class='line-break'> </span>conflict between the rule requiring visitors to Mt Auburn<span class='line-break'> </span>to exhibit a ticket of admission at the gate, &amp; the rule<span class='line-break'> </span>giving the Gate Keeper discretionary power to admit<span class='line-break'> </span>people _ that this power had been exercised to the incon- <span class='line-break'> </span>venience of persons who supposed that no ticket was nec- <span class='line-break'> </span>essary _</p>
<p>And he moved the reference of the whole subject<span class='line-break'> </span>of admission to the Cemetery to a Committee, upon<span class='line-break'> </span>which it was</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Referred to Committee '> Referred to Committee </span></p>
<p>Voted that the same be referred to a Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>consisting of Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>, to report upon at<span class='line-break'> </span>a future meeting. _</p>
<p>The meeting was then dissolved<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> Secretary.</p>

<p>The following is a copy of the deed conveying<span class='line-break'> </span>the land referred to upon the two preceding pages<span class='line-break'> </span>to <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Thomas Dowse</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Deed _ Proprietors to Thomas Dowse '> Deed _ Proprietors to <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Thomas Dowse</a> </span></p>
<p>"Know all men by these presents that the Pro- <span class='line-break'> </span>prietors of the Cemetery of Mount Auburn, by virtue<span class='line-break'> </span>of a vote of the Trustees of said Proprietors, passed at<span class='line-break'> </span>a regular meeting duly notified &amp; held in <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a><span class='line-break'> </span>on the <date when='1856-09-01'>first day of September A.D. 1856</date> and in consid- <span class='line-break'> </span>eration of the sum of forty dollars paid to them<span class='line-break'> </span>by <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Thomas Dowse</a> of <a href='/pages/subjects/53203' title='Cambridge, MA'>Cambridge</a>, the receipt whereof is<span class='line-break'> </span>hereby acknowledged, do hereby grant, bargain, sell &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span>convey to the said <a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Thomas Dowse</a> &amp; his heirs and<span class='line-break'> </span>assigns a certain piece of land in the Cemetery of<span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn, in the County of Middlesex, situated on<span class='line-break'> </span>the way called <a href='/pages/subjects/59585' title='Pine Avenue'>Pine Avenue</a>, between the <a href='/pages/subjects/64042' title='Lot 1169'>lots numbered<span class='line-break'> </span>eleven hundred &amp; sixty nine</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/64043' title='Lot 1170'>eleven hundred &amp; seventy</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>and extending from said <a href='/pages/subjects/59585' title='Pine Avenue'>Pine Avenue</a> to <a href='/pages/subjects/64044' title='Lot 1810'>lot numbered<span class='line-break'> </span>eighteen hundred &amp; ten</a>, recently conveyed by said Dowse<span class='line-break'> </span>to said Proprietors; _ said piece of land containing<span class='line-break'> </span>eighty superficial square feet. _</p>
<p>To have and to hold the same to the said<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62002' title='Dowse, Thomas'>Thomas Dowse</a> &amp; his heirs &amp; assigns forever, on the<span class='line-break'> </span>condition that said land shall be kept open as a <span class='line-break'> </span>Path forever. _</p>
<p>In witness whereof, the said Proprietors of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery of Mount Auburn, have caused this instrument<span class='line-break'> </span>to be signed by their Treasurer and countersigned by their<span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary and their Common seal to be hereto affixed the<span class='line-break'> </span><small><date when='1856-09-03'>third day of September A.D. eighteen hundred &amp; fifty six.</date> - " [Hand-drawn image of seal around letters "L.S."]<span class='line-break'> </span>Countersigned<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>, Secretary _ <a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'>Geo. W<sup>m</sup> Bond</a> Treas<sup>r</sup> </small><span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees October 6. 1856. '> Trustees<date when='1856-10-06'> October 6. 1856.</date> </span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>was held at the usual place on <date when='1856-10-06T10:00:00'>Monday October<span class='line-break'> </span>sixth, AD 1856 - at 10 o'clock A.M.</date> ~</p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, &amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>,<span class='line-break'> </span>Read &amp;</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. _</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report in part of Comee on Public Lots. '> Report in part of Com<sup>ee</sup> on <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public Lots</a>. </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>, the Committee chosen at the last meeting to cause<span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public Lots</a> to be put in proper order, made a report in part,<span class='line-break'> </span>verbally, stating the expenses that had been incurred, &amp; giving<span class='line-break'> </span>an estimate of the expense of putting an iron fence around<span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>St. James Lot</a>, &amp; asking authority to have such fence<span class='line-break'> </span>erected instead of the stone posts recommended by him<span class='line-break'> </span>at the last meeting. _</p>

<p>Voted that the Committee be authorized to have <span class='line-break'> </span>said fence erected &amp; to execute the other matters entrusted<span class='line-break'> </span>to his care in connection with said Lots. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Mr Cheever chosen to fill vacancy in Comee on Lots _ '> <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Mr Cheever</a> chosen to fill vacancy in Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots _ </span></p>

<div id="page-1279271">
<h3><a name="page-1279271">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 104)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>104</p>
<p>(<a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr Crocker</a> here joined the meeting)</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Commee chosen to considerrelations &amp; obligations of this Corpn to the Mass. Hort. Socy '> Comm<sup>ee</sup> chosen to considerrelations &amp; obligations of this Corp<sup>n</sup> to the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Mass. Hort. Soc<sup>y</sup></a> </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> stated that this Corporation is <span class='line-break'> </span>about to incur a considerable expense in fitting up <span class='line-break'> </span>unsaleable lots for the market, and suggested the <span class='line-break'> </span>desirableness of ascertaining the nature of its liability <span class='line-break'> </span>to the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Mass. Horticultural Society</a>, in such sales, under<span class='line-break'> </span>the Charter. _ and it was</p>
<p>Voted that a Committee of three,<span class='line-break'> </span>consisting of <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, &amp; Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>, be <span class='line-break'> </span>chosen to consider the relations and obligations of <span class='line-break'> </span>this Corporation to the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Mass. Hort. Society</a>, &amp; report thereon.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Planting trees on Westerly line _ '> Planting trees on Westerly line _ </span></p>
<p>Voted that the Committee on Grounds be <span class='line-break'> </span>requested to consider the expediency of planting trees <span class='line-break'> </span>on a part of the Westerly line of the Cemetery, with <span class='line-break'> </span>authority to cause the same to be done, if they think fit. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Lot 182. Representative of same des-ignated. '> <a href='/pages/subjects/64052' title='Lot 182'>Lot 182</a>. Representative of same des-ignated. </span></p>
<p>In accordance with the petition of the heirs at law <span class='line-break'> </span>of <a href='/pages/subjects/58348' title='Boyd, James'>James Boyd</a>, late proprietor of <a href='/pages/subjects/64052' title='Lot 182'>lot numbered 182</a><span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/64053' title='Boyd, James, Mrs.'>Mrs James Boyd</a> of <a href='/pages/subjects/54347' title='Roxbury, MA'>Roxbury</a> was designated <span class='line-break'> </span>to represent the same,  &amp; vote at meetings of the Corpo- <span class='line-break'> </span>ration, until another designation may become necessary.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Comee on Grounds to consider what space might to be preserved between adjoining lots - '> Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds to consider what space might to be preserved between adjoining lots - </span></p>
<p>Some remarks were made upon the need of uniform- <span class='line-break'> </span>ity in the spaces to be preserved between the lots of <span class='line-break'> </span>adjoining proprietors _ and it was</p>
<p>Voted to refer the consideration of the same <span class='line-break'> </span>to the Committee upon Grounds, to report upon at a <span class='line-break'> </span>future meeting. _</p>

<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a>, of the  Committee upon Statuary <span class='line-break'> </span>reported verbally, that two pedestals had been placed<span class='line-break'> </span>in the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'>Chapel</a> for statues, and that the <a href='/pages/subjects/56255' title='Joseph Story Statue'>statue of <span class='line-break'> </span>the late Mr Justice Story</a> had been removed from the <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54944' title='Boston Athenaeum'>Boston Atheneum</a> &amp; placed in the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Lot 859 _ Perpetl care. referred to Com. on Lots _ '> <a href='/pages/subjects/64058' title='Lot 859'>Lot 859</a> _ Perpet<sup>l</sup> care. referred to Com. on Lots _ </span></p>
<p>An application was presented for <a href='/pages/subjects/64059' title='Sumner, Jesse, Mrs.'>Mrs Sumner</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>widow of <a href='/pages/subjects/64060' title='Sumner, Jesse'>Jesse Sumner</a>, late proprietor of <a href='/pages/subjects/64058' title='Lot 859'>Lot 859</a> on <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/57829' title='Snowdrop Path'>Snowdrop Path</a>, inquiring on what terms the <span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation will assume perpetual care of said lot. _</p>

<p>The meeting was then dissolved. _</p>

<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->The Secretary</a>, in the absence of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, to whom <span class='line-break'> </span>was referred at the last meeting the question of correcting <span class='line-break'> </span>upon the Record of deeds, the erroneous numbering of the lots <span class='line-break'> </span>of <a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Messrs Little</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/58450' title='Brown, James'>Brown</a>, read the following preamble<span class='line-break'> </span>&amp; vote prepared by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>. _</p>
<p>"Whereas a lot containing six hundred feet numbered <span class='line-break'> </span>on the Plan of the Cemetery 1126 was granted to the late <a href='/pages/subjects/58450' title='Brown, James'>James <span class='line-break'> </span>Brown</a>, and a deed dated <date when='1844-10-12'>October 12. 1844</date> was issued to <span class='line-break'> </span>him, but said deed was ^ <sup>by mistake</sup> numbered and recorded 1127 :_</p>
<p>And whereas a lot containing the same quantity of land <span class='line-break'> </span>numbered on the plan 1127 was granted to <a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Charles C. Little</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>and a deed of the aforesaid date was issued to him, but <span class='line-break'> </span>was by mistake numbered and recorded 1126: and <span class='line-break'> </span>whereas on the ninth of June 1852 a deed of 211 feet of <span class='line-break'> </span>land was issued to <a href='/pages/subjects/58450' title='Brown, James'>James Brown</a> as an addition to his <span class='line-break'> </span>lot number 1126, and was recorded as such: _ and <span class='line-break'> </span>whereas it is desirable that the said errors should <span class='line-break'> </span>be corrected, _ it is hereby ordered that the said lot of <span class='line-break'> </span>land granted to <a href='/pages/subjects/58450' title='Brown, James'>James Brown</a> shall be deemed and <span class='line-break'> </span>taken to be No 1126, and the lot of land granted to <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Charles C. Little</a> shall be deemed and taken to be _</p>

<div id="page-1279277">
<h3><a name="page-1279277">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 110)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>110</p>
<p>form. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lots โ Spaces between. '>Lots โ Spaces between. </span></p>
<p>"That, in all future sales of lots, a space of not <span class='line-break'> </span>less than three nor more than six feet feet in width,<span class='line-break'> </span>at the discretion of the Committee on Lots, shall be <span class='line-break'> </span>reserved between the fence limits of different lots,<span class='line-break'> </span>unless otherwise ordered by a vote of the Trustees.</p>
<p>That the land left vacant as intermediate space<span class='line-break'> </span>between lots in Mount Auburn, and not exceeding ten feet <span class='line-break'> </span>in width between any two lots, may be sold to the nearest <span class='line-break'> </span>lot  holder or holders, at one third of the selling prices <span class='line-break'> </span>per foot at the time of said sale, with the condition that <span class='line-break'> </span>said land shall forever be kept open and without inter- <span class='line-break'> </span>ments:  provided that if the Committee on lots deem <span class='line-break'> </span>it inexpedient in any special case to make such sale, <span class='line-break'> </span>the question may be submitted to the Board of <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees." _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Receiving Tomb _ Old discontind '> <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tomb</a> _ Old discontin<sup>d</sup> </span></p>
<p>The Committee also recommended the following with <span class='line-break'> </span>respect to the <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving tombs</a>. _</p>
<p>"That the old <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tomb</a> be discontinued, and <span class='line-break'> </span>that the lot be prepared for sale: _ and that hereafter <span class='line-break'> </span>no body be allowed to remain in the new <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tomb</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>longer than four months. " _</p>
<p>Voted that the same be adopted. _</p>

<p>Voted that the consideration of the same be postponed to an <span class='line-break'> </span>adjourned meeting. _ </p>

<p>A meeting of the Trustees was held according to the <span class='line-break'> </span>adjournment at the usual place on <date when='1826-12-04T18:00:00'>Thursday, Decem- <span class='line-break'> </span>ber  4<sup>th</sup> at 6 O'clock P. M.</date> ~</p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Eldredge, O. &amp; E. H. _ Lots 2657, 2658 _ Special deeds authorized to preserve a passage-way '> <a href='/pages/subjects/64062' title='Eldredge, Oliver'>Eldredge, O.</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/64222' title='Eldredge, Edward H.'>&amp; E. H.</a> _ <a href='/pages/subjects/64223' title='Lot 2657'>Lots 2657</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/64224' title='Lot 2658'><!--lot-->2658</a> _ Special deeds authorized to preserve a passage-way </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/64062' title='Eldredge, Oliver'>Mr Oliver Eldredge</a> having purchased <a href='/pages/subjects/64223' title='Lot 2657'>lot <span class='line-break'> </span>N<sup>o</sup> 2657</a> at the corner of <a href='/pages/subjects/61130' title='Bellwort Path'>Bellwort Path</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/59904' title='Spruce Avenue'>Spruce Avenue</a>, and <a href='/pages/subjects/64222' title='Eldredge, Edward H.'>Edward H. Eldredge</a> having pur- <span class='line-break'> </span>chased the adjoining <a href='/pages/subjects/64224' title='Lot 2658'>lot N<sup>o</sup> 2658</a> at the corner of <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/60005' title='Pyrola Path'>Pyrola Path</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/59904' title='Spruce Avenue'>Spruce Avenue</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that a passage-way of six feet in width <span class='line-break'> </span>in the rear of said lots be forever kept open and free<span class='line-break'> </span>from interments, and that a covenant to that effect <span class='line-break'> </span>be inserted in each of the deeds to the Grantees. _</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees - Adjourned Meeting _ Decemr 9. 1856. '> Trustees - Adjourned Meeting _ <date when='1856-12-09'>Decem<sup>r</sup> 9. 1856</date>. </span></p>
<p>A meeting of the Trustees was held according <span class='line-break'> </span>to the adjournment, at the usual place on <date when='1856-12-09T18:00:00'>Tuesday <span class='line-break'> </span>Evening December 9<sup>th</sup> at 6 O'clock</date>. -</p>
<p>There were present Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Chairman pro tem _ '> Chairman pro tem _ </span></p>
<p>The President being absent <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr. Nazro</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span>chosen Chairman pro tem. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Bye Laws - Report of Comee taken up _ amends &amp; adopted in articles _ '> Bye Laws - Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> taken up _ amend<sup>s</sup> &amp; adopted in articles _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Postponed _ '> Postponed _ </span></p>
<p>The report of the Committee on Bye Laws was <span class='line-break'> </span>taken up where it was left at the last meeting, read and <span class='line-break'> </span>considered article by article, _ several amendments were <span class='line-break'> </span>incorporated into the same, and they were severally passed<span class='line-break'> </span>as far as the article on "Alterations of Bye Laws", &amp; were <span class='line-break'> </span>ordered to be numbered; _ and the further consideration of <span class='line-break'> </span>the report was postponed to the adjourned meeting. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Adjournt _ '> Adjourn<sup>t</sup> _ </span></p>
