<div id="page-1279324">
<h3><a name="page-1279324">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 157)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>157</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Expenditures limited _'>Expenditures limited _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/72375' title='Hallett, Benjamin F.'>B. F. Hallett Esq.</a> then offered the following resolution <span class='line-break'> </span>That hereafter no expenditure exceeding the sum of <span class='line-break'> </span>one hundred dollars shall be ordered or authorized, <span class='line-break'> </span>unless the same shall be voted by a majority of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Board of Trustees.</p>
<p>Pending this <a href='/pages/subjects/60695' title='Brigham, William'>W<sup>m</sup> Brigham Esq.</a> offered <span class='line-break'> </span>the following as an amendment to the same: _</p>
<p>"That the Proprietors recommend that the <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees adopt a By-Law for the action of the Board <span class='line-break'> </span>that no money beyond the sum of one hundred <span class='line-break'> </span>dollars in any on instance be appropriated without <span class='line-break'> </span>the consent of a majority of the whole Board."</p>
<p>After the discussion of the same by Messrs <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/72375' title='Hallett, Benjamin F.'>Hallett</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/60695' title='Brigham, William'>Brigham</a>. <a href='/pages/subjects/64700' title='Wightman, J. M.'>J. M. Wightman</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>C. P. Curtis</a>, the <span class='line-break'> </span>amendment, by common consent, was withdrawn. _</p>
<p>The original resolution was thus put and adopted.</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/72014' title='Hawes, Prince'>Mr Prince Hawes</a> then submitted the following <span class='line-break'> </span>resolution _</p>
<p>"That the Trustees shall not be allowed to <span class='line-break'> </span>expend more than three thousand dollars for any one <span class='line-break'> </span>object until the consent of the Proprietors shall have <span class='line-break'> </span>been given at a meeting legally called for that purpose."</p>
<p>It being suggested that the motion in this <span class='line-break'> </span>form applied to the ordinary expenses for the care of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery as well as to other objects, the same was withdrawn.</p>
<p>The meeting then adjourned without day.<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> Secretary.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />

<p>159</p>
<p>I have this day Examined the books and<span class='line-break'> </span>accounts of the Treasurer of Mount Auburn <span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery for the year ending <date when='1856-12-31'>Dec<sup>r</sup> 31<sup>rd</sup> 1856.</date><span class='line-break'> </span>and have found them correctly kept and properly <span class='line-break'> </span>balanced, with satisfactory vouchers for all<span class='line-break'> </span>payments charged. _</p>
<p>The certificates of stock and ^<sup>other,</sup> evidences of <span class='line-break'> </span>property were found in accordance with the<span class='line-break'> </span>statements in his account. _ In the fund for <span class='line-break'> </span>repairs there appeared to be on hand sixteen<span class='line-break'> </span>hundred &amp; fifty nine 68/100 dollars ($1.659.68) and <span class='line-break'> </span>to be due the Treasurer in the general account<span class='line-break'> </span>seven hundred &amp; ninety three &amp; 75/100 dollars, as per <span class='line-break'> </span>balance in this book.</p>

<p>The current expenses at the Cemetery <span class='line-break'> </span>have been reduced during the past year, as<span class='line-break'> </span>will be seen by the ^<sup>report of the</sup> Superintendant to be less than<span class='line-break'> </span>$4.000</p>

<div id="page-1279331">
<h3><a name="page-1279331">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 164)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>164</p>
<p>Trustees Records 1857.-8 ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Feby 9. 1857'>Trustees <date when='1857-02-19'>Feb<sup>y</sup> 9. 1857</date></span></p>
<p>In accordance with notification duly issued con<span class='line-break'></span>formably to the By-Law requiring the first meeting of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees to be held within two weeks after the <span class='line-break'> </span>Annual Meeting of the Corporation, the Trustees <span class='line-break'> </span>met at the office of the Secretary on <date when='1857-02-09T10:00:00'>Monday <span class='line-break'> </span>February ninth, AD 1857. at 10 o'clock A. M.</date>  _</p>
<p>There were present _</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>, Read &amp;</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Dr Lawrence&apos;s qualified resignation'><a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Dr Lawrence</a>'s qualified resignation</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Dr Lawrence</a> stated that he was elected last year <span class='line-break'> </span>without being consulted. _ that he reluctantly accepted the<span class='line-break'> </span>office for one year, _ that he had supposed that he had <span class='line-break'> </span>verbally communicated to the Secretary his declination to be <span class='line-break'> </span>reelected for the present year, but by some misunderstanding <span class='line-break'> </span>the fact was not made public until too late, &amp; that he <span class='line-break'> </span>had consequently been reelected contrary to his wishes: _<span class='line-break'> </span>that, as the Trustees had no power to fill vacancies, <span class='line-break'> </span>he did not desire to embarrass the action of the Trustees <span class='line-break'> </span>by an immediate and absolute withdrawal, if his with<span class='line-break'></span>drawal might occasion such embarrassment: _ he would <span class='line-break'> </span>therefore tender his resignation to take effect at such time <span class='line-break'> </span>as the Trustees should see fit to act thereon. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Election of Officers &amp;c'>Election of Officers &amp;c</span></p>
<p>The Chairman announced the first business ^<sup>in</sup> order <span class='line-break'> </span>to be the choice of Officers and Committees, and also <span class='line-break'> </span>to fix the salary or compensation of officers for the ensuing <span class='line-break'> </span>year. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />

<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a> was requested to collect, assort &amp; count <span class='line-break'> </span>the votes for the respective officers, and Committees which <span class='line-break'> </span>are required by the By Laws to be chosen by ballot.</p>
<p>Pending which it was. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Salary &amp;c of Secretary &amp; Treasurer'>Salary &amp;c of Secretary &amp; Treasurer</span></p>

<div class="page-content">
<p>166</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on Reg. &amp; Records of Interment'>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Reg. &amp; Records of Interment</span></p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>Messrs</th> <th><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a></th> <th>} for Committee on Regulations<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a></td> <td>} and Records of Interments _</td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Compensation of Superintendent'>Compensation of Superintendent</span></p>
<p>Voted that the compensation of the Superintendent <span class='line-break'> </span>be the same as on the last year - viz a salary of <span class='line-break'> </span>one thousand dollars, and the use of a house<span class='line-break'> </span>with no perquisites. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Choice of Supt'>Choice of Sup<sup>t</sup></span></p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Jonathan Mann</a> be chosen <span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent for the year ensuing. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Adjourned Meeting'>Adjourned Meeting</span></p>
<p>Voted that when this meeting adjourn it be <span class='line-break'> </span>to the first Monday of March next. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Compensation &amp; Choice of Gate Keeper &amp;c postponed _'>Compensation &amp; Choice of Gate Keeper &amp;c postponed _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the subject of compensation of Super<span class='line-break'></span>indent's Clerk and Gate Keeper, also the choice <span class='line-break'> </span>of a persons to fill those offices respectivly be postponed<span class='line-break'> </span>until the adjourned meeting. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on Statuary'>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Statuary</span></p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> be a Committee in relation <span class='line-break'> </span>to the outstanding contracts for Statuary, for the present<span class='line-break'> </span>year. _</p>
<p>Voted that all special unfinished matters be recom<span class='line-break'></span>mitted, as follows: _</p>

<div id="page-1279335">
<h3><a name="page-1279335">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 168)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>168</p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a> _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Supt to visit other Cemeteries'>Sup<sup>t</sup> to visit other Cemeteries</span></p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'><!--Mann-->the Superintendent</a> be authorized to <span class='line-break'> </span>visit. <a href='/pages/subjects/64140' title='New York, NY'>New York</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/64806' title='Philadelphia, PA'>Philadelphia</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/64807' title='Baltimore, MD'>Baltimore</a> for the <span class='line-break'> </span>purpose of acquiring information useful to the Cemetery.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Amendt to By-Laws proposed _'>Amend<sup>t</sup> to By-Laws proposed _</span></p>
<p>The following amendments &amp; additions to the By<span class='line-break'></span>Laws were proposed, which under the rule lie over <span class='line-break'> </span>until the adjourned meeting. _</p>
<p>By <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>.</p>
<p>That the last Article in "Alterations of By<span class='line-break'></span>Laws" shall be amended so as to read _</p>
<p>"That no alteration <u>nor</u> <u>addition</u> shall be made<span class='line-break'> </span>to any of the By-Laws unless the proposed alteration or <span class='line-break'> </span>addition ^<sup>shall</sup> have been submitted to the Trustees at a meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>at least seven days previous to the meeting at which <span class='line-break'> </span>it is to be acted upon".  _</p>
<p>The following to be added to the By-Laws _</p>
<p>"That no vote of the Trustees shall be valid (except <span class='line-break'> </span>a vote to adjourn to a day certain, or without day,)<span class='line-break'> </span>unless the same be adopted at a stated meeting, or <span class='line-break'> </span>at a special meeting duly called, by not less than <span class='line-break'> </span>five members of the Board _  which fact shall <span class='line-break'> </span>be recorded by the Secretary." _</p>
<p>The following by <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a></p>
<p>"That no Trustee shall receive any salary, contract,<span class='line-break'> </span>or other emolument for servies rendered by him, while <span class='line-break'> </span>holding the office of Trustee." ~</p>
<p>The meeting ws then adjourned as above ordered <span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>,, Secretary.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-1279336">
<h3><a name="page-1279336">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 169)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>169</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Secretary&apos;s Oath of Office'>Secretary's Oath of Office</span></p>
<p>Commonwealth of Massachusetts<span class='line-break'> </span>Suffolk ss. <date when='1857-02-09'>February 9<sup>th</sup>. 1857</date>. Then personally <span class='line-break'> </span>appeared <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> and made oath <span class='line-break'> </span>that he would faithfully perform the duties of <span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary of the Proprietors of the Cemetery of Mount <span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn for the ensuing year: _</p>
<p>Before me <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>C.P. Curtis</a> _ Justice of the Peace</p>
<p>-------------------</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees March 2d 1857. _'>Trustees <date when='1857-03-02'>March 2<sup>d</sup> 1857</date>. _</span></p>
<p>An adjourned meeting of the Trustees was held <span class='line-break'> </span>at the usual place on<date when='1857-03-02T10:00:00'> Monday March 2<sup>d</sup>, 1857, <span class='line-break'> </span>at 10 o'clock a.m.</date> (the same being also the time <span class='line-break'> </span>for the regular monthly meeting.)</p>
<p>There were present <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messes <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>McKean</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>, <span class='line-break'> </span>Read and</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a>. ~</p>
<p>The Record of the Last meeting was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Amendments to By-Laws. Adopted'>Amendments to By-Laws. Adopted</span></p>
<p>The amendments proposed at the last meeting to be made <span class='line-break'> </span>to the By-Laws were then taken up: and the following <span class='line-break'> </span>proposed by Mr. Read, was unanimously adopted, and <span class='line-break'> </span>ordered to be incorporated in its place with the By-Laws <span class='line-break'> </span>recently adopted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Amendt to Art.  3d'>Amend<sup>t</sup> to Art.  3<sup>d</sup></span></p>
<p>"No Trustee shall receive any Salary, contract, <span class='line-break'> </span>or other emolument for services rendered by him, <span class='line-break'> </span>while holding the office of Trustee." _</p>

<div id="page-1279337">
<h3><a name="page-1279337">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 170)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>170</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Amendment to Art. 29 _'>Amendment to Art. 29 _</span></p>
<p>The amendment to the last By-Law, on "Alter<span class='line-break'></span>ation", proposed last month was, at the same time, <span class='line-break'> </span>adopted. _  The By Law is now as follows. _</p>
<p>"No alteration nor addition shall be made <span class='line-break'> </span>to any of the By Laws, unless the proposed alteration <span class='line-break'> </span>or addition shall have been submitted to the <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees at a meeting at least seven days pre<span class='line-break'></span>vious to the meeting at which it is to be acted <span class='line-break'> </span>upon." _</p>
<p>The clause respecting the number of Trustees <span class='line-break'> </span>who must vote for a measure to make it valid, sub<span class='line-break'></span>mitted by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, at the last meeting as an <span class='line-break'> </span>addition to the By Laws, (see p. 168.) was discussed <span class='line-break'> </span>and withdrawn, for another to be presented by <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the <span class='line-break'> </span>President</a> in the following words, which under <span class='line-break'> </span>the new rule lies over till the next meeting. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Addition to By Laws proposed'>Addition to By Laws proposed</span></p>
<p>"No order of the Board, except to adjourn, <span class='line-break'> </span>shall be valid, unless it has received the <span class='line-break'> </span>votes of at least five Trustees." _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Addition to By Laws proposed.'>Addition to By Laws proposed.</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> also submitted the following as an <span class='line-break'> </span>additon to the By Laws, which also lies over. ~</p>
<p>"The President shall call a special <span class='line-break'> </span>meeting of the Board, whenever requested in writing <span class='line-break'> </span>so to do by five Trustees." _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Amendt to Art 16th on Lots &amp; Spaces proposed'>Amend<sup>t</sup> to Art 16<sup>th</sup> on Lots &amp; Spaces proposed</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> submitted a new draft of Art. 16. <span class='line-break'> </span>of the By Laws, on "Lots and Spaces", as a substitute therefor, <span class='line-break'> </span>which was read, and it was Voted that the same <span class='line-break'> </span>be referred to <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a>. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279338">
<h3><a name="page-1279338">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 171)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>171</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Gate Keeper _'>Gate Keeper _</span></p>
<p>The choice of a Gate Keeper, and Superinten<span class='line-break'></span>dent's Clerk, and the determination of the compensation <span class='line-break'> </span>for the duties of the respective offices for the year ensuing, <span class='line-break'> </span>which were postponed to this meeting, next came up <span class='line-break'> </span>for consideration.</p>
<p>A motion was made that a Committee of <span class='line-break'> </span>three Trustees be appointed to inquire into any charges<span class='line-break'> </span>or complaints made against the present Gate Keeper,<span class='line-break'> </span>and report thereon at an adjourned meeting: _</p>
<p>And the same being put was decided in the negative.</p>
<p>It was then moved to postpone action on the same <span class='line-break'> </span>to an adjourned meeting. _</p>
<p>And the motion was put, but not carried.</p>
<p>It was then Voted to proceed to choose a Gate Keeper and <span class='line-break'> </span>Clerk. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Safford, T. H.'><a href='/pages/subjects/52579' title='Safford, Truman H.'>Safford, T. H.</a></span></p>
<p>It was accordingly moved that <a href='/pages/subjects/52579' title='Safford, Truman H.'>Mr Truman H.<span class='line-break'> </span>Safford</a> of <a href='/pages/subjects/53204' title='Watertown, MA'>Watertown</a> be chosen to those offices, to perform <span class='line-break'> </span>the duties thereof during the pleasure of the Trustees. _</p>
<p>Pending this, testimonials in favor of <a href='/pages/subjects/52579' title='Safford, Truman H.'>Mr Safford</a> were <span class='line-break'> </span>presented and read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Chosen Gate Keeper'>Chosen Gate Keeper</span></p>
<p>The motion was put &amp; adopted, and <a href='/pages/subjects/52579' title='Safford, Truman H.'>Mr Safford</a><span class='line-break'> </span>was declared chosen Gate Keeper &amp; Clerk according to the tenor <span class='line-break'> </span>of said motion. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Salary _ of $450. _'>Salary _ of $450. _</span></p>
<p>It was then Voted that the compensation for the duties <span class='line-break'> </span>of said offices combined, be at the rate of four hundred and <span class='line-break'> </span>fifty dollars per annum, for all services rendered. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279339">
<h3><a name="page-1279339">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 172)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>172</p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Public Lots_'><a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public Lots</a>_</span></p>
<p>Voted that the unfinished business in connec<span class='line-break'></span>tion with the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public Lots</a>, referred last year to <span class='line-break'> </span>a special Committee, be referred to the Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>on Lots. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Disputed bills of Supt referred to Comee on Lots'>Disputed bills of Sup<sup>t</sup> referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots</span></p>
<p>The following communication was received from the <span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent: _</p>
<p>"To the Board of Trustees of Mt Auburn Cemetery,</p>
<p>Gentlemen,</p>
<p>There having been some complaints <span class='line-break'> </span>by Proprietors of exorbitant charges, by the Superintendent, <span class='line-break'> </span>for service rendered.</p>
<p>Therefore if compatible, I would ask, <span class='line-break'> </span>that a Committee be appointed to whom all bills<span class='line-break'> </span>supposed to be excessive shall be referred. _</p>
<p>Very Respectfully submitted<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Jon<sup>a</sup>. Mann</a> Sup<sup>t</sup>"</p>
<p>And therefore it was</p>
<p>Voted that, hereafter, all bills presented <span class='line-break'> </span>by the Superintendent to Proprietors which may be deemed <span class='line-break'> </span>exorbitant by them shall be referred to the Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee on Lots.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Representatives of Lots'>Representatives of Lots</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->The Secretary</a> presented the written petition of sundry <span class='line-break'> </span>parties for the appointment of representatives to their respective <span class='line-break'> </span>lots. _</p>
<p>And it was ordered that the persons therein<span class='line-break'> </span>severally designated be appointed to represent the lots<span class='line-break'> </span>hereinafter mentioned in connection with their respective names.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees April 6. 1857'>Trustees <date when='1857-04-06'>April 6. 1857</date></span></p>

<p>There were presents, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. <div id="page-1279341">
<h3><a name="page-1279341">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 174)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>174</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Amendt to Bye Laws _ '>Amend<sup>t</sup> to Bye Laws _ </span></p>
<p>The following  proposed at the last meeting as <span class='line-break'> </span>an addition to the Bye Laws first came up for con<span class='line-break'></span>sideration: viz.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Order must receive five Trustees&apos; Votes _ '>Order must receive five Trustees' Votes _ </span></p>
<p>"No order of the Board, except to adjourn<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be valid, unless it has received the votes of at <span class='line-break'> </span>least five Trustees. " _</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>Mr. M<sup>c</sup>Kean</a> moved to substitute the word "four" <span class='line-break'> </span>instead of "five" before the word "Trustees." _</p>
<p>And the motion was not carried.</p>
<p>The question then recurred upon adopting the orig<span class='line-break'></span>inal proposition, and the same was adopted in the <span class='line-break'> </span>words above expressed. _</p>
<p>Another proposed addition to the By Laws sub<span class='line-break'></span>mitted at the last meeting next came up. viz: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Special Meetings of Trustees how ^to be called _'>Special Meetings of Trustees how ^<sup>to be</sup> called _</span></p>
<p>"The President shall call a special meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Board, whenever requested in writing so <span class='line-break'> </span>to do by five Trustees." _</p>
<p>The question was put, &amp; the same was adopted unan<span class='line-break'></span>imously. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Spaces between Lots _'>Spaces between Lots _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> for the Committee, to whom at the last meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>was referred a new draft proposed ^<sup>by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>,</sup> as a substitute for the<span class='line-break'> </span>16<sup>th</sup> Article of the By-Laws, upon "Lots and Spaces" _ reported <span class='line-break'> </span>still another draft, which varied somewhat from that originally <span class='line-break'> </span>adopted; _ and after some discussion it was</p>
<p>Voted that the whole subject be recommitted <span class='line-break'> </span>to the same Committee, and that <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> be<span class='line-break'> </span>added, and that the Committee be requested</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Permanent Fund - Rept of Comee on _'>Permanent Fund - Rep<sup>t</sup> of Com<sup>ee</sup> on _</span></p>
<p>//<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr. Curtis</a> of the Committee appointed in Febru<span class='line-break'></span>ary to consider and report upon a plan for securing <span class='line-break'> </span>the preservation and continuance of the fund which <span class='line-break'> </span>has been ordered to be established for the perpetual care <span class='line-break'> </span>and preservation of the Cemetery and its appurtenances; <span class='line-break'> </span>and also to report such regulations for the investment<span class='line-break'> </span>and use of the said fund, as they may deem expedient, _<span class='line-break'> </span>submitted a written report, of which a copy is hereto<span class='line-break'> </span>appended. ~</p>

<div id="page-1279343">
<h3><a name="page-1279343">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 176)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>176</p>
<p>Report on the Permanent Fund</p>
<p>//<span class='line-break'> </span>"The undersigned, the majority of the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>appointed to report a plan for insuring the preservation <span class='line-break'> </span>and continuance of the accumulating fund, _ have <span class='line-break'> </span>considered the subject, and ask leave to report: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Permanent Fund Report'>Permanent Fund Report</span></p>
<p>That they find that the establishment of the <span class='line-break'> </span>said Fund is an act generally received with favor <span class='line-break'> </span>by the Proprietors whom they have conferred with; and <span class='line-break'> </span>they have no doubt it will be universally approved, <span class='line-break'> </span>when it is known that by it, the future  prosperity of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Cemetery will be secured. _ With a view to this <span class='line-break'> </span>end, your Committee have taken into consideration the <span class='line-break'> </span>means of securing the <u>perpetual</u> <u>preservation</u> of this safety<span class='line-break'> </span>fund; and, after consulting some of the most sagacious <span class='line-break'> </span>proprietors, they have come to the conclusion to recommend<span class='line-break'> </span>the adoption of an order by the Trustees, that in all <span class='line-break'> </span>the deeds of lots which shall hereafter be issued, there <span class='line-break'> </span>be inserted a covenant, that this fund shall be in<span class='line-break'></span>creased by yearly additions and by the accumulation of <span class='line-break'> </span>the interest, until it reaches the sum of one hundred <span class='line-break'> </span>and fifty thousand dollars; _  when the interest, and <span class='line-break'> </span>that alone, may be applied, if the wants of the Corpo<span class='line-break'></span>ration require it, to the payment of the expenses of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery.  If the Trustees in office at that time shall <span class='line-break'> </span>not need the income of this fund for expenses, they can <span class='line-break'> </span>if they see fit, permit it to accumulate still longer. _</p>
<p>In order to carry this design into effect, it will be ex<span class='line-break'></span>pedient to amend the proposition adopted <date when='1857-01-05'>January 5<sup>th</sup></date>,</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279344">
<h3><a name="page-1279344">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 177)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>177</p>
<p>1857,  by providing that, instead of placing the income <span class='line-break'> </span>at the disposal of the officers at the end of <u>twenty</u><span class='line-break'> </span>years, it shall not be made use of, until the accumu<span class='line-break'></span>lated capital shall amount to the sum before men<span class='line-break'></span>tioned, namely, one hundred and fifty thousand<span class='line-break'> </span>dollars. _</p>
<p>With these views your Committee recommend the<span class='line-break'> </span>passage of the following orders. _<span class='line-break'> </span>\\<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th> Signed</th> <th>{ <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Charles P. Curtis</a> <span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td> ___</td> <td>{ <a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Charles C. Little</a></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Permanent Fund - Mode of Accumulation _'>Permanent Fund - Mode of Accumulation _</span></p>
<p>//<span class='line-break'> </span><u>It</u> <u>is</u> <u>Ordered</u> - by the Trustees of the Cemetery of<span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn, that in the month of December of each <span class='line-break'> </span>year, the Treasurer of the Proprietors of the Cemetery of <span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn shall deposit with the <a href='/pages/subjects/64235' title='Massachusetts Hospital Life Insurance Company'>Massachusetts Hos<span class='line-break'></span>pital Life Insurance Company</a>, if they will receive it on <span class='line-break'> </span>as favorable conditions as other deposits, in trust for the <span class='line-break'> </span>said Proprietors, a sum equal to one <u>fifth</u> part of the gross<span class='line-break'> </span>proceeds of the lots and parts of lots, and intermediate <span class='line-break'> </span>spaces between lots, which shall have been sold subsequently <span class='line-break'> </span>to the first December in the year preceding; the interest of <span class='line-break'> </span>which sums shall annually, or oftener, be added to the <span class='line-break'> </span>capital for the purpose and upon the principles of accu<span class='line-break'></span>mulation; until the whole of said deposits, with the <span class='line-break'> </span>accumulated interest, shall amount to one hundred and fifty <span class='line-break'> </span>thousand dollars. _</p>
<p>And when the said fund shall have amounted <span class='line-break'> </span>to the sum of one hundred and fifty thousand dollars, <span class='line-break'> </span>it shall be lawful for the Trustees, if they see fit,</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279345">
<h3><a name="page-1279345">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 178)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>178</p>
<p>to withdraw the income thereof, and appropriate the <span class='line-break'> </span>same to the care, preservation, and keeping in order <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Cemetery and its appurtenances, to the payment of <span class='line-break'> </span>the salaries, and to the other necessary expenses of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Institution:  And by vote of <u>four</u> <u>fifths</u> of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>for the time being, they may withdraw from time to time, <span class='line-break'> </span>the principal of the said fund, and invest the same <span class='line-break'> </span>as _____ hereinafter is prescribed.</p>
<p>If at any time the Trustees ^<sup>deem</sup> the <a href='/pages/subjects/64235' title='Massachusetts Hospital Life Insurance Company'>Massachusetts<span class='line-break'> </span>Hospital Life Insurance Company,</a> to be an <u>unsafe</u><span class='line-break'> </span><u>place</u> <u>of</u> <u>deposit</u> of the said fund, and shall by a <span class='line-break'> </span>vote of a majority of all the members of the board so <span class='line-break'> </span>declare of record, the said fund may be withdrawn <span class='line-break'> </span>from the custody of the said Insurance Company, as soon <span class='line-break'> </span>as by the conditions of the deposit it may be, and shall <span class='line-break'> </span>then be invested in the name of the Proprietors of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery of Mount Auburn, upon the same trusts, in the <span class='line-break'> </span>Public Debt of the United States, or in that of the State <span class='line-break'> </span>of Massachusetts, or in the debt of the <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>City of Boston</a>, or <span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/54284' title='Charlestown, MA'>City of Charlestown</a>, or the <a href='/pages/subjects/54347' title='Roxbury, MA'>City of Roxbury</a>, or the <a href='/pages/subjects/53203' title='Cambridge, MA'>City <span class='line-break'> </span>of Cambridge</a>, or in mortgages of real estate in <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a>;<span class='line-break'> </span>provided that no mortgage shall be taken for a sum <span class='line-break'> </span>exceding two thirds of the value of the estate as it stands, <span class='line-break'> </span>when taken, on the valuation books of the assessors<span class='line-break'> </span>of the city taxes; nor for a period exceeding five years; <span class='line-break'> </span>nor, in which the interest shall not be paid as often <span class='line-break'> </span>as annually; to which shall be added, insurance <span class='line-break'> </span>against fire by some competent insurance Company<span class='line-break'> </span>in <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a>, for the amount of the loan, or such pro<span class='line-break'></span>portion thereof as the value of the buildings on the land</p>

<h3><a name="page-1279346">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 179)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>179</p>
<p>shall enable the  owner to obtain; which insurance<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be renewed from time to time at the expense<span class='line-break'> </span>of the mortgagor, and his assigns, and shall be payable, <span class='line-break'> </span>in case of loss, to the Trustees of the Cemetery of Mount <span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn. _</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Adjo Meeting _ April 13, 1857.'>Trustees Adj<sup>o</sup> Meeting _ <date when='1857-04-03'>April 13, 1857</date>.</span></p>
<p>A meeting of the Trustees was held <span class='line-break'> </span>according to adjournment on Monday <span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1857-04-13T10:00:00'>April 13<sup>th</sup> 1857 at 10 o'clock a.m</date>. ~</p>
<p>There were present <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a> _  seven. ~</p>
<p>The reading of the records was dispursed <span class='line-break'> </span>with.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lots and Spaces - Rept of Comee not adopted.'>Lots and Spaces - Rep<sup>t</sup> of Com<sup>ee</sup> not adopted.</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> for the Committee to consider what amend<span class='line-break'></span>ment, alteration or addition ought to be made to Art. <span class='line-break'> </span>16 of the By Laws, entitled "Lots and Spaces", submitted a<span class='line-break'> </span>draft containing additions and alterations of the Article <span class='line-break'> </span>as originally adopted, unanimously agreed to by the committee.</p>
<p>Moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mr. Tisdale</a> to strike out the word <span class='line-break'> </span>"side" in the fourth line of the report, so as to preserve the same<span class='line-break'> </span>space in the rear of the lots that is to be preserved upon the sides.</p>
<p>The motion was lost.</p>
<p>It was then moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Mr Cheever</a> that the report <span class='line-break'> </span>be accepted.</p>
<p>This motion was also lost, not receiving <span class='line-break'> </span>the requisite number - five, so that the article remained <span class='line-break'> </span>as originally adopted. _</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> then submitted the following form <span class='line-break'> </span>prepared by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr. Curtis</a> for conveyance of spaces between <span class='line-break'> </span>lots, the same being proposed as a substitute</p>
</div>

<div id="page-1279349">
<h3><a name="page-1279349">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 182)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>182</p>
<p>for that heretofore adopted, recorded upon page <span class='line-break'> </span>134 of this book. _</p>
<p>Voted that the same be adopted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Deed - Form of to convey spaces between Lots _'>Deed - Form of to convey spaces between Lots _</span></p>
<p>"Know all men by these presents, that <span class='line-break'> </span>the Proprietors of the Cemetery of Mount Auburn, in <span class='line-break'> </span>consideration of _____ dollars, paid to them by<span class='line-break'> </span>_____ of _____, the receipt of which is hereby acknowledged, <span class='line-break'> </span>do hereby grant, bargain, sell and convey to the said<span class='line-break'> </span>_____ and _____ heirs and assigns, a certain piece <span class='line-break'> </span>of land in the Cemetery of Mount Auburn, adjoining <span class='line-break'> </span>the _____ side of _____ lot, which is situated on the <span class='line-break'> </span>way called, _____ and numbered _____ on<span class='line-break'> </span>the plan of said Cemetery; the said piece of land <span class='line-break'> </span>being _____ feet wide and _____ feet in length, <span class='line-break'> </span>containing _____ square feet. _</p>
<p>To Have and to Hold the aforegranted prem<span class='line-break'></span>ises unto the said _____ heirs and assigns <span class='line-break'> </span>forever; subject however to the conditions and lim<span class='line-break'></span>itations following, to wit:</p>
<p><u>First</u>. That no part of said premises shall ever <span class='line-break'> </span>be used as a place of burial for the dead; unless <span class='line-break'> </span>the owner of the said lot shall purchase the same <span class='line-break'> </span>for the purpose of enlarging his burial lot. _</p>
<p><u>Second</u>. That the whole of said premises shall <span class='line-break'> </span>forever remain as a part of the open grounds of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Cemetery; except in the event of being purchaser <span class='line-break'> </span>by the owner of the said lot, as aforesaid. _</p>
<p><u>Third</u>. That no tree shrub or plant and no <span class='line-break'> </span>inscription, landmark, monument, fence or structure <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279350">
<h3><a name="page-1279350">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 183)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>183</p>
<p>whatever, shall be placed in or upon the premises,<span class='line-break'> </span>or be removed therefrom, without the consent of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Board of Trustees, for the time being, of <span class='line-break'> </span>said Corporation."</p>
<p>[The remainder is in the same form as, <span class='line-break'> </span>and consists of the covenants now in use for <span class='line-break'> </span>deeds of conveyance of lots, including the covenant <span class='line-break'> </span>just adopted. - ]</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Blank Deeds in this Form to be printed.'>Blank Deeds in this Form to be printed.</span></p>
<p>It was further Voted, upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span>Curtis</a>,</p>
<p>That <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> cause the foregoing for, and <span class='line-break'> </span>the usual covenants to be printed in form for con<span class='line-break'></span>veyance, also a book of record to correspond therewith.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='New Blanks for Conveyance of Lots to be printed'>New Blanks for Conveyance of Lots to be printed</span></p>
<p>Also upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>prepare and have printed a new form for conveyance <span class='line-break'> </span>of Lots, to conform to the order passed on <date when='1857-04-06'>the sixth<span class='line-break'> </span>day of April</date> relating to an accumulating fund;<span class='line-break'> </span>also record books to correspond.- -</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Represents of Lots Designated -'>Represent<sup>s</sup> of Lots Designated -</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->The Secretary</a> presented the written petitions <span class='line-break'> </span>of sundry parties for the appointment of representatives <span class='line-break'> </span>to respective Lots: - -</p>
<p>And it was ordered - That the persons <span class='line-break'> </span>therein severally designated be appointed to represent <span class='line-break'> </span>the lots hereafter mentioned in connection with <span class='line-break'> </span>their respective names. - -</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees May 4. 1857'>Trustees <date when='1857-05-04'>May 4. 1857</date></span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees was <span class='line-break'> </span>held at the usual place on <date when='1857-05-04'>Monday, May 4<sup>th</sup> at 10<span class='line-break'> </span>O'clock A. M.</date> _</p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>M<sup>c</sup>Kean</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a> = 7. _</p>
<p>The records of the last monthly meeting and the <span class='line-break'> </span>adjournment thereof were read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lands west of Chapel _ Price of _'>Lands west of <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a> _ Price of _</span></p>
<p>Upon Motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, Chairman of Com<sup>ee</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>on Lots,</p>
<p>Voted that the inquiry by <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Mr Mann</a>, the</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279362">
<h3><a name="page-1279362">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 195)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>195</p>
<p>Superintendent as to the price to be fixed on lands<span class='line-break'> </span>Westerly of and near the <a href='/pages/subjects/53239' title='Bigelow Chapel'><!--Bigelow-->Chapel</a>, which was referred to <span class='line-break'> </span>the Committee on Lots, be referred to the Committee on <span class='line-break'> </span>Grounds. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lot 339 respecting Tomb Right_'><a href='/pages/subjects/66416' title='Lot 339'>Lot 339</a> respecting Tomb Right_</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/66417' title='Dyer, Micah'>Micah Dyer</a> having made application for leave to <span class='line-break'> </span>construct a tomb on his lot, <a href='/pages/subjects/66416' title='Lot 339'>no. 339</a> on <a href='/pages/subjects/61262' title='Primrose Path'>Primrose Path</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>the subject was referred to the Committee on Lots, with <span class='line-break'> </span>power to contract with <a href='/pages/subjects/66417' title='Dyer, Micah'>Mr Dyer</a> for the price to be <span class='line-break'> </span>paid by him for the privilege, and mode in which <span class='line-break'> </span>the tomb is to be constructed, conformably to the By-Law. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Hubbard, G. G. Part of lot not paid for _ '><a href='/pages/subjects/60717' title='Hubbard, Gardner G.'>Hubbard, G. G.</a> Part of lot not paid for _ </span></p>
<p>Voted, That the Secretary address a communication <span class='line-break'> </span>to <a href='/pages/subjects/60717' title='Hubbard, Gardner G.'>Gardner G. Hubbard</a> acquainting him that it is ascer<span class='line-break'></span>tained that <a href='/pages/subjects/66419' title='Lot 1741'>Lot no. 1741</a> enclosed by him, contains <span class='line-break'> </span>658 square feet, and that unless the 358 feet which <span class='line-break'> </span>remain unpaid for, be paid for forthwith, the<span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees will cause the fence to be removed, and the <span class='line-break'> </span>lot to be reduced to the size of the lot paid for by him -<span class='line-break'> </span>to wit 300 square feet. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Suptt House _ Fence around.'><a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Supt<sup>t</sup> House</a> _ Fence around.</span></p>
<p>Voted _ that the Committee on Grounds, who were <span class='line-break'> </span>authorized at a meeting in February to take charge of any <span class='line-break'> </span>remaining expenditure in connection with the <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Sup<sup>t</sup>'s <span class='line-break'> </span>house</a> and grounds, be authorized to have a fence <span class='line-break'> </span>erected around the same at a price not exceeding <span class='line-break'> </span>$400.00 ~</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> being obliged to leave the meeting, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> was called to the Chair. _</p>

<p>196</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Water - Mr Tisdale added to Comee'>Water - <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mr Tisdale</a> added to Com<sup>ee</sup></span></p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mr Tisdale</a> be added to the <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee appointed at the last meeting to inquire upon <span class='line-break'> </span>what terms a supply of water for the Cemetery can <span class='line-break'> </span>be obtained from the <a href='/pages/subjects/64852' title='Cambridge Water Works'>Cambridge Water Works</a>. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on relations of this Corpn to Mass. Hort. Socy authorized to take legal advice _'>Com<sup>ee</sup> on relations of this Corp<sup>n</sup> to <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Mass. Hort. Soc<sup>y</sup></a> authorized to take legal advice _</span></p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, ^<sup>a</sup> member of the Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee to consider the relations and obligations of this <span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation to the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Massachusetts Horticultural Society</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>including in the subject of their inquiry the <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that said Committee be authorized<span class='line-break'> </span>to take the opinion of one or two eminent counsel <span class='line-break'> </span>on the respective rights of this Corporation and the <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Massachusetts Horticultural Society</a> with reference to the <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a>. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Represents of Lots appointed _'>Represent<sup>s</sup> of Lots appointed _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->The Secretary</a> presented the written petition of sundry<span class='line-break'> </span>parties for the appointment of representations of their <span class='line-break'> </span>respective lots: _</p>
<p>And it was ordered that the persons therein <span class='line-break'> </span>severally designated be appointed to represent the lots<span class='line-break'> </span>hereinafter mentioned in connection with their respective <span class='line-break'> </span>names. ~</p>

<h3><a name="page-1279368">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 201)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>201</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees. June. 1. 1857.'>Trustees. <date when='1857-06-01'>June. 1. 1857</date>.</span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees was held <span class='line-break'> </span>at the usual place on <date when='1857-06-01T10:00:00'>Monday June 1<sup>st</sup> 1857, at <span class='line-break'> </span>10 O'clock a.m.</date> ~</p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a> = 7. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee to settle claims of L. Stanwood and heirs of Edwd Miller appointed โ'>Com<sup>ee</sup> to settle claims of <a href='/pages/subjects/66840' title='Stanwood, Lemuel'>L. Stanwood</a> and heirs of <a href='/pages/subjects/58456' title='Miller, Edward'>Edw<sup>d</sup> Miller</a> appointed โ</span></p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>,</p>
<p>Voted, that <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the Presiden</a>t appoint a Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>to adjust and settle the claims of <a href='/pages/subjects/66840' title='Stanwood, Lemuel'>Lemuel Stan<span class='line-break'></span>wood</a>, and the Heirs of <a href='/pages/subjects/58456' title='Miller, Edward'>Edward Miller</a> for lots <span class='line-break'> </span>sold as vacant and claimed by the said parties.</p>
<p>And <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> was so appointed. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Old Receiving Tomb to be removed, &amp;c.'><a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Old Receiving Tomb</a> to be removed, &amp;c.</span></p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mr Tisdale</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that the <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Old Receiving Tomb</a> be re<span class='line-break'></span>moved and that the ground be prepared for sale <span class='line-break'> </span>as a lot or lots. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Bills due Corporation in arrear -'>Bills due Corporation in arrear -</span></p>
<p>A communication was received from <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'><!--Mann-->the Superintendent</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>stating substantially that there are outstanding bills due the <span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation for materials and labor amounting to thirteen <span class='line-break'> </span>hundred dollars ($1300.) which have been due from <span class='line-break'> </span>six to eighteen months - said bills being in sums mostly <span class='line-break'> </span>upwards of $10, and not exceeding $138: - that they have been <span class='line-break'> </span>presented for payment where the parties could be found,<span class='line-break'> </span>and further asking instructions with regard to the same. _</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1279369">
<h3><a name="page-1279369">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 202)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>202</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Secretary authorized to collect same _'>Secretary authorized to collect same _</span></p>
<p>Upon the foregoing communication, upon motion <span class='line-break'> </span>of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> be authorized to <span class='line-break'> </span>cause any bills due the Corporation, of which pay<span class='line-break'></span>ment has been delayed, to be collected. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Numbering of Lots, and the deeds thereof _ '>Numbering of Lots, and the deeds thereof _ </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->The Secretary</a> suggested that an improvement might <span class='line-break'> </span>be made in our system of numbering lots, and <span class='line-break'> </span>the deeds thereof, inasmuch, as by the present prac<span class='line-break'></span>tice, numerous blanks from time to time occur in <span class='line-break'> </span>the record of deeds, and in the catalogue. _</p>
<p>It was therefore, upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='to be done by Secretary -'>to be done by Secretary -</span></p>
<p>Voted. that, hereafter, the Superintendent be  instruc<span class='line-break'></span>ted to report to the Treasurer, all lots sold by him,<span class='line-break'> </span>without numbering them; and that the Treas<span class='line-break'></span>urer be also instructed to send the Secretary his <span class='line-break'> </span>orders for deeds without affixing numbers; _ that <span class='line-break'> </span>the numbers be affixed by the Secretary consec<span class='line-break'></span>utively in the order in which he receives them,<span class='line-break'> </span>and that he furnish the Superintendent a list of <span class='line-break'> </span>the lots with the numbers affixed, as fast as deeds <span class='line-break'> </span>are issued. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Death of H. S. McKean _'>Death of <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>H. S. M<sup>c</sup>Kean</a> _</span></p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, the following preamble<span class='line-break'> </span>and resolutions were adopted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Resolutions _'>Resolutions _</span></p>
<p>"Whereas the members of this Board of Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>have learned that, since the last meeting thereof,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>Henry S. M<sup>c</sup>Kean</a>, one of their associates, has de<span class='line-break'></span>parted this life: _ <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1279370">
<h3><a name="page-1279370">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 203)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>203</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Death of H. S. McKean - Resolutions -'>Death of <a href='/pages/subjects/62843' title='McKean, Henry S.'>H. S. M<sup>c</sup>Kean</a> - Resolutions -</span></p>
<p>Voted, That the Trustees desire to express their <span class='line-break'> </span>deep sympathy with the widow of the deceased, <span class='line-break'> </span>in this afflicting bereavement, and to assure her<span class='line-break'> </span>of the sincere respect they entertained for their depar<span class='line-break'></span>ted friend. _</p>
<p>Voted  that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> transmit a certified copy of <span class='line-break'> </span>these votes to <a href='/pages/subjects/66844' title='McKean, Anna H.'>Mrs Anna H. M<sup>c</sup>Kean</a>.</p>
<p>The meeting was then adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest. <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> Secretary</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Comee on Grounds on petitn of Wyeth, late Gate Keeper.'>Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds on petit<sup>n</sup> of <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Wyeth</a>, late Gate Keeper.</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a>, as Chairman of the Committee, sub<span class='line-break'></span>mitted the following report. _</p>
<p>"The Committee on Grounds to whom was re<span class='line-break'></span>ferred the application of <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr B.F. Wyeth</a>, the late Gate<span class='line-break'></span>Keeper report _</p>
<p>That the term of service of <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr Wyeth</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>having expired, and the Trustees in pursuance of <span class='line-break'> </span>their duty, and with a view to the good of Mount<span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn having appointed a new Gate Keeper, no<span class='line-break'></span>further measures are deemed necessary in relation<span class='line-break'> </span>to this matter."</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Accepted by yea &amp; nay-'>Accepted by yea &amp; nay-</span></p>
<p>It was moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> that the report be ac<span class='line-break'></span>cepted.</p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that the question be taken by yea and nay.</p>
<p>The motion for acceptance was then passed _<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, and Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a><span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'><!--Charles-->Little</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'><!--James-->Read</a> voting <u>yea</u>, and <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a> voting <span class='line-break'> </span><u>nay</u>. _    7 to 1 ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Loring, Abby W.&apos;s proposal to purchase land _'><a href='/pages/subjects/66845' title='Loring, Abby M.'>Loring, Abby W.'s</a> proposal to purchase land _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> submitted a written proposition made <span class='line-break'> </span>by <a href='/pages/subjects/66845' title='Loring, Abby M.'>Abby M. <p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee appoind to effect removal of tomb on Snowberry Path _'>Com<sup>ee</sup> appoin<sup>d</sup> to effect removal of tomb on <a href='/pages/subjects/64063' title='Snowberry Path'>Snowberry Path</a> _</span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Special Deed in  Trust authorized _'>Special Deed in  Trust authorized _</span></p>
<p>An application was made by <a href='/pages/subjects/66853' title='Storey, Charles W.'>Charles W. Storey</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>Executor of the will of the late <a href='/pages/subjects/66854' title='Sawyer, Matthias Plant'>Matthias P. Sawyer</a>, for <span class='line-break'> </span>the issuing of a deed of a lot containing two thousand <span class='line-break'> </span>square feet in the following special terms: _</p>
<p>..."in consideration of $1000 paid by <a href='/pages/subjects/66853' title='Storey, Charles W.'>Cha<sup>s</sup> W. <span class='line-break'> </span>Storey</a>, Executor of the last will of <a href='/pages/subjects/66854' title='Sawyer, Matthias Plant'>Matthias Plant Sawyer</a>, late <span class='line-break'> </span>of <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a>, Merchant, deceased _ .</p>
<p>At the request of said Storey,<span class='line-break'> </span>to <a href='/pages/subjects/66855' title='Raymond, Curtis B.'>Curtis B. Raymond</a> of <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a>, merchant _<span class='line-break'> </span>....in trust to permit the body of the said <span class='line-break'> </span>Sawyer and such suitable monument as said Storey shall <span class='line-break'> </span>select to be deposited and to remain undisturbed forever in <span class='line-break'> </span>and upon the said lot, and to use the said lot for the <span class='line-break'> </span>purposes of a burial ground for the families of said Raymond<span class='line-break'> </span>and his heirs in such manner as he or they may from time <span class='line-break'> </span>to time see fit not inconsistent with said trust, nor <span class='line-break'> </span>with the terms of these presents." _</p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Mr Gould</a>.</p>
<p>Voted that said deed in the form above stated <span class='line-break'> </span>be approved. _</p>

<p>An application in writing was made by <a href='/pages/subjects/66856' title='McConnell, James'>James <span class='line-break'> </span>M<sup>c</sup>Connell</a> to be allowed some compensation <span class='line-break'> </span>for a right of interment in the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>public lot</a>, which <span class='line-break'> </span>he formerly purchased, but had recently re<span class='line-break'></span>linquished by the removal of the interred body <span class='line-break'> </span>from the Cemetery.</p>
<p>It was stated by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> that such allow<span class='line-break'></span>ance would not be justified by any usage of this <span class='line-break'> </span>Board, and upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a>, it was</p>
<p>Voted that the petitioner have leave to <span class='line-break'> </span>withdraw.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lot 1741 G. G. Hubbard case _'><a href='/pages/subjects/66419' title='Lot 1741'>Lot 1741</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/60717' title='Hubbard, Gardner G.'>G. G. Hubbard</a> case _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->The Secretary</a> having reported that, pursuant<span class='line-break'> </span>to the order of May 4<sup>th</sup>, he had notified <a href='/pages/subjects/60717' title='Hubbard, Gardner G.'>G. G. Hubbard</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>that the fence was to be removed from that portion of <a href='/pages/subjects/66419' title='Lot 1741'>lot <span class='line-break'> </span>no. 1741</a> not yet paid for by him, unless the same should <span class='line-break'> </span>be paid for forthwith, and that, up to the present time, <span class='line-break'> </span>said land remained unpaid for, it was</p>
<p>Voted, that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> be directed to notify <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/60717' title='Hubbard, Gardner G.'>Mr Hubbard</a>, that if said land shall not be<span class='line-break'> </span>paid for before the first day of September, the fence <span class='line-break'> </span>will be removed at said Hubbard's expense. ~</p>

<div id="page-1279377">
<h3><a name="page-1279377">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 210)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>210</p>
<p>to appoint <a href='/pages/subjects/52579' title='Safford, Truman H.'>Mr T. H. Safford</a> a special policeman<span class='line-break'> </span>without compensation. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on Grounds report on Subject of Greenhouse, care of lots, &amp;c.'>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds report on Subject of <a href='/pages/subjects/61312' title='Greenhouse'>Greenhouse</a>, care of lots, &amp;c.</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> as Chairman of the Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>on Grounds submitted a written report upon the subject <span class='line-break'> </span>contained in the Superintendent's report referred to <span class='line-break'> </span>them at the last meeting, which is as follows: _</p>
<p>"The Committee on Grounds report _  That the great <span class='line-break'> </span>and increasing number of lots in Mount Auburn<span class='line-break'> </span>which are annually sold, surveyed and graded, and <span class='line-break'> </span>especially of those which after being made are to be pre<span class='line-break'></span>served in repair, _ also the many miles of paths and <span class='line-break'> </span>avenues which are to be kept in order, and the nu<span class='line-break'></span>merous applications from individual proprietors for various <span class='line-break'> </span>services, constitute collectively a duty too great to be well <span class='line-break'> </span>and advantageously performed by one individual.</p>
<p>They believe that it would conduce to the benefit <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Corporation and the convenience of proprietors,<span class='line-break'> </span>if a new subordinate officer should be appointed, with the <span class='line-break'> </span>title of Gardener, who shall have charge of the repair <span class='line-break'> </span>of lots of proprietors, and the sale and planting of <span class='line-break'> </span>shrubs, flowers &amp;c.  They therefore recommend that a <span class='line-break'> </span>gardener be appointed whose duties and tenor of<span class='line-break'> </span>office shall be defined by the adoption of the following <span class='line-break'> </span>bye-law."</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Bye Law _ Gardener _'>Bye Law _ Gardener _</span></p>
<p>Gardener _</p>
<p>"The Gardener, under direction of the Superintendent, <span class='line-break'> </span>shall take charge of and keep in repair the lots of such <span class='line-break'> </span>proprietors as may apply to him for that service,</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279378">
<h3><a name="page-1279378">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 211)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>211</p>
<p>and on such terms as may be agreed on between the <span class='line-break'> </span>parties; he shall also keep for sale at some convenient <span class='line-break'> </span>place designated by the Trustees, shrubs, trees and <span class='line-break'> </span>flowers, and be ready to furnish, plant or cultivate <span class='line-break'> </span>the same, at his own expense, and for such price and <span class='line-break'> </span>remuneration as may be agreed on with the purchasers.</p>
<p>That</p>
<p>Article 3<sup>d</sup> of the ByeLaws should be amended by <span class='line-break'> </span>inserting the words "a Gardener" after the words "Super<span class='line-break'></span>intendent's Clerk". _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Gardener _'>Gardener _</span></p>
<p>The Committee further recommends that a Gar<span class='line-break'></span>dener shall be appointed by this board for the remain<span class='line-break'></span>der of the present year, as soon as a suitable person <span class='line-break'> </span>can be determined on, and that the piece of ground<span class='line-break'> </span>west of the <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'>Superintendent's house</a> be leased to him <span class='line-break'> </span>per annum, on such terms and for such time <span class='line-break'> </span>as the Committee on Grounds may determine." _</p>
<p>Upon Motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that the report be adopted so far as <span class='line-break'> </span>can be done antecedently to the passage of the proposed <span class='line-break'> </span>bye law, and so far as may be necessary to authorize the<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee on Grounds to initiate the proper steps to such <span class='line-break'> </span>an appointment and arrangement of duties, and that they <span class='line-break'> </span>be hereby authorized with full power when said bye<span class='line-break'> </span>law shall have been adopted to carry its provisions <span class='line-break'> </span>into effect. _</p>
</div>
</div>

<h3><a name="page-1279383">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 216)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>216</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lease to A. Apple - the Gardener - read &amp; Adopted _'>Lease to <a href='/pages/subjects/66870' title='Apple, Anthony'>A. Apple</a> - the Gardener - read &amp; Adopted _</span></p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, the following <span class='line-break'> </span>preamble and vote were adopted.</p>
<p>"Whereas, under the direction of the Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee on Grounds, who were authorized to <span class='line-break'> </span>arrange the terms of a lease to <a href='/pages/subjects/66870' title='Apple, Anthony'>Anthony Apple</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> has prepared such lease to said <span class='line-break'> </span>Apple for the term of ten years, which lease <span class='line-break'> </span>has now been presented to this board and read.</p>
<p>Voted that said lease be hereby adopted. _ <span class='line-break'> </span>and that the <a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->Treasurer</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->Secretary</a> execute <span class='line-break'> </span>the same on behalf of this Corporation." _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on Lots to have control of the mode and manner of erecting Head Stones in Public ^Lots.'>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots to have control of the mode and manner of erecting Head Stones in <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public ^<sup>Lots</sup></a>.</span></p>
<p>Upon motion of the chairman of the Committee on Lots,</p>
<p>Voted that said Committee have control <span class='line-break'> </span>of the mode and manner of erecting monuments, <span class='line-break'> </span>and head stones in the <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>public lots</a>.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lot 32 _'><a href='/pages/subjects/66882' title='Lot 32'>Lot 32</a> _</span></p>
<p>Upon petition of <a href='/pages/subjects/66883' title='Austin, Daniel'>Daniel<!--Austin--></a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/66884' title='Austin, Hannah'>Hannah Austin</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/66885' title='Joy, Elizabeth'>Elizabeth Joy</a> of <a href='/pages/subjects/64824' title='Waltham, MA'>Waltham</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>sister and joint heir with the said Hannah of<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/66886' title='Joy, Joseph B.'>Joseph B. Joy</a>, late proprietor of <a href='/pages/subjects/66882' title='Lot 32'>lot numbered <span class='line-break'> </span>32</a>, on <a href='/pages/subjects/61237' title='Myrtle Path'>Myrtle Path</a>, be hereby designated to <span class='line-break'> </span>represent said lot. ~</p>
<p>Adjourned</p>
<p>Attest,, <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. J. Coolidge</a>, Secretary.</p>
