<h3><a name="page-1279384">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 217)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>217</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Decr 7. 1857'>Trustees <date when='1857-12-07'>Dec<sup>r</sup> 7. 1857</date></span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees <span class='line-break'> </span>was held at the usual place on <date when='1857-12-07T10:00:00'>Monday the <span class='line-break'> </span>seventh day of December  A. D. 1857, at 10 O'clock,<span class='line-break'> </span>a.m.</date></p>
<p>Present _  <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'><!--Charles-->Little</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lime Ave Location of refd to Comee on Grounds _'><a href='/pages/subjects/61222' title='Lime Avenue'>Lime Av<sup>e</sup></a> Location of ref<sup>d</sup> to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> stated that the location of <a href='/pages/subjects/61222' title='Lime Avenue'>Lime <span class='line-break'> </span>Avenue</a> as laid down upon the plan, does not <span class='line-break'> </span>correspond with its actual location. _</p>
<p>On motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Mr Little</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that the subject be referred to the <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee on Grounds, to report on at the next <span class='line-break'> </span>meeting.</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Mr Bangs</a> for the Committee on Lots submitted<span class='line-break'> </span>the following report. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Rept Comee on Lots _ on Head Stones in Public Lots _'>Rep<sup>t</sup> Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots _ on Head Stones in <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public Lots</a> _</span></p>
<p>"The communication from the Superintendent referred <span class='line-break'> </span>to the Committee on Lots _ subject _ the placing of Grave-Stones <span class='line-break'> </span>without sufficient foundation, _ has received their attention,<span class='line-break'> </span>and they having carefully examined, find that very <span class='line-break'> </span>few of the stones have sufficient foundation to keep them <span class='line-break'> </span>in place, and recommend that the Superintendent be <span class='line-break'> </span>directed to do what he can without too much expense <span class='line-break'> </span>to keep those already erected in their proper places; <span class='line-break'> </span>also to see that all stones erected hereafter, have a <span class='line-break'> </span>good and sufficient foundation."</p>
<p><date when='1857-12-07'>Dec<sup>r</sup> 7. 1857</date>.  (Signed) <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Isaiah Bangs</a>, for the Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots.</p>
</div>
</div>

<p>On motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Mr Gould</a><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the report be accepted &amp; adopted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Compensation of Secy for Extra Services. Referd to Comee _ '> Compensation of Sec<sup>y</sup> for Extra Services. Refer<sup>d</sup> to Com<sup>ee</sup> _ </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Mr Bangs</a> stated that it was well known to<span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> had rendered<span class='line-break'> </span>many services during the year or two past not falling<span class='line-break'> </span>under his regular duties, particularly in connection with<span class='line-break'> </span>the correcting of errors in the place and catalogue as well<span class='line-break'> </span>as the records, and in the preparation of the catalogues,<span class='line-break'> </span>the code of bye-laws &amp;c. _</p>
<p>And upon motion by him it was</p>
<p>Voted that a committee of two be appointed<span class='line-break'> </span>to consider if any, and what compensation be allowed<span class='line-break'> </span>him for such services. _</p>

<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr Crocker</a> be added to the<span class='line-break'> </span>committee.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Mr Tisdale _ Resignation as Trustee _ '> <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mr Tisdale</a> _ Resignation as Trustee _ </span></p>
<p>A communication received from <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mr Tisdale</a><span class='line-break'> </span>was read, in which he tendered his resignation<span class='line-break'> </span>as Trustee of Mount Auburn Cemetery from this date,<span class='line-break'> </span>(Dec<sup>r</sup> 7<sup>th</sup>).</p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Mr Gould</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that said resignation be laid upon the<span class='line-break'> </span>table for one month.</p>
<p>The meeting was then adjourned.<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A. J. Coolidge</a>, Secretary.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees of <span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn Cemetery was held on <date when='1858-01-04T10:00:00'>Monday<span class='line-break'> </span>January 4, 1858, at 10 O'clock, a.m.</date> ~  at<span class='line-break'> </span>the usual place. _</p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, and Messrs <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. <p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lime Avenue Plan to be corrected.'><a href='/pages/subjects/61222' title='Lime Avenue'>Lime Avenue</a> Plan to be corrected.</span></p>
<p>The Chairman of the Committee upon Grounds, <span class='line-break'> </span>to which Committee was referred at the last meeting<span class='line-break'> </span>the subject of the deviation of the plan from the location<span class='line-break'> </span>of <a href='/pages/subjects/61222' title='Lime Avenue'>Lime Avenue</a>, reported _ recommending that <span class='line-break'> </span>the plan be corrected so as to conform to the actual<span class='line-break'> </span>location: and the report was adopted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report  of Commee on Lots on bill disputed by Mr. C. G. Nazro'>Report  of Comm<sup>ee</sup> on Lots on bill disputed by <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr. C. G. Nazro</a></span></p>
<p>The Chairman of the Committee upon Lots, to which <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee is referred disputed bills against proprietors, <span class='line-break'> </span>submitted a written report upon a bill disputed <span class='line-break'> </span>by <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr C.G. Nazro</a>, with the accompanying papers:<span class='line-break'> </span>that no item of the bill appeared to them overcharged; <span class='line-break'> </span>and setting forth the views of the Committee as to the <span class='line-break'> </span>principle by which the Corporation should be governed <span class='line-break'> </span>in charging proprietors for work done upon lots. _</p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Mr Bangs</a>, the report was accepted, <span class='line-break'> </span>and the same, with the correspondence, is placed on file.</p>

<p>220</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='to Secy'>to Sec<sup>y</sup></span></p>
<p>written report, recommending an allowance of <span class='line-break'> </span>one hundred dollars for said services.</p>
<p>Upon Motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, the report was <span class='line-break'> </span>accepted and adopted: and the same is placed <span class='line-break'> </span>on file. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Path to Lot 1994 referred to Comee on Grounds'>Path to <a href='/pages/subjects/67011' title='Lot 1994'>Lot 1994</a> referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> for the Committee upon Lots stated that <span class='line-break'> </span>the Committee had initiated an arrangement with <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/67012' title='Story, C. W., Mr.'>Mr C. W. Story</a>, Executor of the late <a href='/pages/subjects/66854' title='Sawyer, Matthias Plant'>M. P. Sawyer</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span>lay out a path from <a href='/pages/subjects/61234' title='Moss Path'>Moss Path</a> to <a href='/pages/subjects/67011' title='Lot 1994'>Lot 1994</a>, lately <span class='line-break'> </span>purchased by him, he having purchased a lot of <span class='line-break'> </span>300 square feet on the line of said proposed pathway;<span class='line-break'> </span>and he further moved the reference of the subject<span class='line-break'> </span>to the Committee upon Grounds, which was adopted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lot 116 _ Division of authorized. '><a href='/pages/subjects/67014' title='Lot 116'>Lot 116</a> _ Division of authorized. </span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> stated that he was the Proprietor <span class='line-break'> </span>of a lot containing 600 feet, situated upon <a href='/pages/subjects/61127' title='Beech Avenue'>Beech Avenue</a><span class='line-break'> </span>and <a href='/pages/subjects/61187' title='Geranium Path'>Geranium Path</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/67014' title='Lot 116'>numbered 116</a>, _ that 300 feet<span class='line-break'> </span>of it situated upon <a href='/pages/subjects/61187' title='Geranium Path'>Geranium Path</a> belonged to <a href='/pages/subjects/67015' title='Scollay, Catherine'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span>Catherine Scollay</a>, and was conveyed to him by accident,<span class='line-break'> </span>and requested that that the lot might be divided,<span class='line-break'> </span>and conveyed in accordance with the above facts.</p>
<p>Upon which it was</p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/67014' title='Lot 116'>Lot No. 116</a> be divided into two lots, <span class='line-break'> </span>and 300 feet thereof be conveyed to <a href='/pages/subjects/67015' title='Scollay, Catherine'>Mrs Catherine <span class='line-break'> </span>Scollay,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> first making the requisite <span class='line-break'> </span>transfer. _</p>
<p>The meeting ws then adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>, Secretary.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees February 1. 1858.'>Trustees <date when='1858-02-01'>February 1. 1858</date>.</span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees, (the <span class='line-break'> </span>same being the final meeting of this Board,) was held<span class='line-break'> </span>at the usual place on <date when='1858-02-01T10:00:00'>Monday, February 1<sup>st</sup> at 10<span class='line-break'> </span>O'clock a.m. </date>_</p>
<p>Present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'><!--James-->Read</a>. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Claims of Miller Heirs, &amp; L. Stanwood _ Final'>Claims of <a href='/pages/subjects/58456' title='Miller, Edward'>Miller</a> Heirs, &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/66840' title='Stanwood, Lemuel'>L. Stanwood</a> _ Final</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr. Curtis</a> who was appointed a Committee to settle<span class='line-break'> </span>the claims of the heirs of <a href='/pages/subjects/58456' title='Miller, Edward'>Edward Miller</a> and of <a href='/pages/subjects/66840' title='Stanwood, Lemuel'>Lem<span class='line-break'></span>uel Stanwood</a>, for lots taken, reported _</p>
<p>That he has made a settlement of the claims of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Miller heirs by the payment to them of the sum of<span class='line-break'> </span>one hundred and fifty dollars, in return for which <span class='line-break'> </span>they have releasd all right and title in the lots<span class='line-break'> </span>granted them. _</p>
<p>Also, that he has made an arrangement with <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/66840' title='Stanwood, Lemuel'>Lemuel Stanwood</a> for an exchange of lots, the papers<span class='line-break'> </span>for which however have not been completed. _</p>
<p>And the report was accepted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Relations with M.H. Socy Unfinished'>Relations with <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>M.H. Soc<sup>y</sup></a> Unfinished</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> for the Committee to consider the relations <span class='line-break'> </span>of this Corporation to the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Massachusetts Horticultural Society</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>stated that the Committee had given the subject much <span class='line-break'> </span>consideration, but are not yet able to report,. _</p>

<div id="page-1279392">
<h3><a name="page-1279392">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 225)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>225</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Proprietors Annual Meeting _ Feby. 1.1858.'>Proprietors Annual Meeting _ <date when='1858-02-01'>Feby. 1.1858</date>.</span></p>
<p>"Mount Auburn Cemetery</p>
<p>The annual meeting of the Proprietors of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Cemetery of Mount Auburn will be held at<span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/62836' title='Meionaon, Tremont Temple'>Meionaon (Tremont Temple)</a>, on <date when='1858-02-01T16:00:00'>Monday the<span class='line-break'> </span>first day of February, at 4 O'clock. P.M.</date>, to <span class='line-break'> </span>hear the reports of the Trustees, Treasurer and<span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent; to choose Trustees for the ensuing<span class='line-break'> </span>year; and to act on any other business that may<span class='line-break'> </span>legally come before the meeting.</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a> <date when='1858-01-23'> January 23<sup>d</sup> 1858</date> <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>, Secretary."</p>
<p>Pursuant to the foregoing notice which was<span class='line-break'> </span>published more than seven days before the time of<span class='line-break'> </span>meeting in the <a href='/pages/subjects/58551' title='Boston Daily Advertiser'>Boston Daily Advertiser</a> and several<span class='line-break'> </span>other newspapers in <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a>, the Proprietors met<span class='line-break'> </span>at the time and place therein named. _</p>
<p>A quorum being in attendance, the President,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr Jacob Bigelow</a> took the chair.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Reading of Records'>Reading of Records</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->The Secretary</a> read the ^<sup>printed</sup> notification of the meeting;<span class='line-break'> </span>also the record of the last annual meeting,<span class='line-break'> </span>and the adjournment thereof.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Annual Report'>Trustees Annual Report</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> read the Annual Report of the Trustees,<span class='line-break'> </span>and the same, upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/62826' title='Bates, George'>Dr Geo. Bates</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>was accepted, and ordered to be printed for dis- <span class='line-break'> </span>tribution among the Proprietors.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Treasurer&apos;s Annl Rept'>Treasurer's Ann<sup>l</sup> Rep<sup>t</sup></span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->The Treasurer</a> read his annual report, also<span class='line-break'> </span>that of the Superintendent. ~</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Memorial of B. F. Wyeth-'>Memorial of <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>B. F. Wyeth</a>-</span></p>
<p>from <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr B. F. Wyeth</a>, late Gate Keeper, complaining that <span class='line-break'> </span>he had been discharged by the last Board of Trustees,</p>

<div id="page-1279395">
<h3><a name="page-1279395">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 228)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>228</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Referred to Trustees'>Referred to Trustees</span></p>
<p>without any reason being assigned therefor,<span class='line-break'> </span>and asking a hearing before the Proprietors.</p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/72375' title='Hallett, Benjamin F.'>B. F Hallett Esq.</a>, it was<span class='line-break'> </span>voted to refer the memorial to the Board<span class='line-break'> </span>of Trustees about the elected.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees requested to modify Permanent Fund so as to apply to Lots _'>Trustees <ins>requested</ins> to modify Permanent Fund so as to apply to Lots _</span></p>
<p>It was also moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/72375' title='Hallett, Benjamin F.'>Mr Hallett</a> _<span class='line-break'> </span>That the Trustees be instructed so to modify<span class='line-break'> </span>the terms of investment for the accumulating Fund as<span class='line-break'> </span>to make the income apply to the case of lots as well<span class='line-break'> </span>as to the grounds of the Cemetery.</p>
<p>After some discussion by several gentlemen,<span class='line-break'> </span>an amendment was moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/62119' title='Lee, Thomas J.'>Mr T.J. Lee</a>, and<span class='line-break'> </span>accepted by <a href='/pages/subjects/72375' title='Hallett, Benjamin F.'>Mr Hallet</a> [sic], to substitute the word<span class='line-break'> </span>"requested" for "instructed"; and the resolution<span class='line-break'> </span>was passed in that form. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Thanks voted to Messrs Tisdale &amp; Lawrence _'>Thanks voted to Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Tisdale</a> &amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Lawrence</a> _</span></p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/67765' title='Brown, Charles H.'>Mr Cha<sup>s</sup> H. Brown</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>it was</p>
<p>Voted that the thanks of the Propri- <span class='line-break'> </span>etors be tendered to <a href='/pages/subjects/54952' title='Tisdale, Mace'>Mace Tisdale</a> Esq<span class='line-break'> </span>and <a href='/pages/subjects/104060' title='Lawrence, William R. (1812-1885)'>Doct. W<sup>m</sup> R. Lawrence</a> for their<span class='line-break'> </span>able and faithful services, which have<span class='line-break'> </span>been so beneficial to the Corporation; <del>and</del><span class='line-break'> </span><small>and that the Secretary be requested to transmit to them severally a copy</small><span class='line-break'> </span><small>of this vote. _</small></p>
<p>The Committee appointed to receive, assort, count<span class='line-break'> </span>and declare the votes for Trustees reported: _</p>

<p>----------------------------</p>
<p>This certifies that we have examined the books and accounts of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Treasurer of the Proprietors of the Cemetery of Mount Auburn, for<span class='line-break'> </span>the year ending <date when='1857-12-31'>Decem<sup>r</sup> 31, 1857</date>, and have found them correctly<span class='line-break'> </span>kept and properly balanced with satisfactory vouchers for all<span class='line-break'> </span>payments charged.</p>
<p>The certificates of stocks and other evidences of property were<span class='line-break'> </span>found in accordance with the statements in his accounts.</p>
<p>In the Fund for Repairs there appears to be due him<span class='line-break'> </span>one hundred &amp; twenty four 88/100 dollars, and to be in his hands<span class='line-break'> </span>belonging to the general accounts of the Corporation one<span class='line-break'> </span>hundred &amp; seventy three 89/100 dollars.</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a> <date when='1858-02-01'>Feby. 1, 1858</date>.</p>

<h3><a name="page-1279402">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 235)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>235</p>
<p>Trustees Records ~ 1858 ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees _ Feby. 8. 1858'>Trustees _ <date when='1858-02-08'>Feby. 8. 1858</date></span></p>
<p>In accordance with the by-law requiring the Secretary to call<span class='line-break'> </span>the first meeting of the Trustees written fourteen days after<span class='line-break'> </span>the annual meeting, and notices having been issued<span class='line-break'> </span>for such meeting, the Trustees met at the office of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Secretary, on <date when='1858-02-08'>Monday, February 8<sup>th</sup>, 1858 at 10 o'clock am.</date></p>
<p>There were present Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Bigelow</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>, Read,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/65944' title='Sleeper, Jacob'>Sleeper</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/67763' title='Tobey, Edward S.'>Tobey</a> ; <span class='line-break'> </span>and <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr Crocker</a> subsequently appears. _ 10 members</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr Bigelow</a> took the Chair, and the record of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Annual meeting was read. ~</p>
<p>The chair announced the first business to be the election<span class='line-break'> </span>of officers and committees for the ensuing year. _</p>
<p>The Trustees then proceeded to ballot for officers<span class='line-break'> </span>and Committees, each of which received eight votes<span class='line-break'> </span>the whole number cast, and they are as follows: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Officers Chosen _'>Officers Chosen _</span></p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>President</th> <th><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Jacob Bigelow</a><span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Secretary</td> <td><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a></td> </tr> <tr><td>Treasurer</td> <td><a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'>George W<sup>m</sup> Bond</a></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comees Chosen'>Com<sup>ees</sup> Chosen</span></p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>Committee on</th> <th>} Messrs</th> <th><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'><!--Charles-->Little</a><span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Finance</td> <td>}</td> <td><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span>[text inscribed on the left margin of the page]<span class='line-break'> </span>Commonwealth of Massachusetts, Suffolk ss.<span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1858-02-08'>February 8, 1858</date>. <p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Choice of Supts Clerk &amp; Gate Keeper postponed to adjourned meeting'>Choice of Supt<sup>s</sup> Clerk &amp; Gate Keeper postponed to adjourned meeting</span></p>
<p>The choice of Superintendent's clerk, and gate Keeper<span class='line-break'> </span>being next in order, it was moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>and Voted _ That the choice of Gate Keeper and <span class='line-break'> </span>Sup<sup>t</sup>'s Clerk be laid upon the table until the time <span class='line-break'> </span>to which this meeting may be adjourned; and that</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='B. F. Wyeth&apos;s memorial referred to a Comee of three.'><a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>B. F. Wyeth</a>'s memorial referred to a Com<sup>ee</sup> of three.</span></p>
<p>the memorial of <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr B. F. Wyeth</a>, former Gate Keeper, <span class='line-break'> </span>which was referred by the Proprietors, at their Annual <span class='line-break'> </span>Meeting to this board of Trustees, be now referred <span class='line-break'> </span>to a committee of three to report thereon at such <span class='line-break'> </span>adjourned meeting: _ and that when this meeting <span class='line-break'> </span>adjourns, it will be to the next regular meeting.</p>
<p>Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a> were <span class='line-break'> </span>appointed such committee. _ </p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Secy&apos;s  &amp; Treasr&apos;s Salaries'>Sec<sup>y</sup>'s  &amp; Treas<sup>r</sup>'s Salaries</span></p>
<p>{ Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, ^<sup>voted that</sup> the salary of the Secretary <span class='line-break'> </span>{ be the same as last year: three hundred dollars, and the <span class='line-break'> </span>{ usual fees. _<span class='line-break'> </span>{ Upon Motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a>, Voted that the compensation <span class='line-break'> </span>{ of the Treasurer be the same as last year, a com<span class='line-break'></span>{ mission of two and one half per cent on the gross sales of <span class='line-break'> </span>{ lots.</p>

<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr Crocker</a>, voted that the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>on Finance be instructed to examine and report upon the <span class='line-break'> </span>sufficiency of the bond given by that Treasurer. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Salary of Sup.t.'>Salary of Sup.t.</span></p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Mr Bangs</a>, Voted that the salary <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Superintendent be the same as the last year _<span class='line-break'> </span>one thousand dollars and the use of the house.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Privilege to Sup.t.'>Privilege to Sup.t.</span></p>
<p>It was further voted upon motion of <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Mr Gould</a>, that the Committee on Grounds have <span class='line-break'> </span>authority to allow the Superintendent to use such wood <span class='line-break'> </span>from the Cemetery, for fuel, as they shall think proper. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Salary of Gate Keeper &amp;c postponed _'>Salary of Gate Keeper &amp;c postponed _</span></p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>, Voted that the subject <span class='line-break'> </span>of the salary of the Gate Keeper and Superintendent's Clerk<span class='line-break'> </span>be postponed until the adjourned meeting. _</p>

<p>238</p>
<p>and disbursing moneys by the Superintendent, and <span class='line-break'> </span>report at the adjourned meeting.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Mr Hallett&apos;s Resolution respecting Care of Lots. referred to Specl Comee'><a href='/pages/subjects/72375' title='Hallett, Benjamin F.'>Mr Hallett's</a> Resolution respecting Care of Lots. referred to Spec<sup>l</sup> Com<sup>ee</sup></span></p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, Voted that the resolu<span class='line-break'></span>tion offered by <a href='/pages/subjects/72375' title='Hallett, Benjamin F.'>B. F. Hallett Esq.</a> at the annual <span class='line-break'> </span>meeting of the Proprietors respecting such modification <span class='line-break'> </span>in the terms of the accumulating fund as to make <span class='line-break'> </span>the same apply to the care of lots, which was referred <span class='line-break'> </span>to this Board of Trustees, be now referred to a <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee of three, to consider and report thereon.</p>
<p>Upon nomination of <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a> were so appointed.<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Mr Cheever</a> declining, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> was appointed <span class='line-break'> </span>in his stead.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Plan for preservation &amp; use of Gravel _ Refd to Comee on Grounds _'>Plan for preservation &amp; use of Gravel _ Ref<sup>d</sup> to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds _</span></p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>, Voted that the com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee on Grounds be instructed to report a prospec<span class='line-break'></span>tive plan for the preservation and use of the gravel <span class='line-break'> </span>on the unsold parts of Mount Auburn. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Purchase of lots on Laurel Hill, Refd to Comee on Grounds'>Purchase of lots on <a href='/pages/subjects/55347' title='Laurel Hill'>Laurel Hill</a>, Ref<sup>d</sup> to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds</span></p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, Voted that the Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee on Grounds be instructed to inquire on what <span class='line-break'> </span>terms they can purchase the lots on <a href='/pages/subjects/55347' title='Laurel Hill'>Laurel Hill</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>(so called) with full power to act in the premises. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Receiving Tombs _ Refd to Comee on Grounds _'><a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tombs</a> _ Ref<sup>d</sup> to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds _</span></p>
<p>Upon motion also by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, Voted that the Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee on Grounds be instructed to consider and <span class='line-break'> </span>report upon the general subject of <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tombs</a>, and <span class='line-break'> </span>whether a new one is or is not necessary. _</p>

<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr Crocker</a>.</p>

(1787-1859)'>Mr Gould</a> be a Committee with all <span class='line-break'> </span>necessary power in relation to any existing contracts for <span class='line-break'> </span>statuary.</p>

<p>Upon motion from <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Mr Bangs</a>, Voted to renew the<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee of last year _ viz.</p>
<p>Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>, and <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'><!--James-->Read</a>,</p>
<p>To inquire on what terms a supply  of water for <span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn can be obtained from the <a href='/pages/subjects/64852' title='Cambridge Water Works'>Cambridge <span class='line-break'> </span>Water Works</a>, and report thereon.</p>

<p>The meeting was then adjourned,,</p>
<p>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>,, Secretary.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees March 1. 1858'>Trustees <date when='1858-03-01'>March 1. 1858</date></span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees,<span class='line-break'> </span>the same being ^<sup>also</sup> an adjourned meeting, was held <span class='line-break'> </span>on <date when='1858-03-01'>Monday, March 1<sup>st</sup> 1858. at 10 o'clock a.m.</date><span class='line-break'> </span>at the usual place. _</p>
<p>Present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little,</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>, and <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'><!--James-->Read</a>.</p>
<p>The record of the meeting for organization was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Comee on memorial of B. F. Wyeth.'>Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> on memorial of <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>B. F. Wyeth</a>.</span></p>
<p>The Committee to whom was referred at the last <span class='line-break'> </span>meeting the memorial of <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr B. F. Wyeth</a>, reported <span class='line-break'> </span>through <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, the report being signed by Messrs <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a> _ declining to <small>inquire whether any or what allegations were</small> <span class='line-break'> </span>^<sup>made against <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr Wyeth</a>, for reasons fully set forth in the report ~</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>the Chairman of the Committee <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a> presented <span class='line-break'> </span>a minority report</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Accepted.'>Accepted.</span></p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, seconded by <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>it was voted that the report be accepted, six voting <span class='line-break'> </span>affirmatively,  and one in the negative.</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr Crocker</a> joined the meeting at this stage.</p>
<p>It was then moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a> and seconded by <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span>Crocker</a> that the following votes which were appended <span class='line-break'> </span>to his report, be adopted, and that the question be <span class='line-break'> </span>taken by yea and nay. _</p>
<p>"That in the opinion of this board, while <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span>Wyeth</a> held the offices of Gate Keeper and Superintendent's <span class='line-break'> </span>Clerk, at Mount Auburn, he was faithful and honest <span class='line-break'> </span>in the performance of his duties, and that the Trustees, <span class='line-break'> </span>at the time they appointed another individual to succeed<span class='line-break'> </span>him in those offices, had nothing against his</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1279408">
<h3><a name="page-1279408">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 241)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>241</p>
<p>character for faithfulness or capacity โ but deemed <span class='line-break'> </span>it proper to appoint another person in his place.</p>
<p>That <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a> be directed to transmit a <span class='line-break'> </span>copy of the above vote to <a href='/pages/subjects/62093' title='Wyeth, Benjamin F.'>Mr Wyeth</a>."</p>
<p>The motion was put and not carried, <span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> voting yea, and <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the <span class='line-break'> </span>President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>, Little &amp;</a> <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'><!--James-->Read</a><span class='line-break'> </span>voting nay. 2 โ 6.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Salary of Gate Keeper &amp; Supts clerk'>Salary of Gate Keeper &amp; Sup<sup>ts</sup> clerk</span></p>
<p>It was moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, ^<sup>&amp;</sup> seconded by <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Mr Cheever</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>that the salary of the Gate Keeper and Superintendent's <span class='line-break'> </span>Clerk be five hundred dollars per annum. ~</p>
<p>An amendment was moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a> sec<span class='line-break'></span>onded by <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr Crocker</a> that the sum of four hundred <span class='line-break'> </span>and fifty dollars be substituted for five hundred,<span class='line-break'> </span>but the amendment was rejected, two voting in the affirm<span class='line-break'></span>ative and six in the negative.</p>
<p>The motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> was then put and adopted <span class='line-break'> </span>by a vote of six to two. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='T. H. Safford chosen Gate Keeper. &amp; Supts Clerk.'><a href='/pages/subjects/52579' title='Safford, Truman H.'>T. H. Safford</a> chosen Gate Keeper. &amp; Supt<sup>s</sup> Clerk.</span></p>
<p>It was further moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, seconded by <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a>, that  <a href='/pages/subjects/52579' title='Safford, Truman H.'>Truman H. Safford</a> be chosen <span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent's Clerk and Gate Keeper for the year ensuing <span class='line-break'> </span>which was adopted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Comee on Grounds, on Improving, filling up [&amp; grading unsold lands _]'>Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds, on Improving, filling up [&amp; grading unsold lands _]</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> as Chairman of the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>on Grounds submitted a report containing certain <span class='line-break'> </span>recommendations for filling up, improving and embellish<span class='line-break'></span>ing the grounds of the Cemetery, which was read and <span class='line-break'> </span>adopted section by section, and then adopted entire,</p>

<div id="page-1279409">
<h3><a name="page-1279409">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 242)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>242</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='[Report of Comee on Grounds, on Improving, filling up] &amp; grading unsold lands _'>[Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds, on Improving, filling up] &amp; grading unsold lands _</span></p>
<p>of which report the following is a copy. _</p>
<p>"That the Committee on Grounds be instructed <span class='line-break'> </span>to expend one thousand dollars per annum in <span class='line-break'> </span>grading and improving the unsold parts of the <span class='line-break'> </span>land within the Cemetery, and that the earth removed <span class='line-break'> </span>by this process be applied towards filling up the super<span class='line-break'></span>flous ponds and hollows in the grounds.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Embellishing with oramental trees _'>Embellishing with oramental trees _</span></p>
<p>That the same Committee be authorized this year <span class='line-break'> </span>to introduce ornamental trees and shrubs into <span class='line-break'> </span>suitable parts of the ground, at a cost not exceeding <span class='line-break'> </span>five hundred dollars.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Constructing Drain through Indian Ridge _'>Constructing Drain through <a href='/pages/subjects/54338' title='Indian Ridge Path'>Indian Ridge</a> _</span></p>
<p>That the same Committee be authorized, if they deem it <span class='line-break'> </span>expedient, to construct a drain through <a href='/pages/subjects/54338' title='Indian Ridge Path'>Indian Ridge</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>from <a href='/pages/subjects/57864' title='Halcyon Lake'>Garden Pond</a> to <a href='/pages/subjects/57593' title='Auburn Lake'>Meadow Pond</a>, so arranging <span class='line-break'> </span>the banks made by cutting this drain, that they may <span class='line-break'> </span>hereafter be used for constructing <a href='/pages/subjects/66005' title='Catacomb Tombs'>catacomb tombs</a>; the <span class='line-break'> </span>outlay not to exceed one thousand dollars."_</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> being called away <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a> was called to the Chair.</p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, the following vote was <span class='line-break'> </span>passed.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Path laid out as a branch of Moss Path to Raymond Lot _'>Path laid out as a branch of <a href='/pages/subjects/61234' title='Moss Path'>Moss Path</a> to <a href='/pages/subjects/66855' title='Raymond, Curtis B.'>Raymond</a> Lot _</span></p>
<p>"Whereas <a href='/pages/subjects/67012' title='Story, C. W., Mr.'>C. W. Storey Esq.</a> Executor of the late <a href='/pages/subjects/66854' title='Sawyer, Matthias Plant'>M. P. <span class='line-break'> </span>Sawyer</a> has purchased a lot of land containing three hun<span class='line-break'></span>dred square feet, in the Cemetery of Mount Auburn, situ<span class='line-break'></span>ated between <a href='/pages/subjects/61234' title='Moss Path'>Moss Path</a> opposite to <a href='/pages/subjects/57672' title='Central Square'>Central Square</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span>the Northerly side of the lot of <a href='/pages/subjects/66855' title='Raymond, Curtis B.'>C. B. Raymond</a>, Trustee, <a href='/pages/subjects/67011' title='Lot 1994'>num<span class='line-break'></span>bered 1994</a>, for the sum of one hundred and fifty dollars, <span class='line-break'> </span>for the purpose of making a way to said <a href='/pages/subjects/67011' title='Lot 1994'>lot numbered 1994</a>, <span class='line-break'> </span>โ and whereas said lot is wider than is necessary for</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279410">
<h3><a name="page-1279410">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 243)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>243</p>
<p>a path but does not extend in length so far as to <span class='line-break'> </span>cover the whole distance to said <a href='/pages/subjects/67011' title='Lot 1994'>lot numbered <span class='line-break'> </span>1994</a>, so that the aforesaid object of purchasing said <span class='line-break'> </span>lot of three hundred feet is not thereby attained, _</p>
<p>Now in consideration of the payment aforesaid <span class='line-break'> </span>by the said <a href='/pages/subjects/67012' title='Story, C. W., Mr.'>Storey</a>: and of his release of all right <span class='line-break'> </span>and title to said lot of three hundred square feet</p>
<p>It is hereby ordered, that said lot of three<span class='line-break'> </span>hundred ^<sup>square</sup> feet be discontinued, and that a path <span class='line-break'> </span>eight feet in width be laid out by this Corpora<span class='line-break'></span>tion from <a href='/pages/subjects/61234' title='Moss Path'>Moss Path</a>, opposite <a href='/pages/subjects/57672' title='Central Square'>Central Square</a>, as <span class='line-break'> </span>aforesaid, to said <a href='/pages/subjects/67011' title='Lot 1994'>lot numbered 1994</a>, over the <span class='line-break'> </span>route above described, and be forever kept open for <span class='line-break'> </span>the benefit of said <a href='/pages/subjects/67011' title='Lot 1994'>lot numbered 1994</a>, and any <span class='line-break'> </span>other lots that may border upon said path.</p>
<p>It was further voted that said path be regarded <span class='line-break'> </span>as a part of <a href='/pages/subjects/61234' title='Moss Path'>Moss Path</a>.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Whether deed can be made to heirs at law? Refd to Comee on Lots _'><small>Whether deed can be made to heirs at law? Ref<sup>d</sup> to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots _</small></span></p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that the Committee on Lots be requested to <span class='line-break'> </span>consider, whether, under the Charter, a deed can be made <span class='line-break'> </span>to the heirs at law of a person, as one person, and <span class='line-break'> </span>report thereon.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lot 209'><a href='/pages/subjects/67819' title='Lot 209'>Lot 209</a></span></p>
<p>Upon the petition of the parties in interest, <a href='/pages/subjects/67820' title='Lindsey, Christina'>Christina<span class='line-break'> </span>Lindsey</a> of <a href='/pages/subjects/54284' title='Charlestown, MA'>Charlestown</a> widow of <a href='/pages/subjects/67821' title='Lindsey, Ichabod'>Ichabod Lindsey</a> late <span class='line-break'> </span>proprietor of <a href='/pages/subjects/67819' title='Lot 209'>lot numbered 209</a>, was appointed to repre<span class='line-break'></span>sent said lot. _</p>
<p>The meeting was then adjourned.</p>
<p>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>,, Secretary.</p>

<div id="page-1279411">
<h3><a name="page-1279411">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 244)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>244</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees April 5. 1858.'>Trustees <date when='1858-04-05'>April 5. 1858</date>.</span></p>
<p>The regular meeting of the Trustees was holden <span class='line-break'> </span>at the usual place on <date when='1858-04-05'>Monday, April 5<sup>th</sup> 1858</date>.</p>
<p>Present _ <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p>On motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>,</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Special Police _'>Special Police _</span></p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Mr Bangs</a> be a Committee to re<span class='line-break'></span>quest the Mayor and Aldermen of <a href='/pages/subjects/53203' title='Cambridge, MA'>Cambridge</a>, and the <span class='line-break'> </span>Selectmen of <a href='/pages/subjects/53204' title='Watertown, MA'>Watertown</a> to appoint the Superintendent,<span class='line-break'> </span>the Gate Keeper and two other suitable men to be nom<span class='line-break'></span>inated by the Superintendent, as special policemen<span class='line-break'> </span>in and around the Cemetery of Mount Auburn,<span class='line-break'> </span>without compensation. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Record of Interments _'>Record of Interments _</span></p>
<p>A communication was presented from <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Mr Mann</a><span class='line-break'> </span>the Superintendent, "recommending that the record of inter<span class='line-break'></span>ments be kept where the numbers of the lots are given."</p>
<p>Voted, upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Mr Nazro</a>, that the matter <span class='line-break'> </span>be referred to the Committee on Lots to report thereon<span class='line-break'> </span>at the next meeting.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Waldo H. S. concerning deed of his lot _'><a href='/pages/subjects/67823' title='Waldo, H. S., Mr.'>Waldo H. S.</a> concerning deed of his lot _</span></p>
<p>The Treasurer, <a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'>Mr Bond</a>, stated that some mis<span class='line-break'></span>understanding has occurred with <a href='/pages/subjects/67823' title='Waldo, H. S., Mr.'>Mr H.S. Waldo</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>the proprietor of <a href='/pages/subjects/67824' title='Lot 1751'>lot no. 1751</a>, on <a href='/pages/subjects/61186' title='Gentian Path'>Gentian Path</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/59904' title='Spruce Avenue'>Spruce<span class='line-break'> </span>Avenue</a>, with reference to the issue of a deed to him <span class='line-break'> </span>of a lot in the rear of said 1751, upon <a href='/pages/subjects/61186' title='Gentian Path'>Gentian<!--Path--></a></p>

<p>Path, without the payment of $20 for right of <span class='line-break'> </span>choice, under the old system of selling, and also <span class='line-break'> </span>an unpaid balance for said lot, as now sur<span class='line-break'></span>veyed. _ <a href='/pages/subjects/67823' title='Waldo, H. <p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees _ June. 7th 1858.'>Trustees _ <date when='1858-06-07'>June. 7<sup>th</sup> 1858</date>.</span></p>
<p>The monthly meeting of the Trustees was held at <span class='line-break'> </span>the usual place on <date when='1858-06-07T10:00:00'>Monday, June 7<sup>th</sup> 1858,<span class='line-break'> </span>at 10 o'clock a.m.</date></p>
<p>There were present, <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Crocker</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/67763' title='Tobey, Edward S.'>Tobey</a>. ~</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Comee on Records at Cemetery and numbering of Lots _'>Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> on Records at Cemetery and numbering of Lots _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/67763' title='Tobey, Edward S.'>Mr Tobey</a> for the Committee upon Lots read <span class='line-break'> </span>the following report.</p>
<p>"The Committee upon Lots to whom was re<span class='line-break'></span>ferred a communication from <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'>Jon<sup>a</sup> Mann</a>, Sup<sup>t</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>addressed to the Trustees of Mount Auburn Cemetery <span class='line-break'> </span>in reference to the mode of keeping the records of <span class='line-break'> </span>interments at the Cemetery respectfully</p>
<p>Report</p>
<p>That they have examined the records referred to, as <span class='line-break'> </span>now kept, and after having fully considered the subject<span class='line-break'> </span>referred to them, are of opinion that the liability <span class='line-break'> </span>to inaccuracy in the records will be much diminished</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279416">
<h3><a name="page-1279416">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 249)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>249</p>
<p>by some change in the system.  They would therefore <span class='line-break'> </span>recommend that the records of interments should <span class='line-break'> </span>continue to be kept at the Cemetery, but that <span class='line-break'> </span>the Superintendent be authorized and directed to <span class='line-break'> </span>number the lots when selected by any person<span class='line-break'> </span>proposing to purchase, and to place on such lot <span class='line-break'> </span>or lots a broad stake, on which shall be <span class='line-break'> </span>printed in legible figures the number he has<span class='line-break'> </span>applied to said lot or lots.  He shall also be <span class='line-break'> </span>directed to issue to the person who has selected <span class='line-break'> </span>a lot, a certificate in form according to the <span class='line-break'> </span>copy hereto appended.</p>
<p>The certificates to be used for this purpose should <span class='line-break'> </span>be printed, with suitable blanks to be filled by the <span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent as required, and said blurbs should <span class='line-break'> </span>be bound in a book, with a wide margin opposite<span class='line-break'> </span>the blanks; and it shall be made the duty of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Superintendent to record in said margin the number <span class='line-break'> </span>of the certificate issued, the name of the party to whom <span class='line-break'> </span>it has been issued, and also the number of the lot <span class='line-break'> </span>which said certificate represents.  Said book of cer<span class='line-break'></span>tificates and record shall be designated (and marked)<span class='line-break'> </span>as a "Record of selected lots in Mount Auburn Cemetery".<span class='line-break'> </span>As soon as the Superintendent has received from the<span class='line-break'> </span>Treasurer notice that the deed of a selected lot has <span class='line-break'> </span>been issued, it shall be his duty to write on the <span class='line-break'> </span>record book of selected lots _ against the number <span class='line-break'> </span>of the lot indicated by the deed _ <u>"Deed issued."</u><span class='line-break'> </span>It shall also be the duty of the Superintendent<span class='line-break'> </span>to make a monthly report in writing of any</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279417">
<h3><a name="page-1279417">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 250)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>250</p>
<p>lots selected which have been forfeited by the <span class='line-break'> </span>omission of the person holding a certificate to <span class='line-break'> </span>present it to the Treasurer within the time <span class='line-break'> </span>specified.</p>
<p>Which is respectfully submitted for <span class='line-break'> </span>the Com<sup>ee</sup> _____ <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>C. P. Curtis</a>, Chairman</p>

This laying out and<span class='line-break'> </span>sale of this lot to be subject to the approval <span class='line-break'> </span>of the "Committee on Lots,,.</p>

<div id="page-1279418">
<h3><a name="page-1279418">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 251)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>251</p>
<p>Upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>.</p>
<p>Voted that the foregoing report be adopted.</p>
<p>Also upon motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>,</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Certificate book to be prepared _'>Certificate book to be prepared _</span></p>
<p>Voted that <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the Secretary</a>, under the Direction <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Committee upon Lots, be requested to have <span class='line-break'> </span>prepared for <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'><!--Mann-->the Superintendent</a>, the Certificate <span class='line-break'> </span>Book and Record, referred to in this report <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Committee.</p>
<p>Report _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Comee  on relations and obligations of this Corporation to Mass. Hort. Society _'>Report of Com<sup>ee</sup>  on relations and obligations of this Corporation to <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Mass. Hort. Society</a> _</span></p>
<p>"The Committee appointed to consider the <span class='line-break'> </span>relations and obligations of the Proprietors of Mount <span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn Cemetery to the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Massachusetts Horticultural Soci<span class='line-break'></span>ety</a>, with special reference to the <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a>, have con<span class='line-break'></span>sidered the subject and ask leave to report. _</p>
<p>The question to which they have devoted their <span class='line-break'> </span>attention is, whether in case the <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a> shall <span class='line-break'> </span>be annexed to the Cemetery, and burial lots therein<span class='line-break'> </span>be sold, the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Horticultural Society</a> will be entitled to any<span class='line-break'> </span>part of the proceeds of such sales. _</p>
<p>It will be perceived that this is a question of <span class='line-break'> </span>importance.  If the Trustees should dedicate that land <span class='line-break'> </span>to the purposes of a Cemetery, it will be an irrevocable <span class='line-break'> </span>act.  Your Committee were unwilling to assume the respon<span class='line-break'></span>sibility of determining this question: they submitted it with <span class='line-break'> </span>the Charter and other documents to three of the most eminent<span class='line-break'> </span>Counsel in <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a> - Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54994' title='Loring, Charles G.'>C. G. Loring</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/25007507' title='Bartlett, Sidney'>S. Bartlett</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>and <a href='/pages/subjects/58532' title='Curtis, Benjamin R.'>B. R. Curtis</a>, separately; the result of their opinions<span class='line-break'> </span>is that the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Horticultural Society</a> will <u>not</u> be entitled<span class='line-break'> </span>to any portion of the proceeds of sale of lots laid out <span class='line-break'> </span>in the land comprising the <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279419">
<h3><a name="page-1279419">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 252)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>252</p>
<p>Your Committee concur in this result,<span class='line-break'> </span>and they therefore recommend the passage of the fol<span class='line-break'></span>lowing Resolutions: _</p>
<p>That the <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone Farm</a> may be annexed<span class='line-break'> </span>to the Cemetery, and be dedicated to the same uses<span class='line-break'> </span>and purposes, whenever it shall be deemed ex<span class='line-break'></span>pedient to annex the same, without incurring<span class='line-break'> </span>any liability to the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Massachusetts Horticultural<span class='line-break'> </span>Society</a>.</p>
<p>Your Committee, with their report, submit<span class='line-break'> </span>the written opinions of the said counsel, and re<span class='line-break'></span>commend that they be placed on file by <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'><!--Coolidge-->the<span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary</a>.</p>

Curtis</a><span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>June 7, 1858 signed</td> <td>{ <a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Charles G. Nazro</a></td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>{ <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Jacob Bigelow</a></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span>The report having been read _</p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/62842' title='Crocker, Uriel'>Mr Crocker</a>, it was accepted<span class='line-break'> </span>And upon further motion by him, the resolutions<span class='line-break'> </span>contained therein were adopted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Sales in Public Lots _ motion Respecting paying 25% ch. thereof to Mass. Hort. Socy _ '>Sales in <a href='/pages/subjects/61319' title='Public Lot'>Public Lots</a> _ motion Respecting paying 25% ch. thereof to <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Mass. Hort. Soc<sup>y</sup></a> _ </span></p>
<p>The following motion was submitted by Mr<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a></p>

<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/67763' title='Tobey, Edward S.'>Mr Tobey</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that this motion be laid upon the table.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div class="page-content">
<p>254</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Treasurer&apos;s Bonds &amp; rects &amp; payment by Supt'>Treasurer's Bonds &amp; rec<sup>ts</sup> &amp; pay<sup>ment</sup> by Sup<sup>t</sup></span></p>
<p>submitted a report in writing, the material portion<span class='line-break'> </span>of which is _</p>
<p>1<sup>st</sup> in relation to the bonds of the Treasurer: _ "That the<span class='line-break'> </span>Treasurer is under bonds, with good and sufficient<span class='line-break'> </span>security, to the amount of Three thousand dollars,<span class='line-break'> </span>which they think is amply sufficient." _</p>
<p>With regard to the receipts and disbursements of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent, they recommended _</p>
<p>"That all sums due to the Corporation of one<span class='line-break'> </span>hundred dollars and upward, shall be paid to the<span class='line-break'> </span>Treasurer, and that all bills of like amounts shall be<span class='line-break'> </span>paid by him _ and that all bills except those for<span class='line-break'> </span>labor, shall be approved either by the Proprietor for<span class='line-break'> </span>whom the work is done, or by the Committee on Lots."</p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Mr Cheever</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the report be laid upon the table<span class='line-break'> </span>till the next meeting.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Mr Curtis declines appointment on Comee to confer with Hort. Socy'><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a> declines appointment on Com<sup>ee</sup> to confer with <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Hort. <p><a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>, on account of his absence from town during<span class='line-break'> </span>the summer months, and his present indisposition, declined<span class='line-break'> </span>to accept a place on the Committee to confer with<span class='line-break'> </span>the <a href='/pages/subjects/54281' title='Massachusetts Horticultural Society'>Massachusetts Horticultural Society</a>.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Supts Departt Mode of receiving &amp; disbursing moneys _ '>Sup<sup>ts</sup> Depart<sup>t</sup> Mode of receiving &amp; disbursing moneys _ </span></p>
<p>The report of the Finance Committee in relation<span class='line-break'> </span>to the mode of receiving and disbursing moneys in the<span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent's department, which was laid upon the<span class='line-break'> </span>table at the last meeting, was called up and<span class='line-break'> </span>discussed; and, upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>the same was accepted, and after the following<span class='line-break'> </span>amendment โ by adding the words "provided that nothing<span class='line-break'> </span>herein contained shall be understood as conflicting with<span class='line-break'> </span>the provisions of any existing by-law" โ the vote re<span class='line-break'></span>commended by the report was adopted โ and<span class='line-break'> </span>is as follows: _</p>

<p>"That all sums due the Corporation of<span class='line-break'> </span>one hundred dollars and upwards shall be paid<span class='line-break'> </span>to the Treasurer; and that all bills of like</p>

<div class="page-content">
<p>257</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='[Supts Departt Mode of receiving &amp; disbursing moneys _] and by Treasr Bills for labor to be approved by Propr or Comee on Lots - '>[Sup<sup>ts</sup> Depart<sup>t</sup> Mode of receiving &amp; disbursing moneys _] and by Treas<sup>r</sup> Bills for labor to be approved by Prop<sup>r</sup> or Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots - </span></p>
<p>amount shall be paid by him; <s> and that<span class='line-break'> </span>all bills of like amount shall be paid by him; </s><span class='line-break'> </span>and that all bills except those for labor shall<span class='line-break'> </span>be approved either by the proprietor for whom the<span class='line-break'> </span>work is done, or by the Committee on Lots; provi<span class='line-break'></span>ded that nothing herein contained shall be under<span class='line-break'></span>stood as conflicting with the provisions of any existing<span class='line-break'> </span>by-law."</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='No paid Servant of Corporation to be interested in any work or material in and for Cemetery โ '>No paid Servant of Corporation to be interested in any work or material in and for Cemetery โ </span></p>
<p>It was further voted, upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Mr Curtis</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span>and in accordance with the recommendation of the<span class='line-break'> </span>said report,</p>
<p>"That neither the Superintendent, Gate Keeper,<span class='line-break'> </span>nor any other paid servant of the Corporation, <span class='line-break'> </span>shall have any interest whatever in any work at<span class='line-break'> </span>or materials furnished for the Cemetery."</p>
<p>The Committee on Grounds to which was referred,<span class='line-break'> </span>at the last meeting, the subject of puchasing a piece of<span class='line-break'> </span>land westerly of and adjoining the <a href='/pages/subjects/53229' title='Stone Farm'>Stone farm</a>, re<span class='line-break'></span>ported through <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr Bigelow</a>, chairman,</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee on Grounds report against purchase of land of D. Stone-'>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds report against purchase of land of <a href='/pages/subjects/58540' title='Stone, David'>D. Stone</a>-</span></p>
<p>That the Committee had examined the premises, and<span class='line-break'> </span>found that the purchase of a piece of land from <a href='/pages/subjects/58540' title='Stone, David'>Mr Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span>would not tend to straighten the westerly line, as<span class='line-break'> </span>a piece of meadow or pond makes a sharp angle with<span class='line-break'> </span>the Stone land, and would therefore separate this from<span class='line-break'> </span>direct connection with the present cemetery.<span class='line-break'> </span>They therefore reported that it was inexpedient<span class='line-break'> </span>to purchase the same. ~</p>
<p>The report was adopted. _</p>

<p>Voted that it be referred to Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/54773' title='Curtis, Charles P.'>Curtis</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/54771' title='Bangs, Isaiah'>Bangs</a>.</p>

<div id="page-1279426">
<h3><a name="page-1279426">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 259)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>259</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Land on Hill-sides _'>Land on Hill-sides _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Mr Cheever</a> stated that it was desirable to induce<span class='line-break'> </span>the purchase by individuals of lots on the side-hills for<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/66005' title='Catacomb Tombs'>catacomb tombs</a>, there being a good deal of land in the<span class='line-break'> </span>cemetery suitable for that purpose only, and suggested<span class='line-break'> </span>that the charge of fifty dollars extra upon a lot of three<span class='line-break'> </span>hundred square feet for the privilege of constructing a tomb<span class='line-break'> </span>therein operated as a bar to the ready sale of such lots.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Motion to charge same as for other Lots โ '>Motion to charge same as for other Lots โ </span></p>
<p>He, therefore _ for the sake of bringing the matter before<span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees at the next meeting _</p>
<p>Moved that lots for <a href='/pages/subjects/66005' title='Catacomb Tombs'>catacomb tombs</a> on the hill<span class='line-break'></span>sides, in such places as the Committee on Lots shall<span class='line-break'> </span>approve, shall be sold at the same price as other lots<span class='line-break'> </span>in the Cemetery are now sold - viz. fifty cents per square<span class='line-break'> </span>foot: ~ and that that motion be upon the table till the next meeting.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Laid on table till next meeting. '>Laid on table till next meeting. </span></p>
<p>The meeting was then adjourned.<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>,, Secretary.</p>
<p>------------------------------</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees October, 4. 1858.'>Trustees <date when='1858-10-04'>October, 4. 1858</date>.</span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>was held on <date when='1858-10-04T10:00:00'>Monday, October 4, 1858, at 10 o'clock<span class='line-break'> </span>a.m.</date> at the usual place.</p>
<p>Present _ <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a>, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Gould</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54820' title='Nazro, Charles G.'>Nazro</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'><!--James-->Read</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/65944' title='Sleeper, Jacob'>Sleeper</a>.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Motion relative to price of tomb lots in hill-sides called up _ '>Motion relative to price of tomb lots in hill-sides called up _ </span></p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read.</p>
<p>The motion made at the last meeting, and laid<span class='line-break'> </span>upon the table until this meeting, was stated to be in <span class='line-break'> </span>order _ viz.</p>
<p>That lots for <a href='/pages/subjects/66005' title='Catacomb Tombs'>catacomb tombs</a> on the hill-sides,<span class='line-break'> </span>in such places as the Committee on Lots shall approve,<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be sold at the same price as other lots in the<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery are now sold โ viz โ fifty cents per square</p>

<div id="page-1279427">
<h3><a name="page-1279427">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 260)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>260</p>
<p>foot. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Amendt _ for _ Price of Tomb Lots in Hill-sides'>Amend<sup>t</sup> _ for _ Price of Tomb Lots in Hill-sides</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'>Mr Read</a> moved the following be substituted as<span class='line-break'> </span>an amendment thereto.</p>
<p>"That lots for tombs on the hill-sides, in such<span class='line-break'> </span>places as the Committee on Lots shall approve, may<span class='line-break'> </span>be sold at fifty cents per square foot, on the pur<span class='line-break'></span>chasers binding themselves to erect no tomb or repos<span class='line-break'></span>itory which shall not be made air tight, to the satis<span class='line-break'></span>faction of the Committee on Lots."</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Adopted _ '>Adopted _ </span></p>
<p>And the same was adopted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Land on South  &amp; West sides of Consecration Dell not to be sold _ '>Land on South  &amp; West sides of <a href='/pages/subjects/61308' title='Consecration Dell'>Consecration Dell</a> not to be sold _ </span></p>
<p>The following was then moved by <a href='/pages/subjects/54772' title='Gould, Benjamin A. (1787-1859)'>Mr Gould</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span>was adopted. _</p>
<p>That the sloping grounds on the southern and<span class='line-break'> </span>western sides of <a href='/pages/subjects/61308' title='Consecration Dell'>Consecration Dell</a> be withheld from<span class='line-break'> </span>sale, till further ordered by the Trustees.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Communicaton of Supt as to price for purpetl care of small lots - referred to Comee on Lots _'>Communicaton of Sup<sup>t</sup> as to price for purpet<sup>l</sup> care of small lots - referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots _</span></p>
<p>A communication was received from <a href='/pages/subjects/59191' title='Mann, Jonathan'><!--Mann-->the Superintendent</a><span class='line-break'> </span>inquiring whether there ought not to be a provision for<span class='line-break'> </span>the perpetual care of small lots for a less sum than<span class='line-break'> </span>three hundred dollars, as now required by the by-laws.</p>
<p>Also whether the present price for depositing bodies<span class='line-break'> </span>in the <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tomb</a> is sufficient to meet cases where<span class='line-break'> </span>the deposit money is forfeited and the bodies have to be<span class='line-break'> </span>removed to some part of the grounds at the expense of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Corporation. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='As to price of Receiving Tomb deposit _ referred to Comee on. Rules &amp; Regulations of intermt _'>As to price of <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tomb</a> deposit _ referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> on. Rules &amp; Regulations of interm<sup>t</sup> _</span></p>
<p>Voted to refer the inquiry as to the sum for perpetual<span class='line-break'> </span>care of small lots to the Committee on Lots; and that relation<span class='line-break'> </span>to the price for deposit in the <a href='/pages/subjects/57656' title='Receiving Tomb'>Receiving Tomb</a> to the Committee on Rules and<span class='line-break'> </span>Regulations of Interments. _ Adjourned _ Attest <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>A.J. Coolidge</a>,, Secretary</p>

<h3><a name="page-1279428">Trustees Records, Vol. 2, 1854 (page 261)</a></h3>
